O vos, tres chiers filz, je vos ai acomplit cest livre qui est li derriens de la science de medicine ensamble l’emplissement de lui, et ai fait la fin per ses expositions et par ses declarations.	O you, very dear sons, I have completed this book for you which is the last in the science of medicine together with its fulfillment, and I have made an end through its explanations and by its declarations.
Et m’est venu en vision que je le vos acomplisse avec cest traitier, qui est partie de l’uevre de mains, c’est a savoir «cyrurgie».	And it came to me in a vision that I complete it for you with this treatise which is part of the work of hands, that is to say, "surgery".
Et por ceu que l’uevre de mains est fortraite en nostre region et est etraingie dou tout en tout, si est perie li science et decopee, et n’est riens demorez de li fuers que les petites descriptions en livres des anciens que les mains ont muees.	And because the work of hands is neglected in our region and has been lost to all, so its knowledge is depleted and cut off, and nothing remains from it but small descriptions in ancient books that have come down to us.
Et de ceu est venue li error et li vanitez, et sont closes les ententions et est aloignie li science.	And from this has come error and vanity, and intentions have been clouded over and knowledge pushed away.
Or me semble que je la vuel vivifier ensamble l’ordination de cest traitier selonc la voie d’exposition et de declaration et de l’abreviation;	Now it seems to me that I will revive it together with the arrangement of this treatise according to the way of exposition, explanation and abbreviation.
et venrai ensamble les formes des ferremens de cautere, et des autres estrumens de l’uevre avec l’ajostement de la declaration et de preparation de li, sicom il est mestier.	and will come with the forms of the cautery irons and other instruments for the work along with their adjustment, explanation and preparation as is necessary.
Et por la raison de ceu que nuls boins maistres de mains n’est trovez en nostre tens, est li ars de medicine eslongié.	And for the reason that no good master of hands is found in our time, the art of medicine has become distant.
Et covient celui qui s’en entremet sormonter en la science d’anathomie, si com Galiens dit, tant qu’il saiche la juement des menbres, et les formes et les conjunctions et les separations d’aus, et aient connissance des osses et des nerf et des brais et le nombre d’ous, et le demenement et des voines movans et des reposans, et dou leu de lor issue.	And it is necessary for anyone who wishes to undertake this to overcome the science of anatomy, as Galen says, so that they know the judgment of members and their forms and conjunctions and separations; and have knowledge of bones, nerves, brains, and the number of them, also movement and moving veins and resting ones, and where they emerge.
Et por ceu dist Ypocras que li nons avec le non est mout, et avec l’uevre est poc;	And for this Hippocrates said that word with the name is much, and with the deed is little;
et meismement en l’art de main.	especially in the art of medicine.
Nos vos disons en l’introite de cest livre que qui n’est conissans des choses devant dites, si se gart qu’il ne chiece en error et qu’il n’ocie les homes;	We tell you in the introduction of this book that one who is not knowledgeable about the things mentioned beforehand should be careful not to fall into error and cause harm to others.
ensi que j’ai veut maintes fois plusors de ces qui s’entremettent de ceste science et si s’abandonent sen science et sens experiment.	So I have often seen many who attempt this science and so abandon themselves without knowledge and without experience.
Car je vis un fol mire qui copa I apostume de scrophules ou col d’une femme, et copa les arteres dou col;	For I saw a mad surgeon who cut into the abscess of scrofula on a woman's neck, and he cut her carotid arteries.
por coi tant de sanc issit hors que li femme cheit morte entre ses mains.	which is why so much blood came out that the woman fell dead in his hands.
Et vis I autre mire qui traït une piere d’un home d’eaige, et li piere estoit grans;	And I saw another surgeon who treated the bladder stone of an old man, and the stone was large;
si emporta avec li une piece de la vessie, et fut mors li hons dedens III jors.	he took away with him a piece of the bladder, and the man died within three days.
Et je i avoie ja esteit apelez por lou traire, et vis la disposition dou malaide et la grandor de la piere, et soi bien s’on lou tailloit il en morroit.	And I had already been called to treat him, and saw the condition of the patient and the size of the stone, and if they cut it out, he would die.
Et vis I autre mire qui prist en cure I duc de nostre terre qui avoit la jambe brisie, et avec la briseure ot plaie;	And I saw another surgeon who treated a duke of our land who had a broken leg, and with the break he had an open wound;
et li mires plains d’ignorance estraint la brisure sus la plaie as esteles par fort lieure, et ne lassa a la plaie point de xalain, et le lassa ensi I termine;	and the ignorant physician binds the fracture over the wound with tight bandages, leaving no room for drainage, and thus it ends.
et li comanda qu’il ne la desliast mie;	and he instructs them not to untie it.
et demora ensi que li jambe fut toute enflee et li piez et vint a perdition.	and as a result, the leg became completely swollen, the foot was affected too, and it led to ruin.
Je fuis apelez por venir a lui, et me hastai por venir deslier la jambe;	I am called upon to treat him, and I hasten to come and untie the leg.
et quant je l’oi desloie si fut em pais et ne sentit point de dolor.	and when I unbind it, he is at peace and feels no pain.
Mais toute voie li corruptions estoit ja confermee ou membre, et ne la poi saner;	But nonetheless, the corruption had already taken hold in the limb, and I could not heal it.
et ne cessa li corrution d’aler par le membre tant que li membres fut dou tout perdus.	And the corruption did not cease to travel through the member until the limb was completely lost.
Et vis I autre mire qui effondra I apostume enchancreit, et puis enflama per le malice de sa signorie.	And there was another evil physician who would burst an abscess open and then inflame it with the malignancy of his power.
Car chancre, quant il est purs d’umor melancolique, ne covient mie qu’on i(l) touche de fer s’il n’est en teil leu c’on puisse toute oster ce que est corrumpus.	For a cancer, when it is caused by melancholic humour, one should not touch it with iron unless it is in such a place that one can remove all the corrupted tissue.
Et por ceu, treschier filz, vos est besoig que vos sachiez que oevre de mains est devisee en II divisions:	And for this, my dear son, you must know that manual work is divided into two categories:
c’est asavoir, huevre ou il a peril en plusors dispositions;	That is to say, works where there is danger in many situations;
et je mostrerai en chescun leu de cest livre ou il a paour et peril.	and I will show you in each place of this book where there is fear and danger.
Por coi il est besoig que vos vos en gardez, si que li fol mire ne puissent mal parler de vos.	This is why you must be cautious so that the foolish physician cannot speak ill of you.
Si prenez vos armes en cusenson, et entreprenez vos malaides legierement et fermement, et usez de la millor voie si que per la graice de Deu vos venez a salut et soiez loez;	Take up your tools with prudence, approach your patients gently yet firmly, and employ the best method so that by God's grace you may succeed in healing them and be praised.
et lassiez les maladies espoantables de grief saniteit;	And leave behind terrifying illnesses of severe unhealthiness;
et ostez vos armes de ceu que vos fait douter, et aiez foit en vos si que vos puissiez venir de cestui monde a l’autre de gloire.	And remove your weapons from whatever makes you doubt, and have faith in yourself so that you may travel from this world to the other with glory.
Galiens dist en aucuns de ses amonestemens:	Galen says in some of his admonishments:
«Ne prenez mie en cure male maladie, que vos ne soiez apelez fol mire.	Do not treat any illness badly, or you will be called a foolish physician.
» J’ai deviseit cest traitier selonc III chapitres.	I have devised this treatise in three chapters.
Li premiers chapitres est des cauteres de feu et dé cauteres de medicine ague, et est li chapitres ordenez de lou chief jusques as piez;	The first chapters are about fire cauterization and medical incisions, and the chapters are organized from head to toe.
et des formes des estrumens, et des ferremens de cautere, et de tout ceu qui est necessaire en l’ueuvre.	And about the shapes of instruments, the preparation for cauterization, and everything that is necessary for the procedure.
Li secons chapitres si est de taillier et de percier, et des ventouses et des plaies, et des estractions des saiettes, et des semblans choses;	The second chapter is about cutting and piercing, and cupping, wounds, arrow extractions, and similar things.
et est li chapitres ordenez et les formes des estrumens.	And it describes the order of chapters and the shapes of instruments.
Li tiers chapitres est de restorer les dislocations et des torcions, et des semblans choses;	The third chapter is about restoring dislocations and torsions, and similar things.
et est ordeneiz des lou chief jusc’as piez, et des formes des estrumens.	And it is ordered from head to foot, and the shapes of instruments.
Ainsois que nos nos remembriens de l’uevre, il covient que je die la qualiteit de l’aide et dou nuisement de chescune complexion.	Before we recall the work, it is necessary for me to speak of the quality of aid and harm of each humour.
Je dis que li qualiteis de l’aide, et dou nuisement, est li plus longe parole et subtilz science et li secrez reponus;	I say that the qualities of treatment, and their harm, is a long discourse and subtle science, and hidden secrets.
et de ceu parlerent li plusors des saiges, et s’acorderent a ceu;	And many wise men have spoken of this, and they agree on it.
et me soffisent poc lor paroles, car je redous la longesce.	And their words suffice for me, for I fear lengthening it.
Je dis que cautere aide universement a toute complexion ou il a matiere, fuer que II complexions:	I say that cautery aids universally all constitutions where there is cause, except two constitutions:
c’est a savoir complexion chaude sens matere, et complexion seche sens matere.	That is to say hot constitution without matter, and dry constitution without matter.
En complexion chaude et seche ensamble matiere, deviserent aucun et dirent que cautere i est grans aide;	In the combination of hot and dry constitution with matter, some debated and said that cautery is a great help;
et li autre dirent le contraire:	And others said the opposite:
que cautere ne vaut a maladie que vient de chalor et de sechour.	That cautery is of no use in illnesses arising from heat and dryness.
Car li nature dou feu si est chaude, et ne doit mie estre cureiz de chaude maladie par chalor, ne per sechour;	For the nature of fire is hot, and it should not be used to treat hot diseases caused by heat or dryness;
et dist cil qui dist lou contraire que cautere fait grant aide a maladie chaude et seche que vient en cors des homes.	And he who says the opposite claims that cauterization provides great relief to hot and dry illnesses that afflict men's bodies.
Car quant tu comperes le cors de l’ome et sa moistor a la complexion dou feu, tu trueves le cors froit.	When you compare the body of man with its moisture to the complexion of fire, you find the former cold.
Et je m’acorde a ceste parole.	And I agree with this statement.
Car je l’ai troveit aucune fois per experiment.	For I have found it by experience once.
Et toute voie, ne s’en entremette mie fuers que cil qui l’a esproveit, et qui conoit par lonc usaige le chapistre des cauteres, et la diversiteit des complexions des homes, et les dispositions et les causes de lor maladies, et les sorvenues et l’espaice dou tens;	And in any case, let no one interfere unless it is he who has experienced it and knows the chapter on cauterization well through long practice, understanding the diversity of human temperaments, their dispositions, the causes of their illnesses, their symptoms, and the passing of time.
des autres complexions n’avons nos mie paour, meismement em maladies froides et moistes.	Of other temperaments we have no fear, especially in cold and moist illnesses.
Et tuit li mire s’asemblerent et s’acorderent au cautere.	And all the doctors agreed and consented to the cautery.
Et sachiez, filz, que cautere ensamble feu si est des secrez des cures, et de plus grant bonteit que cautere de medicine ardant.	And know, my child, that fire cautery is one of the secrets of healing and is of greater benefit than burning medical cautery.
Car li feus est simples, et ne vient mie fuers que au membre qui est cuis, et ne nuit a autre membre se poc nom.	For fire is simple, and it does not arise except on the member that is cooked, and it harms no other member unless touched.
Les medicines ardans vienent de membre a autre en aloignant, et font venir au membre maladies de grief sanation;	Burning medicinal agents spread from one member to another by contact, causing illnesses that heal quickly.
et par aventure ocit lou malaide.	And occasionally the patient dies.
Li feus por sa hautece et por la bonteit de sa substance ne fait mie ceu, s’il n’i a superfluiteit.	The fires for their height and for the goodness of their substance do not make coals, unless there is superfluity.
Et ceu vos ai je troveit par experiment et par la longesce dou servise et de l’estude que j’ai mis en l’art, et esteit sus la verteit des choses;	And I have found this through experimentation and the length of service and study that I have put into the art, and it is based on the truth of things;
et por ceu je m’escuse de la longesce de la parole, car il ne me plait mie que je vos oste le secreit qui est reponus ou feu, et la qualiteit de l’uevre, coment il deboute les maladies des cors, si com li philosophe le dit en demostrant;	and for this I excuse myself for the length of speech, because it does not please me to take away from you the secret that is hidden in fire, and the quality of work, how it cures illnesses of the body, as the philosopher says when demonstrating;
or le recevez en vos pensees.	receive this in your thoughts.
Et sachiez, fil, que il s’acorderent en quel tens doient estre faites les cauteres, et eslirent prientens.	And know, son, that they agreed on when the cauterizations should be performed, and chose carefully.
Et je dis que cautere est covenable en tous tens, por ceu que li nuisemens sorvenans est desoz mis par l’aide dou cautere;	And I say that cautery is suitable at all times, for the harm which arises can be removed by the aid of cautery;
et meismement se li cauteres est por dolors necessaires fors et hastans que ne puent atendre le tens que plus grans malice ne veigne au membre.	and especially if the cautery is necessary for pain that requires immediate treatment, lest a greater evil come to the limb.
Et n’i pensez onques, chier fil, si com font li fol mire;	And never think of it, dear son, as some foolish doctors do;
car a la maladie qui est sanee par cautere n’a point de revenue;	for the disease that is cured by cautery has no relapse;
et il le dient ensi;	and they say it like this;
mais il n’est mie si com il cuident, por ce que cauteres nen est que medicine qui mue la complexion, et seche les humors que sont cause de la dolor, et vaut mues que medicine por le hastement de sa valor, et por la vertut de son oevre et de sa signorie.	but it is not as they believe, for cautery is only a medicine that alters the complexion, and dries out the humors which are the cause of pain, and is better than medicines due to its quick action, and because of the virtue of its work and control.
Et possans chose est que li maladie viegne aucune fois selonc la complexion dou malaide et lou leu de la maladie et sa vertut;	And it is possible that the disease comes sometimes according to the complexion of the patient, and the location of the illness and its strength;
et sont assemblees en lui les superfluitez par l’aquisition des viandes et des semblans choses, se ce n’est cauteres administrez em leu ou il ait poc de superfluitez et de moistor, si com cauteres de dens por la dolor, et les semblans choses, et teil dolor ne revient mie;	and are gathered in him the excesses due to acquisition of meat and similar things, unless cauterizations are administered where there is little excess and moisture, such as dental cauterizations for pain, and similar things, and this kind of pain does not return.
mais ce avient poc.	but it happens rarely.
Et mout de gens n’entendent mie por coi cauteres est apelez li derriens de medecine, et c’est voir;	And many do not understand why cauterizations are called the last resort of medicine, and it is true;
mais il ne croient mie que cauteres vaille aprés medicine, mais lor ententions est fause, et est cauteres li derriens de medicine por ceu que quant nos aministrons manieres de cures en aucune maladie et elles ne valent, adonc administrons nos le cautere, et il vaut.	but they do not believe that cauterizations are better than medicines, but their understanding is false, and cauterization is the last resort of medicine because when we administer various treatments for a disease and they fail, then we apply the cautery, and it works.
Adonques apert bien que cauteres est li derriens de medicine, ne mie selonc l’entention des folz mires.	Then it is evident that cauterization is the last resort of medicine, not according to the intention of foolish doctors.
Li ancien dirent que cauteres d’estrument d’or est muedres que de fer, et ne dirent ceu fuers que por la qualiteit de l’or et por la hautece de sa substance;	The ancient ones said that cauterizations with golden instruments are more beneficial than those with iron, and they attributed this to the quality of gold and the nobility of its substance.
et dirent que li leus de cautere ne fait mie porriture, mais ceu n’est mie voir car je l’ai esprovei, et ai troveit que c’est voir en aucuns homes;	And they said that the place of cauterization does not cause corruption, but this is not always true as I have tested it, and found that it is indeed so in some people.
et cauteres d’or vaut mues que de fer, si com il lou dirent.	And gold cauterizations are more valuable than those of iron, just as they said.
Et toutevoie quant tu chaufes estrument d’or, tu ne seis mie quant il est chaus par la color de l’or, et s’est tantost refroidiez;	However, when you heat a golden instrument, you do not know when it is hot by the colour of the gold, and it cools down quickly.
et s’on le chaufe trop;	and if you overheat it.
si font au feu;	They do it with fire.
et ensi i a assez d’empechement.	and thus there is enough hindrance.
Et por ce usons nos de cautere de feir que nos l’avons mues apparilliet a nostre oevre.	And for this, we use fire cautery, which we have adapted to our work.
Or vos ai ordeneit cest chapitre des lou chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que li voie soit plus legiere a trover.	Here you have been ordered this chapter of the head to feet, so that the way is easier to find.
dou cautere olivaire	Olive oil cautery.
Cist cauteres vaut a moistor et a froidor sus lou cerveil, et en i a dous c’on fait par la cause d’une maladie qui est apelee «soda», et par la cause de maintes humors qui dessendent dou chief as eulz, et as oreilles, et por multitude de songes et dolor de dens et dolor de gorge, et meismement a toutes maladies qui vienent de froidor si com paralisie et sode et apoplexie et semblans maladies.	This cautery is beneficial for moisture and cold in the brain, and there are two that are made due to a disease called 'soda', and because of many humours that descend from the head to the eyes, ears, and due to numerous dreams, toothache, sore throat, and especially all diseases that come from cold such as paralysis, soda, apoplexy, and similar illnesses.
Li forme de cest cautere si est que li malaides soit espurgiez par medicine solutive mondifiant le chief III nuis ou IIII, selonc ceu que li vertus et li eaige et li acostumance dou malaide le puet soffrir;	The form of this cautery is such that the patient should be purged with a solvent medicine altering the brain for three or four nights, according to what their condition and constitution can bear;
et puis fai rere lou chief dou malaide.	and then let the patient rest his head.
Et puis le fai seoir croisiet entre tes mains, et mettre ses mains sor som peis;	And then have him sit cross-legged between your hands, placing his hands on top of yours.
aprés met la racine de ta palme sus la racine de son neis entre ses II eulz;	After that, place the root of your palm onto the root of his nose between his two eyes.
et lai ou venra tes dois moiens, si saigne d’enche puis eschaufe le cautere qui est apelé «olivare», de coi ci est li forme:	And let your two fingers be the ones that bleed; then heat up the cautery called 'olivare', and this is its form:
Et le met sor le leu signiet d’encre, et fai en dessendant et en estraignant ta main poc et poc en trestornant;	And place it on the inked spot, then gently pull and squeeze your hand back and forth while twisting.
puis lieve ta main isnelement, et rewarde le leu se tu vois l’os I sol petit;	Then lift your hand slightly, and feel the area if you see any bone at all, even a small one;
et se tu ne lou vois, si rencomence le cautere tant que tu voies l’os si com je lou t’ai dit;	And if you don't see it, repeat the cauterization until you do see the bone as I've instructed;
aprés pren I poc de seil, et met en awe et molle coton dedens, et met sor le leu, et li laisse III jors;	After, take a little bit of silk, put soft cotton inside it, and place it on the spot, leaving it there for three days.
aprés met sus cotun moilliet en burre;	Then put moistened cotton mixed with butter on top of it.
et laisse sus tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	Leave it there until the scalding sensation has passed.
aprés cure la plaie de l’oignement qui est apelez «tetrafarmaçon», tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treating the wound, heal it with 'tetrafarmacon' until it is fully healed.
Et se dirent li ancien, que quant plus demoure overte li plaie, plus s’espurge;	And the ancients said that the longer the wound remains open, the more it purges itself.
et por ce si aide mues.	and for this reason, healing is aided.
Et dirent aucun de ces que on doit tant lassier le cautere que partie de l’os soit arse, et puis rese on ceu qui est ars de l’os, et soit curez.	And some said that one should let the cautery burn until a part of the bone is charred, then remove what has been burned from the bone and it shall be healed.
Et dient li autre c’on doit le cautere tant lassier sus, et bouter si fort c’on abaite de l’os ausi large comme I vertoil que les femmes mettent en lor fusez por ceu que les humors issent mues hors;	And others say that the cauterization should be left on top, and pressed so hard that it dents the bone as wide as a needle that women use in their sewing, for this reason, the humours flow out more easily.
et doit on lassier la plaie longement overte;	And one should leave the wound open for a longer period of time.
aprés le doit on curer et sodeir.	Afterwards, one must treat it and seal it closed.
Et ces II manieres de cauteres ne me semblent mie estre bones dou tout en tout, fuers qu’en aucuns homes ou il ait voie de paor;	And these two types of cauterization do not seem to me to be good at all, except in certain people where there is a way of fear.
et mues me semble que je lou doie laissier;	and I think I should leave it alone.
car li chiés li est afoiblis par les solutions continuees de nature, si com nos le tesmoignons ens autres membres;	because the head is weakened by continuous solutions of nature, as we witness in other body parts.
et meisme quant li chiés dou malaide est foibles par nature, et li premiere semblance de cautere est plus salve et muedre por moi, et de celi use je oevre en donques emsamble salut.	And even when the head of the sick person is naturally weak, and the first method of cauterization seems more effective to me, I use it with great success.
de l’anciainne dolor dou chief	Of the ancient pain of the head
Quant en tout le chief vient dolor croniques, et dure longement, si doit user li malaides yeris et pilules qui sont apelees «cochie», et d’espurgement de chief et d’oiles et d’emplastres;	When the entire head is affected by chronic pain that persists for a long time, the patient must use herbs and pills called 'cockroach', as well as purgatives, oils, and plasters.
et s’on li fait le cautere que nos avons devant dit, et il ne vaut.	And if you perform the cautery as we described before, it is ineffective.
Pren warde se li chiés dou malade est de fort nature, et qu’il ne soit trop froit;	Take note if the patient's shoulder is of strong constitution and not too cold;
adonques le cauterize desoz celui cautere un poc que nos avons dit desus.	Then cauterize underneath that cautery, slightly different from what we said before.
Aprés fai cautere sus chescune corne dou chief jusc’a l’os, si com devant avons dit, et fai I cautere ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz»;	Afterwards, perform a cautery on each corner of the head down to the bone, as we described earlier, and then cauterize the place called "vasselz".
et est I leus en coi on met ventouses;	And it is red where cups are applied;
et alige ta main si que tu ne voises mie jusc’a l’os:	Lighten your hand so that you do not break down to the bone:
li malaides sent trop plus grant dolor en cest cautere que as autres, et je em parlerai aillors;	The sick person feels even greater pain during this cauterization than with others, and I will speak of it later.
et covient que li cauteres des cornes soient plus subtis que cil dont on cautere la moieneteit dou chief, et c’est li forme:	and it is fitting that the cauterizations of the horns be more subtle than those for the middle part of the head, and this is the method:
dou cautere dou chief	For the head cautery.
Quant en une partie dou chief vient dolor sodaine, et est estendue li maladie jusc’a l’oil, et li chiés est espurgiez par medicines mondifians, et on a fait les autres cures que j’ai dit en la division des maladies, et tout ceu ne profite mie:	When pain suddenly arises in one part of the head and extends to the eye, with the skull being purged by cleansing medications, and other treatments I mentioned for various diseases have been performed but are ineffective:
adonques li fai cauteres selonc II manieres, c’est a savoir de medicine ague et de feir.	then you must cauterize it in two ways, namely with cold medicine and by using fire.
Li cauteres de medicine ague si est que tu preignes une doce d’alz, et oste l’escorce et le recope I poc as II chiés, et puis fent la temple ou li dolor tient en teil maniere que tu puisses reponre la doce d’alz desoz le cuir;	The cold medicine cauterization is done by taking a piece of aloes wood, removing the bark and cutting it into two pieces for the temples where the pain lies in such a way that you can place the aloes wood under the skin.
et quant elle sera reponuee si le lie et l’estraint bien et le laisse ensi XII houres;	and when it is answered, bind it well and hold it like this for twelve hours.
et puis le deslie et trait fuers la doce d’ail, et laisse la plaie ensi II jors ou III;	then untie it and treat vigorously with garlic juice, leaving the wound like this for two or three days;
puis met sus cotun plongiet en burre tant que porreture en isse.	then apply cotton soaked in butter until healing takes place.
Aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	After the treatment, let it heal completely.
et se tu vues si fai ceu d’aucunes medicines comburans que j’ai escrites ou dozime traitier des medicines comburans.	And if you want to use any of the caustic medications, refer back to my previous treatise on caustic medicines.
Li cautere de fer si est selonc ceste meniere.	The iron cautery is done in this manner.
Chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Heat the cautery, which has this shape:
Et est apelez «clos» por ceu que li chief est fait a la forme d’un clo ou il ait I poc de corbeure, et em mileu a une petite apparance;	It is called a "close" wound because the head has the shape of a clover or a three-leafed plant with one pocket of curvature and in the middle there is a small appearance.
et le met sor le leu dolorous, et tien ta main et trestorne le feir un poc legierement, tant que li moitiez de l’espés dou keur soit arse;	and place it on the painful spot, hold your hand and slightly turn it over, so that half of the heart's sword is burned.
et lieve ta main que li artere n’arde, que est defuers, et decorre habundance de sanc.	lift your hand so that the artery does not burn, which is outside, and a large amount of blood flows out.
Aprés met coton en awe de seil, et met sor le leu par III jors;	Afterwards, place cotton in front of the wound, and leave it on for three days.
puis i met coton moilliet em burre, et puis cure le leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	then put moist cotton in butter, and then clean the wound until it is healed.
et se tu vuelz cauterize ceste emigraine avec le cautere qui est apelez «cultellare», a tout la pointe, et te garde de coper l’artere en ceste emigraine qui n’est mie anciaine.	and if you wish to cauterize this migraine with the cautery called "knife-like", on all sides of the tip, be careful not to cut the artery in this fresh migraine.
de emigraine	of a migraine
Quant tu cures emigraine si com nos avons devant dit en divisions des maladies, et ne profite mie, et vois que li cauteres devant dis de la medicine et dou fer ne li soffit mie, adonques covient il que tu eschaufes le cautere qui est apelez «cultellare» tant qu’il soit blans;	When you treat a migraine as we have previously stated in the division of illnesses, and it does not improve, and you see that the previous cauterizations with medicine and iron do not suffice for him, then it is necessary that you heat up the cautery called "cultellare" until it turns white;
et seigne ainsois sor le leu doillant une ligne de demi doi de lonc, et oste ta main une fois, et l’estrain que tu ne coper l’artere et que ne viegnes jusc’a l’os;	and incise there instead, over the painful spot, a line half an inch long, and remove your hand once, but be careful not to cut the artery or reach the bone;
et te warde de la mandibule que muet quant on menjut, et li ners n’ait regart que la muet et que spasmus ne veigne a malaide, et te warde de decorrement de sanc de l’artere quant elle sera copee, ou copement ait grant paour et meismement a celui que ne s’i conoit, et qui n’est estudians et esprovez;	and take care of the jaw movement when chewing, making sure it does not become stuck and that no spasm comes to the patient, and beware of the arterial blood loss when cutting into the artery, for this cut has great danger and especially so in those who are inexperienced and untested;
et laisse l’uevre em mi voie;	and leave the work halfway through;
mais je vos dirai coment on restainche sanc quant li artere est copee, et je vos mostrerai a leu ou il afiert en cest livre.	but I will tell you how to staunch blood when the artery is severed, and I will show you where it appears in this book.
Et se tu vois que cist cauteres ne soffise mie a la maladie, et li malaides est soffrans, cauterize le enmi le chief ausi com nos avons dit, et cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And if you see that these cauterizations are not sufficient for the illness, and the patient is still suffering, cauterize it in the middle of the head as we have said, and treat the wound until it is healed.
et se tu vues, aministre le cautere que nos avons dit ou chapistre de l’estraction de l’artere, avec le cautere qui ait II coutelz;	and if you see this, apply the cautery that we mentioned in the chapter on arterial extraction, using the double-bladed cautery.
et est cist cauteres millors de celui et plus aidans.	and this cauterization is better and more helpful than that one.
de la dolor des oreilles de part froidor	From ear pain due to coldness
Quant en l’oreille vient dolor de froit, et on i a ovreit de medicines solutives et des autres cures que nos avons dit en la division, et li dolors ne se muet, adonques eschaufe cest cautere qui est apelez «poins», de coi ci est li forme:	When there is ear pain due to coldness, and one has applied solutive medicines and other treatments as we have mentioned before in the division of this book, but the pain does not subside, then heat up this cautery tool called a "point". This is how it looks like:
Aprés pointoie tout entor l’oreille malaide, ou entor les II se la dolor tient en ambedous, et t’esloigne un poc ensus de la racine de l’oreille puis que tu as signiet le leu d’enche;	After piercing around the diseased ear, or around both if the pain is in both, and remove a little above the root of the ear once you have marked the site for incision.
et ait X poins entor chescune oreille;	and make X incisions around each ear;
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	after treat the site until it is healed.
de la torture de la bouche	Upon the torture of the mouth:
Torture qui doit estre curee par cautere nen est fuers que de celles que muevent de fleume, si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladie;	Wounds that should be treated with cauterization are only those that discharge fluid, as we have said in the classification of diseases;
et ne faire point de cautere as semblances que vienent de sechor et de spame de ners.	and do not apply cauterization to similar conditions that come from drying out and of nerve spasms.
Quant tu cures ceste semblance de torture qui muet de fleume d’ydres et d’espurgemens de chief et de gargarisme, et ceu ne vaut, adonc covient que tu cauterizes le malaide de III cauteres:	When you treat this type of wound that discharges fluid from ulcers and purgings of the head and gargling, and it is not successful, then you must cauterize the patient with three cauterizations:
l’une en la racine de l’oreille, et l’autre un poc defuers la temple, et le tier en l’ajostement des II levres;	One at the root of the ear, another slightly outside the temple, and the third where the two lips meet.
et met le cautere en la partie qui apert saine, et li fai cautere endroit le chief de l’oreille desus un poc desoz la corne dou chief, et un autre en la temple ausi longe com uns poce;	Place the cautery on the part that appears healthy, and make a cauterization spot above the ear, slightly below the crown of the head, and another in the temple as long as a thumb.
et laisse le cautere tant sus que li moitiez dou keur soit arse;	Leave the cautery until half of the heart is burned.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And this is the shape of the cauterization mark:
Et est li semblance dou cutellaire que nos avons mise devant, mais il est un poc plus subtilz et covient que li coutelz soit un poc plus gros;	It is similar to the shape of the knife we mentioned earlier, but it is slightly more delicate and requires a slightly thicker blade.
aprés cure lou leu si com j’ai devant dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment, leave it to heal as I said before, until it is healed.
Quant apoplexie est ancieinne et tu la cures ensi com nos avons dit, et il ne profite mie, et li malaides n’ait fievre, adonques li fai IIII cauteres:	When apoplexy is old and you treat it as we have said before, but there is no improvement, and the patient has no fever, then make four cauterizations.
II sus les II cornes dou chief, et I emmi le chief, et I ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz» si com nos avons devant dit, et lou derrien cautere sus la bouche de l’estomac;	Two above the two horns of the head, and one in the middle of the head, and one at the spot called "vessel" as we said before, and the last cauterization on the mouth of the stomach.
et soit curez si com nos avons dit devant.	And treat it as we have said before.
de litargie	Of lethargy.
A cest maladie covient doner au malaide yeres grans et pilules mondifians le cerveil;	For this illness, give the patient large herbs and pills that calm the brain.
aprés reis lou chief dou malaide tout, et li met sus l’occipite l’emplaustre de sinapi qui est escrit ou traitier des emplastres;	After treating his head entirely, place the patient's occiput on a mustard poultice as described in the treatise on plasters.
et c’est li maniere dou cautere:	And this is how to apply a cautery:
si lou fai si com j’ai dit.	If you do it as I have said.
S’il est sanez ensi, boin est;	If the incision is done this way, it is good.
et s’il ne l’est, se li fai III cauteres des emmi le chief en dessendant jusc’a col, et ait d’espaice entre chescun cautere I doi de gros;	And if it is not, perform three cauterizations on the head descending to the neck with a two-finger space between each cautery.
et le cure si com les autres, et se tu i vues ajoster, et li malaides est soffrans, se li fai I cautere en mileu;	Treat it as the others, and if you see that it needs adjustment, and the patient is suffering, perform one cautery in the middle.
et se mestiers est, II autres sus les II cornes, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and if necessary, two more above the two horns, and treat until it is healed.
et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «olivare», si com j’ai devant dit.	and let the cauterization be that which is called 'olivare', as I have said before.
de la froidor dou chief	From the coldness of the head
Il covient que li chief soit mundifiez de yeres et de ceu que nos avons devant dit;	The head must be cleansed of hairs and any other matter, as we have said before;
aprés reis le chief dou malaide, puis li fai cautere emmi le chief et sus chescune corne, et I derrier et III sus l’espinee dou col;	after clean the head of the patient, then cauterize it in the middle of the head and on each horn, and behind it, three times along the spine of the neck;
et se tu en as plus mestier, et li cors est moiste et li malaides est soffrans, et li maladie est fors, se li fai IIII cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos;	and if you need to do more, and the body is moist and the patient is suffering, and the illness is severe, then perform four cauterizations along the spine of the back;
et li laisse tant que li plus dou keur soit ars, et lieve ta main;	And leave it until the deepest part of the heart is burnt, then lift your hand.
aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez, et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «olivare» que nos avons devant dit.	After the wound is treated, let it heal completely, and use the cautery called 'olive oil', as we mentioned earlier.
de l’epilempsie	from epilepsy
Li epilentiques ne doit useir de cautere fuers que cil qui est fleumatique, et covient premier mondifier le cerveil de yeres et d’autres cures que nos avons dites en la division quant li malaides est grans et soffrans de penre medicine.	The epileptic should not undergo fire cauterization unless they are phlegmatic; it is necessary to first modify the brain with herbs and other treatments we have mentioned in the section for adults who are suffering greatly.
Et se c’est uns enfes qui ne lou puisse soffrir, se li fai gargarisme et mastication mondifiant le cerveil sovent avec bones viandes;	And if it is a child who cannot endure it, have them do gargles and chew softened meat to nourish the brain frequently.
aprés li reis lou chief em mileu, et i fai I cautere selonc ce que nos avons dit devant, et I cautere sus lou vassel, et sus chescune corne;	After the king's face is in the middle, make a cautery there as we said before, and another on the vessel, and one on each corner.
et se li malaides est fors et soffrans, se li fai cauteres si com j’ai dit a celui qui ait paralisie et mollification de cors, sus l’espinee dou dos et dou col, et soit li cauteres olivier selonc la maniere que j’ai dit.	And if the patient is strong and suffering, apply cauterization as I said for those with paralysis and softening of the body, on the spine from neck to back, and use olive oil cautery as described earlier.
Se li malaides est enfes, se li fai I cautere subtil selonc ceste maniere:	If the patient is a child, perform this delicate cautery as follows:
Quant par la cause de melancolie sunt les superfluitez ou les moistors corrumpues et fleume grosse, adonques lou cauterize de teils cauteres com nos avons dit a celui qui ait paralisie.	When due to melancholia the superfluities or corrupt humours and thick phlegm prevail, then cauterize with three cauteries as we have said for one who has paralysis.
Et se par la cause de melancolie est li superfluitez declinans a melancolie, et est li cors dou malaide moistes, adonc li done a boivre chose par coi li cervelz soit mundifiez, selonc ceu qu’il est devant en la division.	And if due to melancholia the superfluities decline towards it, and the patient's body is moist, then give them something to drink by which their brain may be cleansed, as was said before in the classification.
Aprés reis lou chief dou malaide;	After rising, let the patient rest their head.
aprés fai I torteil de lin bien fait, ausi com I cercle, si le met emmi le chief;	After that, make a well-crafted flaxen pad, like a circle, and place it in the middle of their head.
et li malaides sié croisiez, et soit bien tenus de toutes pars;	Let the patient lie down with crossed legs, ensuring they are well-supported on all sides.
aprés presente le linement, et vaut mues de burre de berbis ancien;	Next, present the flaxen pad and apply some old goat butter to it.
et lou chaufe a feu tempreement, si que li dois s’on li boute le puisse soffrir;	Heat the pad with gentle fire so that the patient's skin can bear it comfortably.
aprés vuide le cercle par dedens emmi le chief, et lou laisse refroidier;	Empty the circle from within their head and let it cool down.
et fai ce a malaide chescune semaine une fois avec autre governement boin, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Do this for the patient once a week along with other good treatments until they are healed.
Ou se tu vues cauterize lou en faisant poins plusors a tot le cautere.	If you see scabs form during the cautery, make multiple punctures across the entire cautery site.
Ceste maniere de cautere amoistit le cerveil igaument;	This manner of cauterization moistens the brain equally.
et puis met sus coton moilliet en burre et en graisse de geline.	And then place on it cotton moistened with butter and chicken fat.
de l’awe des eulz	from eye ache
Quant awe vient premierement as eulz par les signes que j’ai dit en la division, adonques encomence et done boivre au malaide chose mundifiant le chief, et le warde de toutes moistors, et lou fai suer ou bain plusors fois a jeun.	When eye ache first arises from the signs I mentioned earlier in this section, you should begin by giving the patient things that clean out their head and guard against moisture while they sweat it out in the bath multiple times on an empty stomach.
Aprés li comande a rere son chief, et li fai cautere emmi le chief, et li fai II cauteres sus les II temples se li dessendemens de l’awe est as II eulz ensamble, ou en I se li dessendemens est en I;	After, instruct him to lower his head, and cauterize him between the temples, performing two cauterizations if the descent of the weakness is towards both eyes together, or one if it is in one.
et cope a tout le cautere toutes les voines et les arteres que sont desoz le keur, et soient li cautere lonc selon lou large de la temple;	And cut all the veins and arteries that are below the heart during any cauterization, and let the cauterization be long according to the width of the temple.
et te warde de decorrement de sanc, et se tu vois trop de sanc issir, si li estainche de teil pooir com tu as.	Be mindful of the loss of blood, and if you see too much blood emerging, stop it with such power as you have.
Et je t’enseignerai en l’estraction des arteres et a l’incision la cautele coment tu l’estencheras;	And I will teach you about the extraction of arteries and the incision, how to cauterize it and stop the bleeding.
et aucune fois fait on cautere ou hatereil desoz les II os derrier.	and sometimes you make a cautery or hot iron underneath the two hind bones.
dou cors des larmes	body of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont ancienes et acostumees et sont sus les voines, ou delez les arteres que sont en l’aparance dou chief defors;	When the tears of the eyes are old and accustomed, and they sit on the veins or near the arteries that appear outside the head;
et on voit que c’est des superfluitez froides fleumatiques, adonques li fai le cautere que j’ai dit en l’encomencement de l’awe dessendant as eulz:	and you see that they are cold and phlegmatic excesses, then make the cautery that I mentioned at the beginning, descending to the eyes.
I cautere emmi le chief, et II cauteres sus les II temples, et II cauteres ou haiterel desoz les II os;	A cautery in the middle of the head, two cauteries on the two temples, and two cauteries or hot irons underneath the two hind bones.
et s’il i a besoigne plus, si le cauterize saigement desus le sorcil a tout I petit cautere.	And if more is needed, carefully cauterize above the eyebrow with small cauteries.
dou cors des larmes par dedens les eulz	Through the body of tears from within the eyes
Quant tu le medicines selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et il ne profite mie, adonques done a boivre a malaide III nuis cochies;	When you treat him according to what we have said in the classification, and he does not benefit, then give the patient three nights of cuckoos to drink.
aprés li reis le chief, et li fai cautere ou mileu dou cautere olivaire;	After the king's head, apply cauterization to his forehead in the middle of the olive-shaped area.
et fai II cauteres dou cautere qui est apelez «clavilis» sus les II sorcis, un poc desoz les chevous;	And apply two 'clavilis' cauterizations above the two temples, slightly below the hairline.
et te warde de l’artere que tu ne la coper.	Be mindful of the artery to avoid cutting it.
Et c’est li forme dou cautere qui est apelez «clavilis»:	And this is the shape of the 'clavilis' cautery instrument:
Quant li papiere de l’oil est mollifie de maladie et de moistor, adonques la cautarize de cest cautere qui est apelez «olivare».	When the paper of the eye is softened by illness and moisture, then cauterize it with this cautery instrument called 'olivare'.
de coi ci est li forme:	Of which this is the form:
Et se tu vues si fai II cauteres sus les II sorcis ausi lons com li sorcilz sont;	And if you wish, make two additional cauterizations above the temples as long as the eyebrows are.
et n’i lassiez mie la main fors que tant que li tierce partie de la papiere soit arse, selonc la maniere que j’ai dit.	And do not let go of it [the cautery] until a third part of the paper has burned, according to the manner I have said.
dou poil qui point l’oil	on the hair that pricks the eye
Aucune fois avient que li poil des oilz sont convertit au pardedens, et poignent l’oil, et i fait on cauteres selonc II manieres:	Sometimes it happens that the eyelashes turn inwards and prick the eye, and for this, cauterization is done in two ways:
c’est a savoir de feu, ou de medicine ardant.	That is to say, with fire or burning medicine.
Ou cautere de feu comande au malaide qu’il laisse les poilz tant qu’il soient lons et igals;	For the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and even;
et s’il le poignent a lor nassance, se li estraint les eulz qu’il ne se muevent tant qu’il naissent.	and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Quant il naissent et i sont igalz, adonques met le malaide en ton sain;	When they [the eyelashes] have grown evenly, then put the patient into your care.
aprés seigne sus la papiere des eulz une figure que soit ausi com li fuelle dou mirte, et soit li comencemens dou signe delez les poilz;	After, sir, on the paper of the eyes, draw a shape that is similar to the leaf of myrtle, and let the beginning of the sign be beside the hairs.
puis i met coton moilliet en glaire d’uef et muscillaige de persillion sus l’oil, puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Then put moist cotton with egg white and parsley poultice on the eye, then heat the cautery which has this shape:
Aprés cauterize sus la figure que tu as signiet poc et poc mout de fois, que li keurs soit ars lai endroit;	Afterwards, cauterize on the shape you have drawn many times until the heart of the area is burned.
et li signes de la santeit de l’uevre est que tu voies la papiere retraite, et les poilz levez a la pointure de l’oil;	And the sign of success for this operation is that you see the paper shrivel up and the hairs stand on end at the tip of the eye.
adonques lieve ta main, et laisse ensi III jors, puis i met coton moilliet en burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	Then lift your hand away and leave it like this for three days, then apply moist cotton in butter until the scald is removed.
aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the treatment of dressing until it is healed.
Et se aprés ceu vienent li poilz, et li papiere est mollifie adonques rencomence le cautere sus cel leu meisme, si com tu as fait premiers;	And if after these hairs grow, and the paper is softened then restart the cauterization on that same spot as you did initially.
et se li poil sont defuer, si le cauterize tant que li papiere soit levee a son leu natureil, et soit igals, et ne poignent mie li poil l’oil.	If the hair has fallen out, cauterize it until the paper lifts to its natural position, and is even, and does not prick the eye.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il laisse les poilz tant qu’il soient grans et igalz, puis fai de parchemin la forme de la foille de mirte;	The burning medical cauterization is that you instruct the patient to let the hairs grow large and even, then make a parchment in the shape of a myrtle leaf.
puis pren de savon fransois et de vive chalz, de chescun une .З., et broie ensamble bien;	Then take French soap and quicklime, of each one 3 ounces, and grind them together well.
et le fai hastanment, si qu’il ne refroide, puis en espant sus la forme que tu es fait sicom la foille dou mirte, et met sus la papiere des eulz;	And make a poultice with it to prevent cooling, then spread it on the form you have made like the leaf of the myrtle, and place eyes of paper over it.
et se li maladie tient en I oil soulement, si doit on ovrer en I, et se en ambedous ausi;	If the illness is only in one eye, you must operate on that one, and if it affects both eyes as well;
et met desoz l’oil coton moilliet en abin d’uef;	And place under the eye damp cotton soaked in egg white.
et li chiés dou malaide soit en ton sain et met ton doi mostrant sus la medicine, et presse I poc et lou muef toutes les fois que li malaide sent mordication de la medicine, car il sent mordication ausi com de feu.	And let the patient's head be in your hands and put an index finger on the medicine, and press it gently and move it every time the patient feels a stinging sensation from the medicine, because they will feel a burning sensation as well.
Quant tu as ceu fait longement, si oste la medicine a ton doit.	When you have done this for some time, remove the medication with your hand.
Et quant li mordication sera passee, si leve le leu d’awe, et rewarde se tu vois la papiere levee ausi com s’ele estoit levee par constraignement de feu ou par incision;	And when the stinging passes, remove the egg white and observe if you see the paper lifting as well as it would be lifted by a hot iron or an incision.
et s’il est ensi, si est bien.	and if it is so, then it is well.
Se ceu non, si remet encor de la medicine sus lou leu ou li medicine n’ait ovreit, tant que tes ovraiges soit igalz, et tes eulz mis a point;	If not, apply more medicine to the place where the treatment was done, until your work is even and your eyes are sharp.
puis met sus coton moilliet en burre tant que li keurs ars soit cheus, aprés cure le leu de l’oignement qui est apelez «dyafenis» et d’autre, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then place moist cotton soaked in butter until the burning heart is cooled, afterwards treat the area with ointment called "diaphenes" and others, until it is healed.
Et se t’est mestier que tu te warde bien a ton ovraige par grant warde qu’il ne chiece point de la medicine as eulz.	And if it is necessary, ensure you are careful with your work through great vigilance so that none of the medication reaches the eyes.
Et se li papiere devient mole aprés, et li poil poignent en l’oil, si recomence la medicine sus celui leu qui est mollifiez de la papiere proprement, ensi com tu as fait devant;	If the paper becomes soft afterward and hairs prick in the eye, restart the treatment on that softened area from the paper, just as you did before.
aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	Afterward, treat it until it is healed.
et c’est li forme de la fuelle dou mirte:	and this is the form of the myrtle leaf:
Et saichés que li eul des homes sont divers en grandor et en petitece, et selonc ceu soit tes constraignemens;	and know that the eyes of men differ in size and smallness, and according to this are your limitations;
et ne soit mie reponue li droite voie a celui cui est li estude de cest art.	and let not the true way be denied to him who has studied this art.
de la cure de fistule par cautere	on the treatment of fistula with cauterization
Quant tu cures fistule si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladies, et tes cures ne profitent mie, adonques covient il que tu li fais cautere selonc ceste maniere.	When you treat a fistula as we have described in the division of diseases, and your treatments are not effective, then it is necessary to perform cauterization in this manner.
Comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain;	instruct the patient to place their head on a healthy tone.
et teigne li menistres son chief entre tes mains en teil maniere qu’il ne se mueve, ne ne demoinne son chief;	hold the minister's head between your hands in such a way that it does not move or turn.
aprés met coton moilliet en abin d’uef ou en jus de persillion sus l’oil;	afterwards, place moist cotton soaked in egg white or parsley juice on the eye.
aprés chaufe le cautere qui est teilz:	after that, heat the cautery which is as follows:
et est chevez au chief si com li forme d’une penne de vouteul, ensamble la queil soit li cautere;	and it is fixed at the top of the head like the shape of a vaulted ceiling, together with where the cautery is.
se tu vues, si soit apointé des l’un chief dusc’a l’autre, et se tu vues, si soit ausi com une tente;	if you see it [the head], it should be pointed from one side to the other, and if you see it, it should also look like a tent.
mais toutevoie, cist qui est chevez vaut mues por ton ovraige.	however, this one who is beheaded will not move for your work.
Aprés presse la fistule s’ele est overte, et en trai la porriture, et la seche;	Then press the fistula if it is open, and draw out the pus, and dry it [the wound].
et s’ele est close, si la oevre, et trai fuers la bowe;	and if it is closed, open it, and draw out the bowels [the pus].
aprés met sus le cautere chaut forment, et tien ta main au cautere a la partie dou neif ensus de l’oil, que ta mains ne faice folie;	afterwards apply the hot cautery firmly, and hold your hand over the cautery at the part of the nail above the eye, so that your hand does not wander.
et met le cautere en la graisse de l’oil, et la corromp.	and put the cautery in the fat of the eye, and corrupt it.
Se tu viens au comencement dou cautere jusc’a l’os, si serait bien.	If you cauterize down to the bone, it would be beneficial.
Se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere encor une fois, et autre se tu en as mestier, et le laisse III jors;	If not, start the cautery again one more time, or another if you need it, and leave it for three days.
aprés i met sus coton moilliet en burre, et lou cure de l’oignement desiccatif tant qu’il soit sanez, et se XL jors passent qu’il ne soit sanez, si met sus medicine ague corrosive tant que li os soit descovers;	After that, put moist cotton in butter on top, and treat it with a drying ointment until it is healed, and if forty days pass without healing, then apply corrosive medicine until the bone is exposed.
et lou reis selonc ceu que il venrait en son chapistre.	and treat it according to what comes up in this chapter.
Et i a une maniere de cautere de fistule que aucun des anciens dirent.	There is also a method for cauterizing fistulas, which none of the ancients mentioned.
Entens a fistule, et fens le leu;	Understand the fistula, and split the site open.
aprés met en la fendure I camahan subtil de coi ci est li forme:	After that, put into the incision one subtle probe of what this is made from:
et i font a la quantiteit d’une .З. de plonc;	et they make it to the quantity of one 3 of plumb;
et tien ta main ou camahan fermement, et ne se mueve li malaides nes point, que li plons fondus ne corre a son oil;	et hold your hand or hammer firmly, and do not let the patient move at all, so that the molten lead does not run into his eye;
et covient c’on mette sus l’oil a malaide coton moilliet en abin d’uefz ou en awe:	and it is necessary to place on the patient's eye moist cotton dipped in egg white or honey;
li plonc si art lou leu de fistule, et lou saine per mervillouse saniteit.	the lead enters the place of the fistula, and it heals with wonderful health.
Et se li fistule est sanee per le cautere que nos avons dit, c’est boin.	And if the fistula is healed by the cauterization we mentioned, it is good.
Se ce non, si covient aministrer pertus au neif, et ramener la fistule au cors dou neif selonc ceu qu’il covient en som propre leu.	If not, you must administer an opening in the nail, and lead the fistula to the body of the nail according to what is necessary in its proper place.
des crevaices en levres	cracks in lips
Mout de fois avienent crevaices en levres que sont apelees «poil», et meismement en levres des enfans.	Very often cracks occur on lips which are called "hair", especially those of children.
Quant tu cures ces crevaices de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et li cure ne profite, adonques eschaufe I petit cautere cultellaire selonc ceste forme:	When you treat these cracks as we have described in the section above, and the treatment does not work, then heat a small knife-shaped cautery according to this method:
Et le met hastanment en celles crevaices tant qu’il viegne jusc’a font;	And he places them in the crevices until they reach the bottom.
aprés cure le leu de cerote tant qu’il soit sanez.	afterward treat the place of cauterization until it is healed.
de l’aposteme de la goule	the abscess of the throat
Quant apostume vient en la racine de la goule ou en l’uve, ou ou palais, ou as racines des dens, aprés fait porriture et ront et est enveillis et devient fistule;	When an abscess forms at the root of the throat or in the tonsil, or on the palate, or at the roots of the teeth, it causes decay and swelling and becomes inflamed and turns into a fistula;
et tu le cures si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie:	and you treat it as we have said in the section on treatment, but it does not heal:
adonques covient il que tu aies I cautere selonc la quantiteit de la fistule;	then you must apply cauterization according to the size of the fistula;
aprés le bote ou pertus de la fistule, et tien ta main tant que li fer chaus viegne au font de li, et ou derrien leu;	after the hole or opening of the fistula, hold your hand so that the hot iron reaches the bottom of it, and behind it;
et fai ensi une fois ou II, aprés le cure de ce que nos avons dit en cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do this once or twice, after treating it as we have said in the section on treatment, until it is healed;
et s’il est curez ensi, c’est boin;	and if he is cured thus, it is good.
et se ceu non, si covient descovrir le leu et oster l’os corrumput, selonc ceu que vos le troverez en son chapistre.	and if not, it is necessary to expose the place and remove the corrupt bone, according to what you will find in its chapter.
dou movement des dens	Of tooth movement
Quant les gencives sont mollifies par moistor et les dens muevent, et tu le cures per medicines et ceu ne vaut, adonc met le chief dou malaide en ton sain;	When the gums are softened by moisture and the teeth move, and you treat it with medicine but it is not effective, then place the patient's head on your lap.
aprés eschaufe le cautere dont li forme venra ci aprés en teil maniere que tu mettes une cainne sor le dent;	after, heat the cautery which will come after in this way: you place a rod over the tooth.
et met dedens le cautere chaut hastanment, et tien tant ta main que li malaides sente la chalor venant a la racine dou dent;	and put the hot cautery inside until your hand feels the heat reaching the root of the tooth;
aprés lieve ta main et rencomence le cautere selonc ta volenteit;	After lifting your hand, begin the cauterization according to your will.
aprés emplisse li malaides sa bouche d’awe salee, et la teigne une houre et raiche fuers.	After filling the patient's mouth with salty water, hold it there for an hour and rinse thoroughly.
Et en teil maniere li dens qui estoit movans si est confermez, et li gencive mollifie restrainte, et li moistors corrumpue sechie.	In this way, the moving tooth is confirmed to be stable, the softened gum restrained, and the corrupted moisture dried up.
de la dolor des dens	Of the pain of teeth
Quant dolor de dens vient por froidor, ou il i a froidor ou veir, et les cures de medicine ne valent, adonc i ait mestier de cautere selonc II manieres:	When tooth pain arises due to coldness, whether from within or without, and medical treatments are ineffective, it requires cauterization in two ways:
et cautere de burre et cautere de feu.	Cauterization with butter and fire.
Cautere de burre si est telz que tu preignes burre de vaiche, et le bout en une cuillier de fer ou d’arain;	Cauterization with butter is performed by taking cow's butter and melting it in a small iron or brass spoon.
aprés pren coton et envolope sus la pointe d’une tente, et la moille en burre bulit, et met sus le dent dolant hastanment et tien tant qu’il soit refroidiez;	Afterward, take cotton, wrap it around the tip of a needle, dip it in the melted butter, and place it on the aching tooth until it cools.
et ensi fai sovent tant que sa vertus viegne a la racine de la dent, et se tu vues si moille laine et coton en burre froit, et met sus le dent doillant, et met sus I fer chaut tant que li feus viegne au chevement dou dent.	And thus it often happens that its virtue reaches the root of the tooth, and if you wish to moisten wool and cotton in cold butter, and place it on the aching tooth, and apply a hot iron until the heat reaches the end of the tooth.
Li cauteres ensamble feu si est telz que tu preignes uns cainne de fer ou d’arain, et soit grosse si que li feus ne viegne a la bouche dou malaide;	The cautery of fire is such that you take a rod made of iron or copper, and it should be thick so that the heat does not reach the patient's mouth;
aprés chaufe le cautere, de coi li forme venra ci aprés, et le met sus le dent et tien ta main tant que li cauteres soit refroidiez;	After heating the cautery, from which its shape will come afterwards, place it on the tooth and hold your hand there until the cautery has cooled down.
fai ceu sovent, car li dolor sera ostee celui jor meisme ou l’endemain.	Do this often because the pain will be relieved on that very day or the following day.
Et covient que li malaides emplisse sa bouche de boin burre en l’empressement de cel cautere, et puis le raiche fuer;	And it is necessary for the patient to fill their mouth with good butter during the urgency of this cautery, and then let the fire cool.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And this is the form of the cautery:
Et fai cautere dou queil chief que tu voudras, et selonc ceu que tu as pooir;	And make the cautery for whatever part of the head you wish, and according to your ability;
et c’est li forme de la caine:	And this is the form of the cane:
des scrophules	Of scrofula
Quant les scrophules sont de fleume et de moistors froides, et ne sont obeissans a digestion par medicines, adonques eschaufe le cautere cheveit de coi ci aprés vient li forme, et ait II aovertures por les fumees a issir au cautere de l’autre partie;	When scrofula is caused by cold and damp humours, and it does not respond to digestion-based medicines, then heat the cautery with what follows here in this form, and make two openings for the smoke to escape from the other side of the cautery;
et met le cautere chaut sus l’apostume une fois, ou II se mestier est, tant qu’il viegne au font de l’apostume;	And place a hot cautery on the abscess once, or as often as needed, until it reaches the bottom of the abscess.
et se li apostume est petis si met cautere selonc la quantiteit de l’apostume, et le laisse ensi III jors;	And if the abscess is small, apply the cautery according to its size, and leave it in place for three days.
et met sus coton moilliet em burre tant que li arsure soit ostee;	Place damp cotton soaked in butter on top until the burn is healed.
aprés cure le leu d’oignemens et de tentes tant qu’il soit sanez.	Afterwards, treat the area with ointments and bandages until it is healed.
Li forme de la cainne:	The shape of the cane:
Quant les moistors vainquent sus les chenals dou pormon, et meismement quant ce vient de froide complexion, adonc covient que li malaides soit voidiez premiers par medicines solutives;	When moisture prevails in the body's channels, especially when it arises from a cold constitution, it is necessary that the patient first be drained through solvent medications.
aprés li fai cautere a la racine de la gorge, et te garde que tu ne venir mie jusc’a la gorge, et n’ardre dou keur mais c’un poc.	After performing the cautery at the base of the throat, be careful not to go near the throat and burn no more than a little of the heart.

et cure le leu si com nos avons devant dit tant qu’il soit sanez.	Treat the site just as we mentioned earlier until it heals.
de la toust	Of the cough.
Quant tous et maladie de pormon sont de moistors froides, et li malaides nen ait fievre ne sechor, et est li maladie anciaine, se li fai .II cauteres sus la forcele en leus vuis;	When all lung diseases are caused by cold moisture, and the patient has no fever or dryness, and it is an old disease, perform two cauteries on their ribs.

et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «clavile» selonc la forme qui est devant dite.	And let the cauterization, which is called 'clavicle', follow the form as described before.

et soient li poins jusc’a XXX, ou enqui entor.	and let the pricking be up to XXX or thereabouts.

de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	On the shoulder's dislocation:
Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes la dislocation premierement.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.

aprés lieve le keur qui est dedens le titillite as dois de ta main senestre;	Then lift the heart which is within the thistle with two fingers of your left hand.

et cauterize lou keur tant qu’il le perce jusc’a costeit, et venrait li fugure dou cautere ensamble IIII cauteres;	And cauterize the heart until it pierces through to the ribs, which would create a figure like that of four cauteries.
et por ceu est faite cautere avec le cautere qui a III ners, por coi li figure de cauterization sunt sis cauteres;	And for this reason the cautery is made with a cauterizer that has three blades, thus creating a pattern of six cauteries.
et sont li nerf selonc la subtiliteit d’une tente et c’est li forme dou cautere qui a III ners:	And the nerves follow the subtlety of a tent, which is the shape of the cauterizer with three blades.
Et aucune fois est ajostez sus ce I nerf por coi il i a VIII cauteres.	and sometimes it is adjusted to this one nerve, thus there are eight cauteries.
Aprés met sus le cautere porrelz broiez avec seil;	After this place on the cautery some ground ivy leaves.
aprés fai reposer le malaide, et ne soit meus li membres par lonc tens tant qu’il soit bien confortez.	Then let the patient rest, and do not move the limb for a long time until it is well supported.
Et s’il est desaloiez desus, liquelz chose avient poc, adonques fait cautere sus l’epaisse dou cautere clavile, ou mout de cauteres en poignant.	And if it is dislocated again soon after, then quickly perform a cautery on the thick part of the clavicle, or many cauteries in succession.
Car li jointure est refermee, et est ostee li moistor et est sanez li malaides.	For the joints are closed, and moisture is removed, and the patient is healed.
Quant en l’estomac vienent froidures et mout de moistors tant qu’il l’estraient a sa complexion, et sont multipliet li catharre a lui, et es manieres de cures acostumees et il ne profite mie, adonc covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son dos, et estende ses jambes et ses mains.	When cold and excess moisture arise in the stomach to such an extent that they disrupt its natural balance, and catarrh is multiplied within it, and with customary treatments it does not improve, then it is necessary that the patient be recalled onto their back, extending their legs and hands.
De ceu en aprés li fai III cauteres I desoz la cuillier dou pis per la quantiteit d’un doi, a tout le cautere clavile, et II cauteres defuers les II costez tant que li figure des cauteres soit a III angles, et ait teil espaice entre l’une et l’autre qu’elles ne soient jointes ensamble quant elles giteront porriture;	After this perform three more cauterizations - one below the heel of the foot equal in quantity to two thumbs, on each side of the cautery as long as the pattern of the cauteries forms a triangle, and ensure there is enough space between them so they are not joined together when laying down.
et soient li cautere si parfont qu’il porpreignent les II pars dou keur, et soit li figure des cauteres selonc ceste forme sens ajostement:	and let the cauterization be so thorough that it purifies the two parts of the heart, and let the shape of the cauterizations be according to this form without adjustment.
Et se tu vues cauterize d’un grant cautere enmi l’estomac selonc ceste forme;	And if you wish to cauterize with a large cautery in the middle of the stomach according to this form;
et celui qui avra paour de cest cautere, cauterize en poignant et seigne sus l’estomac i. point selonc la quantiteit que tu vues d’enche;	and for those who fear this cautery, cauterize by pricking and making an incision on the stomach instead. Puncture according to the quantity you wish to introduce.
puis le cauterize a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins».	then cauterize with all the "point" cautery.
Aprés le cure de la cure que nos avons eut devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the treatment of the wound that we had before, until it is healed.
Quant au foie vient dolor de froit et de moistor et de grosse ventositeit, tant qu’il est fuer mis de sa complexion natureil per les superfluitez;	When the liver experiences pain from cold, moisture, and excessive gas, indicating it has moved away from its natural state due to excesses;
et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne li profite mie, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son haitereil;	and the patients are cured of what we have said before in sections, and it does not benefit them, so the patient must be reminded about their belongings;
et signe d’enche III cauteres selonc ceste forme et ceste figure et ceste quantiteit sus lou foie, defuer les ypocondres, lai ou li coutes de l’ome vient;	and the sign of the third cautery is applied according to this form and this shape with this amount on the liver, outside the hypochondrium, where the ribs of a man are located;
et ait d’espaice entre chaicun cautere la groissece d’un doi;	and leave a space between each cautery equal to the thickness of one finger;
et soient li cautere dou lonc dou cors, et ne presser mie mout ta main a tot le cautere;	and let the length of the cautery be proportional to that of the body, and do not apply too much pressure with your hand throughout the entire cautery process;
et soit arse tant soulement li moitiez dou keur, et soit li malaides drois sus ses piez;	and let only half of the heart be burned, and keep the patient upright on their feet;

et c’est li forme:	and this is the procedure:
Et se ta volentez est, si cauterize ces cauteres dou cutellaire, se tu es subtilz et saiges en l’art, et te warde que tu n’ardes mie tout le keur, car tu feroies sechier tout le cors;	And if you wish to do so, cauterize these cautery wounds with the knife, provided that you are skilled and wise in this art, and be careful not to burn all of it, for you would make his whole body dry.
et qu’il ne viegne jusc’a boueil, car li keurs est mout subtilz lai endroit, et lou saiches por voir.	and that it does not come close to the mouth, because the heart is very delicate there, and you would make him dry for no reason.
Quant il a apostume au foie, et tu vues savoir s’il est en la char dou foie ou en la toile:	When there is an abscess on the liver, and you wish to determine whether it is within the flesh of the liver or in its membrane:
s’il est en la char, se sent li malaides dolor ne mie trop fort;	If it is within the flesh, the patient feels pain but not excessively strong.
et s’il est en la toile, si sent dolor forsenee.	And if it is in the skin, they feel unbearable pain.

aprés la cure selonc la cure des essues tant qu’il soit sanez;	After the treatment according to the type of dressing until it is healed.
et ne covient mie que de cest cautere use nuls fuers que cil qui ait estudieit longement en l’art de medicine, et par cui mains cestes maladies ont corrut aucune fois.	And it is not suitable for anyone other than those who have studied the art of medicine at length to use this cauterization technique, through whose hands these diseases have sometimes been cured.
Adonques puet il hardiement ovrer, et toutevoies il me semble que mues vaut li laissier.	Then he may operate boldly, and yet it seems to me that one is better off leaving them alone.
dou cautere de pleuresin	sinew cautery.
Li ancien dirent que on doit faire a pleuresin cauteres de racines d’aristologe, et en teil maniere:	The ancients said that one should make cauterizations with the roots of aristolochia, and in this manner:

et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	and do not squeeze your hand, rather apply pressure gently as in smelling.

et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	and if it relieves pain, as we have said for the abscess of the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this work there is fear that the patient may die now or develop a fistula which cannot be cured.
de la mice	From the nose.

When you treat the disease from the nose as we have said in the treatment sections, and it does not improve, then there are three types of cautery that are all good.

de ydropisie	of dropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cauterization is not useful for dropsy, except for the method called 'ascites'.
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you treat it according to the methods we have mentioned in our discussion and your treatment does not benefit them, then it is necessary for you to apply four cauterizations around the navel, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one on the spleen, two behind the back on the spine, and one near the hip;

et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	And healing would hasten, and the two intentions will be together with God's help.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The shape of the cautery for the belly should be like the template we showed before;
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	And that one for the back is an olive-shape, as shown previously.
de l’enfleure des piez	The swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in someone who is dropsical, and they are filled with yellow water, you should cauterize on the back of the foot between the little toe and the ring finger;
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	And lift your hand with the cautery without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply, so as not to pierce the yellow water, and let the cautery be according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	After make on two legs, two cauteries on each leg at the tip of the calf muscle.
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	And let the length of the cautery be such that one is below the knee in front and the other outside, in the middle of the leg.
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	And leave the cauteries open for some time without cleaning them, let pus form within them.
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After that, clean other wounds as we have said before.
de la menoison	From the house
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When belly ache comes from cold and moisture, so that the retaining and digesting virtues which are in the stomach and intestine become weakened, and cannot be cured by means of cauteries.
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	And if you see the patient suffering greatly and of strong constitution, then make one large cautery on the stomach according to what has been discussed before about the stomach cautery, at the circular cautery.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	et four cauterizations around the neck delicate for all one cauterization clavicle delicate, and two cauterizations above the hips.
