Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see abundant moisture and the patient suffering, apply a cautery to the wrist, one cautery on each elbow, and two small cauteries on the stomach near the large [one], for the treatment is beneficial when there is good assistance.
de la cure des emorroydes	For the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When hemorrhoids are at the foundation, one or more, and they are ancient, made of large cold and moist corrupt humors, and they are treated as we have said in sections, but it does not help, then make cauterizations:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	Three above the spine of the back, which is entirely outside below the shoulder, and two in a triangle under the chin.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	and if you think their stomach is chilled, and the flesh is not cooking, and one sees swelling in the face, then make a large cauterization on the stomach as it was said before, and another on the liver, and yet another on the chin with all the clavicle cauterizations;
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	And leave the open cautery for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment, let the site heal until it is completely healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	Of fleshiness which is named "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you treat an abscess, heat up the cautery that looks like a razor, and then place it fully heated onto the opened abscess;
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	And leave your hand there until the cautery reaches the opening of the wound, from which the blood flows out;
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	Do this once or twice, and if there is much abscess, cauterize each part as we have said;
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	After the curative treatments with ointments, continue until they are healed;
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	And if you cauterize with a large cautery on alum, it will provide greater aid.
de plaie mal curee	Of badly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When a patient cannot bear the scalpel or incision, as we will describe in its place, such illness arises that can only be healed through cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When a fistula develops and emits purulent matter along with foul-smelling moisture, you must first examine it carefully using an appropriate probe, taking care to know the entire length of the abscess.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, 
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	And beware of burning the nerves which are sensitive, and the large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	If the fistula goes into the body of the bladder and to the intestine, avoid these places, and do not cauterize over flesh, for it is not deep.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	After treatment, wait until the place is healed, and if the area is salty, and the matter has been removed for a long time, then know that the wound is entirely healed.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	And if the matter has not been removed, know that the wound is still open, and the bone at its base is corrupted.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	And so with one of these that we will say in their place.
de la maladie des reins	En l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When pain from cold comes to the loins, and there is excessive flatulence, and it does not affect a woman's condition, then you must perform a cauterization on one side of the loins and on the other with the clavicle cautery as we previously mentioned;
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	and if we cauterize it in the middle, there will be three cauterizations in a row, and they will provide greater relief.
de la vessie	Of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is soft and weak due to cold and moisture, causing the patient to retain urine, then cauterize above the bladder in the area where the arm hairs begin, on both the right and left sides, and each cautery should be as long as the width of a thumb.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and make one or two cauterizations on the back, depending on your need;
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	And let the clavi cautery be performed according to the form previously mentioned.
de la marris	From a marsh
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the womb is cold and moist, and does not allow for conception, and the flowers are corrupted and their ends delayed;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, she experiences great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	then it is necessary that we apply three cauteries around the navel, as we have mentioned for the bladder cautery, and two cauteries outside the back;
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and let the clavi cautery be performed as we have said.
de la hainche	Of the hip.
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When the viscous moisture descends into the hip socket and causes it to displace from its position, with the sign being that one thigh is longer than the other when measured together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	And you will find the location of the hip joint, so it is necessary that you cauterize the patient on the side of the hip with a cautery similar to a circle, and bleed in front of the joint around the bone as it turns, so that the bone remains within the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and if the cautery is such as those used to cauterize the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if this cautery is not present, make three large olive-sized cauteries, and let the cauteries be as perfect as all hearts;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat [the patient] until they are healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	Of the hip's pain.
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes to the hip bone, and it is due to coldness and moisture, and the patient has been treated as we have said in the previous section but the treatment is not effective, and the illness is chronic:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	So it is necessary for you to purge the patient of gross humours with foul-smelling pills or other good similar pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After doing the cautery procedure;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	And the manner of performing the cautery is according to two methods:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	That is to say, altogether burning medicines, and cauterisation by fire.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Caeterisation by fire is according to many methods, of which one is as follows:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	You should cauterise above the hip with three triangular-shaped cauteries according to this form, making a good deep mark and large in size, leaving space between each cautery equal to the width of your thumb, and let the cauteries be olive-oil coloured.
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Sometimes a cauterization is performed in the middle above the hip joint, for which there are four methods according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you see it, cauterize with the circular cautery we mentioned before for the hip dislocation;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	But make sure that the circles cover the entire hip joint, and all parts of the heart are burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	This is the method employed for sciatica when pain is localized in the hip and does not extend to the thigh or leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it reaches the thigh and leg, do two cauterizations where the patient feels the pain is located, and four above the ankle on the left side.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	The cauterizations should be made with a knife-like instrument, and the thickness of the heart tissue should be burned.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if the patient feels that the pain extends down to their toes or close to them, cauterize where they feel the pain with three or four points using a tool called 'points'.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if it is necessary, do more of this to them;
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if they know that the pain is beneath the knee towards the thigh, use a chisel or circular cautery on them, and be very careful with all your cauterizations so as not to leave the tool for too long, lest you burn their nerves and large arteries, and cause even more harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who underwent cauterization on the ankle of the foot, and they left it so that their leg became completely swollen, as well as their feet, and their feet were pierced and corrupted throughout.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After the abdominal operation which resulted in death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts together, cauterize both one and the other, according to this method.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise ones say regarding hip cauterization, this is how it's done: make a tool that has one end like an inch-wide knuckle bone or slightly smaller, and perforate it with holes at regular intervals, each hole spaced about as wide as your thumb.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and let there be two interlocking parts [of the instrument], also like nuts, and have one iron screw well-made;
et c’est li forme:	and this is its form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	Heat it until it is red hot and throw away the coals, then place it onto the diseased hip bone, turning it towards the healthy side of the body.
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	Cauterise once with one cautery, then leave for three days.
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	Then make an ointment of butter and leave the wound open for a long time.
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the treatment with ointment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasim says that we rarely use this cautery due to the fear of its appearance, and we see few who do.
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	And nonetheless, it is one of the good cauterizations, which can be tolerated if applied correctly and slowly.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The burning cauterizations of medicine are such that you make an instrument with crossed bars into which descends the edge of the port, and it is made of brass or iron on one side, and at a height of two fingers, with each section as thick as a thumb.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	And it should be open on top and bottom, and the parts join together in this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	Afterwards, place the box of the hip on the patient lying on their healthy side, and press your hand firmly onto the box.
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After placing between the two circles of hot water that has been heated over one fire pot, leave it for an hour's time and let the patient bear its heat and burning.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For there is also a biting sensation as of fire found therein;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	And once the biting sensation has passed, lift your hand with the instrument and raise the hip of tepid water, leaving it thus for three days, and apply butter until that which is blackened by scalding is removed.
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	And you let it rest there for three days so as to draw out the corruption of humours.
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	And this would be the last aid after the treatment of ointments until it is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has extended to the thigh or down to the leg, make him a poultice that holds back according to what you have done for the hip similarly.
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and this is the method of the hot poultice, which I have described in the treatise on medical correction.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and quicklime, equal parts of each, grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	where there is a small opening for it, so that the tip of a lancet can enter.
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and place over it another well-sealed pot, and put on alkali and heat, and gentle steam above, until there is two fingers of steam above the powders when you have properly gripped with your hand.
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	leave it this way until steam condenses and drips water into the sealed pot, then take all that steam, pour it over heat and alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And then there will be great pain, administered through many medical procedures and cauterizations of other body parts.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it causes the same effect as fire, and there are other treatments such as those in which one cauterizes the hip well with iron, and mixtures of honey, nuts, and hot soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a cure where a man was cured of hip pain and sciatica, and he praises it greatly, saying that no other treatment was used, and he was healed immediately after this cure was performed, and he took a bath as he instructs below.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And he describes it in this way: take fresh and dry green litharge, grind it very well with a pound of grease, apply it to the hip, thigh, and leg where the pain is felt, and bind it.
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and leave it for three hours, or until the patient no longer feels the burn caused by this treatment.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then let him enter the bath until his body is a little warmed up, and place him in bed, and the pain will disappear completely and he shall be cured.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use such medicines of cauterization without first evacuating the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat dung, it provides much relief;
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	et must be done with the cauterization in such a manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take linen and cover it with old oil-based grease, and place it on the depression which is between the big toe and the one next to it, called the fossa.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After take dry goat fat, and heat it to embers, place on the wool, and leave until it is extinguished.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	then repeat again in this way, and do not stop doing so until you feel it has reached the hip, and that the pain has ceased.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	And this method of cauterization is called "goat cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	From the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether from falling or due to impact or excessive loss, or because of similar spread matter that is cold, in none of these cases are caustic remedies good except for those caused by an influx of cold material.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	The patient must be made to void themselves of foul pills or other such things that are on their back, where the pain is located, three lines signed with ink, and in each line there should be V cauterizations or more depending on their condition and how much they can withstand.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	and perform the caustics according to a caustic called "point
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you see [something], make three or four caustics on the clavicle in this manner:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	This illness often affects young children, and the signs of its onset are narrow shoulders when they rise up, and fear.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you find on the last vertebra of the spine, in us, an appearance that arises on other vertebrae.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this, and treat it, cauterize it with the cold cautery according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that the cautery touches each part of the spine evenly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see fit, cauterize around the spine with the sharp cautery using two or three lines, and let the points be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After treat the place until it is healed according to what we have said, and be wary of applying cautery to a swollen area with nerve damage.
de la dolor des jointes	Of the pain of joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When joint pain arises from moisture that spreads to every limb of the body, and when foot pain comes about, which doctors call "gout" properly, and when it is caused by coldness and medicines cannot cure it, then treat it with caustics in this manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Do a series of fire cauterizations around the ankle joint, and let the cauterizations be olive-shaped according to this form.
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if it is necessary to act upon the front of the foot, make a single cauterization that we call a "dot.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pain extends to the knees and other joints, which happens frequently, apply three or four cauterizations on each knee in every part, with each cauterization being olive-shaped.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you need to do more, proceed with additional cauterizations, but don't hold your hand close for longer than it takes the heart-shaped tip of the cautery iron to become red hot.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the knees and back, apply the cautery as we described in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pain is in the hands, make two lines of punctures around the wrist.
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	And if there remains no pain in the fingers, make punctures on each joint and also above the hair of the hand.
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains reach up to the neck or shoulders, cauterize each affected area and ensure good care for the patient with proper medication.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you provide good care and remove the phlegm, he will be healed with God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	For rupture of the spleen
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When a rupture occurs in the groin area and the testicles descend into the scrotum, which is a recent development, one must ensure that on the day of treatment, the patient does not eat.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	And have him consume things that relax the belly, so that the stool may descend from his abdomen.
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	Afterward, make him sit on his back between your hands, and instruct him to hold his breath until the testicles are retracted, then pull them with your fingers, and cauterize below the rupture onto the bone of the hip joint, marking it entirely in a semi-circle shape above the body.
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Then heat the cautery with this is its shape:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	Until it becomes white and emits no smell.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then replace the balls back to their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	And the attendant should hold his hand so that it does not go backwards;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	Spread the patient's legs well, and place a cushion beneath them with a bandage on their thighs, and another on their feet to hold their hands;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	Then place the cautery on the sign with your whole hand, and hold it straight and firmly until you reach the bone. If you do not reach the bone in one go, repeat this process again until you hit the bone;
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	Be careful that the eye does not pop out when you apply the cautery;
que tu ne le brulasses;	That you do not burn him/it;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and that the patient does not die or suffer other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not reach the bone with the cauterization, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it is appropriate that the cauterization for children be subtle according to their size, and for adults also large according to their measure;
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	after three days treat the site of the butter cautery until the burning sensation is gone;
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	after the treatment with other ointments until it is healed, and let the patient lie on their back for forty days until the wound is well-fused;
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	and it is necessary that his nourishment be sufficient for a long time, so that the wound does not protrude when he tries to go into a room.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after forty days, when he wishes to rise, provide him with a well-made bandage, and wear it for another forty days.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	Let him have good rest, avoid excessive exertion, and guard against too much overindulgence in drinking or eating, as well as shouting at high volume.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And when he follows this instruction, he will be entirely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I shall now speak of the treatment for amputation, in its own chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	Of abdominal rupture.
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When tumors spread to other organs and are known to be malignant, and you see that they no longer grow, apply a cauterization treatment according to its size, burning off one third of the heart.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	After the treatment, follow up as we have instructed.
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	And some of the ancients have said that one must cauterize with a three-angled cautery according to this form.
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	But first mark the spot with an X and draw one line across the width above the rupture, then another perpendicular to it, and hold your hand over the entire cautery instrument.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the initial cauterization is lighter and more gentle.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain arises in any limb, whether from falling or injury, and this pain persists for a long time, and medical treatment is ineffective, then it is necessary that the patient be cauterized with a tool called a "point," and the cautery should be applied according to the length of the limb, its thickness, weakness, strength, and location of twists and pains.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	If it is blistered by the first cautery, that is good.
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If this is not the case, perform another cautery on top of it, for such a practice should change in the member closest to it; therefore, you must carry out cauteries until the patient blisters.
de meselerie	of surgery
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The months are aided sometimes by cauterization for great relief, especially illnesses that come from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	Once you have seen the patient cauterized, observe if the illness is at its beginning and has been treated according to what we've said in the division; it does not descend nor remain, and you doubt that corruption will spread throughout the entire patient, then apply five cauteries on top of each other.
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	On my head at nine o'clock, and the other towards the forehead at the end of the hair.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and two above the horns, and one behind on the nape.
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and I leave your hand there until the cauterization reaches the bone, and also so that scabs form and the vapors of thick humors can escape.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and cauterize it on the wound according to what is necessary.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the injury is spread everywhere,
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and it is clearly discharging pus, then you must cauterize it with these types of cauterization we have mentioned for the head, and one cauterization on top of the nape, two cauterizations on the spine of the neck, six cauterizations on the spine of the back, one large one on the buttocks and another nearby, and two on each shoulder.
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	II on the ribs, II on the knuckles of the toes, I on each joint of hands and feet, and in the pits of the hands.
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and beware of the nerves that are above the back of the heel, lest you burn them.
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	and never make a cauterization on the bone of the wrist, and another one on the bone of the abdomen, and yet another one on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that the more cauterizations you make, the more help you provide, and it benefits him.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And know that the patient feels no pain from the cauterization as a healthy person would, because his body is already corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	The cautery should be large and small depending on the limbs and joints, according to what you find appropriate for the tools at hand.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treatment, apply flour paste with honey to the wound and use other treatments until it is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When swelling occurs in any limb and is treated with medicine, oils, and plasters but it does not heal, then perform cauterization on the limb according to its size and proportion.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	and let the cautery be slightly beyond the depth of the heart's point;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it with ointments until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	One may also apply cauterization to the hand, foot, or back at the exit point of the nerve that moves the limb, and thus remove the swelling.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	however, one should not intervene without knowledge of the limbs and the paths of the nerves that move the body.
de albaras	Of erysipelas.
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the illness known as "albaras" has persisted and medical treatments prove ineffective, then apply a perfect cautery to it slightly, according to the depth of the heart's species until the whiteness is removed, and its colour is changed.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	Then treat it with a remedy made of flour of vetch and lentils mixed with rose oil and plantain leaves, and one part each of pigeon blood and sparrow blood.
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	Mix everything together well, wrap it in a cloth, and apply it to the affected area until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of cancer with cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When cancer appears at the beginning, and you wish to stop its growth, cauterize it with a circular cautery, all around the circumference of the cancerous area.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And yet the wise ones say that one should also apply a cautery to the middle of the cancerous growth.
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	and nevertheless it does not seem good to me, for I fear that it will be ulcerated and corrupted, and I have already seen this happen before.
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	and moreover the most appropriate thing is to cauterize around it with the circular cautery, as we have said before about various cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	On swelling that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When someone has an illness called 'adubelati', and they are slow to die either due to the excess of matter it produces or because of the patient's condition when they are decrepit (that is, very old) with little blood left in them, or perhaps due to the season;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you want to see it hasten their death:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	then cauterize around it with many small cauteries, touching only slightly;
aprés le laisse ensi.	After leaving it like this.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For she will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it piercing through the entire cauterization, then heat the cautery with what it is formed from:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of that illness which is called 'adubelati' until the cautery has pierced the heart, and let it be such a cautery that the patient feels it from outside in such a way that the course of decay is lessened.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	Afterwards, treat until it is perfectly healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	the treatment with fire by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	There is another kind of illness which is called 'corrodens', and it is nothing but a wasting away of the limbs, for it withers the limbs just as fire withers dry branches.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this illness in a place that can withstand cauterization with fire, then heat the small and large claw-shaped cauteries, according to what is suitable for the location or where the illness is;
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	After that, cauterize it from all sides until you eradicate all the corruption, leaving nothing of it behind, so that everything that is corrupted is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Then leave it for three days, and apply on the cauterized areas an ointment ground up with oil so that the scaldings from the fire are removed, along with all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	Afterward treat it with ointments producing flesh.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if you see no new scab form after three days, that is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	If not, begin the cauterization again on what remains in the corrupted areas.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this disease is sometimes cured with medication rather than fire cauterization;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	but nevertheless fire cauterization is of greater aid, and I have already mentioned the treatment for quartan fever in the section on remedies:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	take it when you need it.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	inflamed blisters that come on the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Often the feet become afflicted with a disease we call "claws," which are faulty growths that wound the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And there are two ways of cauterizing this disease.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say, fire cautery, and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Fire cauterization is when you heat an iron cautery as well as a lanceolate-shaped spatula, and it should be made of good iron to the measure that it can grasp the nail from all sides, and that it has fine edges.
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	After that, put it all hot on the nail, and turn your hand around the nail so that it reaches the bottom of the nail.
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	Leave it like this for three days until it begins to discharge pus.
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Then make an ointment of wild mallows crushed with salt, and leave the ointment on overnight; the nail will come out and be uprooted from its root.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the place of injury by applying ointment until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are converted by force within the body, and occur frequently in hands and feet, then you must apply a hot water cautery to them.
et est en teil maniere:	and it is done in this way:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	Take a rod of brass or iron, or the quill of an inkwell, and place it on top of the nail and its counterpart, which are the warts;
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	And place the rod so that it covers all around, then put a drop of hot water on it, and hold your hand firmly, and press your hand while turning so that the edge of the rod reaches the root of the nail, allowing the hot water to penetrate deeply into the root.
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	and let the patient endure a little the bite of hot water for an hour.
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	then leave it like this, and it will pull out all at its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Thus do one after another until you eradicate all those that are in the body, then treat them with ointments that generate flesh.
li cure dou trembler	The doctor for shaking/trembling.
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When some tremble from coldness of nerves, or quartan fever, or any other, you must make four cauterizations on the back's spine, one between each vertebra.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and one cauterization on the foot, and one olive-oil cauterization on the stomach.
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	let him shiver, and hasten his recovery from the cold illness.
des pustules puans	Stinking blisters/pustules.
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Sometimes the body breaks out in baths/sores or stinking blisters which come from gross corrupt matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	for the first, when they appear, it is fitting to make a cauterization on each head of the pimple.
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	A subtle cautery with myrtle wood, for which the tip is taken by fire, or long aristoloche root, or lenticular cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And sometimes they cauterize in the beginning when they appear, according to this method, and it prevents them from growing forward, but breaks the excess that comes forth, and they are healed.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it should be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut off
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	There are often great outflows of blood from the artery that is cut in the wound or incision of an abscess, or when cauterizing a limb and similar things.
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	And it is very difficult to staunch (stop the flow).
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And yet when this happens to someone, hasten to place your index finger on the wound's injury, pressing firmly until blood ceases to flow beneath your finger and not a drop more escapes.
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	then apply multiple small and large olive-oil cauterizers to the fire until they all turn red;
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	take one, either large or small depending on the wound and the location of the artery, place the cauterizer on that vessel where you are holding your finger, and keep it there until the blood flow stops.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if there is a spark when you lift your finger above the wound, and the cauterization has ended, then take another of the hot cauteries immediately.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	Do not cease doing this one after another until the blood is completely extinguished.
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	Be careful not to burn the nerve nearby and avoid any other mischief that may befall the patient.
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	And know that when blood flows from the artery, it cannot be properly staunched especially when the artery is large, unless by one of the four methods we have mentioned.
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	By cauterization or by extraction if it is not treated, or by strongly binding with thread, or by applying medications that have the power to staunch blood.
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And be bound tightly as necessary.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	What will bring about staunching is binding tightly with linen cloths or putting hot things on it, or other similar methods, and nothing else profits therefrom.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if it happens to someone and they have neither thread nor medicine available, they must place their index finger on the wound of the vein as we have said, and press down firmly until it is staunched over the wound and over the vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	And do not move the finger, but moisten it with cold water often so that it is very cold until the blood is frozen and thickened and staunched.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and make incisions beforehand on those parts where it is necessary for cauterization and medication.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of surgical treatments.
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter about all diseases which require fire cauterization or burning medications, and their symptoms, causes, instruments, and methods of cauterization.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	and placed this chapter on the head to feet, and I will go in this same manner in this chapter so that what is desired can be found more easily.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And so, as I begin this work, dear child, you must learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first about cauterization, and thus it requires greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	Where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to undertake foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many types of people come seeking treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	If they die from such [illnesses] that afflict them so much alongside their illness that they faint easily due to the shock they experience from their condition and the severity of their ailment.
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	And these we ought to fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	From such there are those who will give you their insight, and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	Wait, I am healed".
et li maladie est despitouse.	But the illness is obstinate.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	You must not consent to those who approach you with such mannerisms, but place greater emphasis on your honour than on your greed, and do not act hastily but wisely in matters of which you are certain and can claim credit for.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	And use prognostics and indicators in treating your patients for their healing.
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	And this will help you gain a good reputation, glory, and a memorable legacy.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	My dear son, may our Lord give you good understanding and righteousness, and if he wills to inspire you with his holy breath, so be it.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Now I have ordered this chapter for you by dividing it into chapters, according to what is presented in the previous chapter on cauterization, which I explained from head to toe so that you may find more easily what you need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	A head full of water.
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	Know that this illness often comes to children during birth, when the midwife grips the child's head too tightly.
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	And sometimes it happens for reasons unknown.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	I have never seen this illness occur outside of children, and in all cases I've witnessed, the child died.
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And for this reason, it seems best to leave the treatment of such cases to others.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I saw a child whose shoulder was filled with fluid, and the head swelled each day to the point that he could not bear it.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	The moisture grew so much that he died, and this fluid had gathered beneath the bone on the shoulder blade, between the heart and the bone.
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	And the work is such if the fluid is between the heart and bone, and the abscess is small, that you should make a wide incision in the middle of the shoulder.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	And it should be as long as two fingers, so that the fluid runs out.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	And you will see here the shape of the spatula.
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is deeper, and the abscesses are larger, make two incisions in the form of a cross, according to this shape:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is below the bone, and you see signs of the comminution of the skull with the sutures open on all sides, and there is fluid that spurts forth when you press it with your hand inside, and this has not responded to treatment.
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	you must cut into the head with three incisions in this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, remove all moisture quickly.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After treating the incisions with cloths and powders, apply wine and oil, and leave it like this for five days.
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	Then release the head and treat the wound with tented bandages and ointments, leaving it compressed equally, and feed the patient dry meat to absorb moisture until the limb is strengthened and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another method of incision is to look at where the swelling of the abscess appears, and its collection of pus.
car aucune fois est elle devant;	because sometimes it comes before.
aucune fois derrier;	sometimes behind.
aucune fois en destre;	sometimes on the right.
et aucune fois en senestre.	and sometimes on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Cut therefore at the place where the abscess appears, and its filling with pus, and make an incision according to your ability.
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and be careful not to cut the artery.
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and if veins of blood flow, so that the patient dies from loss of blood and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	Of rheumatism.
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When someone has a disease called "cataract" in the eyes or throat, and it is an old illness that does not benefit from medical treatment, then the last resort is cauterization along with cutting of the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	It is necessary, therefore, when you cut his eyes, that the patient turn their head back;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	After rubbing the place with a coarse cloth until the arteries appear, then have the patient stretch their neck away from the cloth;
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	Then look where the vein beats, and its courses are after the ears, and they are ready to be pierced;
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Then mark the courses of blood with ink, then cut one and the other with a sharp spatula that is two fingers wide, so that the blade reaches down to the bone, but not into the brain.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you see it, push the spatula beneath the artery and the cup above, cutting also as II must across.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, blood will continually spurt upwards forcefully.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery does not appear by feeling it, you must measure a space of three fingers, then mark with ink and cut down to the bone;
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	and for this, it is necessary to let out six ounces of blood, and perhaps a little more or less, according to what the patient can endure, and the fullness of the artery.
puis regarde la plaie:	then examine the wound.
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	if there is no bone sticking out of the wound, ensure that a hot abscess does not develop, then clean the wound and bind it, treating it with ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	of migraine
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When an old migraine comes, with a thick discharge due to the moisture of tears and heat in the temples and an old, persistent headache with similar symptoms, and no medical treatment helps, we extract the arteries from the temples and cauterize them, as we have explained.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the method of extracting them is for the patient to pull back the hairs on their temples, and pay attention to the artery that appears in the temple, as it can be easily seen by its pulsation, although it may not appear prominently in some people who are too cold.
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	and if it is dislocated, the patient should have their neck held by some cloth, then rub the area with a rough fabric, and pour warm water over the location until the artery appears clearly.
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	then take the spatula of which this is the shape: [insert shape]
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	then lightly scrape the skin until you reach the artery, then pull it upwards with pincers, and carefully remove the membranes that are underneath on each side;
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	and if the artery is thin, turn it with the point of the hook, then cut it from that side according to the quantity of two fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not cut, the blood cannot flow out completely everywhere.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	and draw out blood from six cents, until you reach three.
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	and if the artery is large, you must tie it in two places with a strong double silk thread so that gangrene does not come before the wound heals, and blood flows out continuously.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	then remove the excess flesh between the two lines at that very moment, and then, if you wish, cauterize it with a knife-cautery down to the bone until the head of the shoulder is cut off.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	and this is a delicate operation if the patient does not have fever and has a hot complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For cauterization helps to dry up moisture.
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	for it is of greater help for moisture.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	For the extraction of arteries, one must fill the space with old cotton and place well-made bandages over it.
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and when you remove them, ensure to apply dry medicinal herbs that promote flesh growth and bandages until it is healed.
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	and if blood escapes from the artery while you work on it, quickly cut and cauterize with a hot iron, or use vitriol and squeeze by hand to stop the bleeding.
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	and if you don't have the aforementioned items available, place your hand directly on it to freeze the blood, pour cold water over until bleeding stops, and apply pressure as necessary.
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	what is more efficient and lightweight in the extraction of an artery is to cauterize the vein with this cutting-edge hot iron divided into two parts, but ensure the divisions are thick enough to maintain heat longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instrument is too thin, it retains less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	And there must be a thickness of space between the two knives, and then when you have secured both places, place the burning iron on it until it reaches the bone, and cut the vein into two parts.
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	and be separated between the two shoulders as they are not fully fused from this cautery on all sides.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	and here is the shape of the cautery:
des larmes	tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	When the tears from the eyes flow down along the veins that are on top of the skull and it is not beneficial to apply any medical treatment here, you will see the patient's face turn red and feel a pulsation or tremor in their forehead.
et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	and if their eyes are swollen and moist so that the hair around them falls out, and the eyelids become hot and scalded by the heat of the tears, then it is necessary to apply this treatment.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	And the ancients called it "healing of contusions," and for the patient suffering from this ailment, make sure they have hair on their forehead, then give them three incisions equally spaced along the length of the forehead.
et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres;	Let one incision be made in the middle of the forehead towards the nose, and the others at both sides above the eyebrows, taking care to avoid cutting into the arteries located at these sides above the eyebrows.
et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins;	Keep your hand away from the line connecting both jaws, and let each wound be three fingers in length across its width.
et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	Have ready a piece of sponge and plenty of cloth to wipe away the blood, then take a spatula with two sharp edges, which is shaped like this:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision;	From the incision which is above the temple to the second incision
et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	And scrape all the heart which is between the two fissures to all the soft part that is above the bone, then do likewise from the middle incision to the other second one, and then extract this spatule.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	Insert into the first incision the instrument that is called a "cultellaire," which is very sharp on one side and soft but not sharp on the other, and it has this form:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	Place the sharp side of the instrument towards the flesh above the scalp and the soft side towards the bone, and insert it until it reaches the middle incision.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer;	And cut all the vessels that descend from the head to the eyes so that the incision is continuous up until those which appear of the heart, and then do likewise in the middle fissure up until the other exterior one.
et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris;	And then extract an equal amount of blood, and press the place for the captured blood.
puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne;	Then place in each fissure a tent of old cotton, and put on moistened bandages with wine and oil and eggs, and make sure no hot abscesses come.
et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	On the third day, undo the binding, and apply a large poultice of warm water, then treat it with an ointment of basilicon mixed with rose oil, and other treatments used for wounds until it is healed.
dou reume des eulz	For the kingdom of eyes
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees;	When someone presents with acute cataracts as a habit, and you see their eyes turned and small, and weakened vision, and the corneas burned;
et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue;	and their hair falls out, and there is pain at the top of the head, and the patient sneezes;
adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	then you will know that these symptoms and this catarrh come from many sources, and the only true cure is as follows:
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	And so you instruct the patient to raise their forehead, then make a large incision in the middle of the forehead, and another from the wide eye socket.
Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os;	Begin with an incision from the left temple to the right temple, going down as deep as the bone;
et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier;	and keep your hand away from the nerves of the temples which cause eating.
et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin;	and when the bone is exposed, wipe all the blood with a sponge, then separate between the two lips of the wound and place old cotton, and line with linen bandages.
puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut;	Then bind moistened cloths soaked in wine and oil on top, and beware of hot abscesses.
quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char.	when it is removed, you must rub the bone until flesh begins to grow, then treat with drying agents that promote healing.
En teil maniere:	In this manner:
pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre;	Take two parts wheat flour, and four parts colophony, and make a plaster.
et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	And administer to these wounds to generate flesh throughout.
