et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	et I saw man with II or belly which were more like fungi than anything else, and there was no difference, and they were white, and had small roots, and were slightly split, and moisture came out of them immediately.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	I cut them open and found in one XVIII ounces of weight, and in the other VI З., and the procedure for incision is such that you observe if the patient is moist, and the color of the material is white, moist, and has a fine root.
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	then cut it open with a wide spatula, and let the cautery be present.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;	For when you cut it open there is often a great gush of blood, and if the blood defeats you, then hasten to cauterize.
et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;	and if you see the patient terrified and fearful of the iron incision, then take some well-made hemp thread, and bind it around the wrist as we have said, leaving it there for two days.
et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;	then hold it tight, and do not stop tightening the hemp thread until you feel the wrist, and each part of it with no movement.
et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	and if the roots are thick, there is fear in cutting them especially for the belly, but you may well cut half of it, then cauterize so that it does not return.
puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	then treat the wound, and make sure you do not cut the tendon which is of a pale color and poor substance with a milky appearance.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	For this is an abscess exacerbated, and I will come to the treatment of cancer thereafter.
quant li boude ist fuer	When the boil bursts open.
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	If the swelling appears due to cauterization of a wound or a fissure caused by erysipelas, and it is located on the belly, affecting some of the bowels as happens with other ruptures, or from blood leaking from veins or arteries according to what has been described before, or from flatulence;
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	and if it is due to the rupture of erysipelas and the discharge from bowels, then the color of the abscess resembles that of flesh, and it feels as a light thing without pain, appearing with several discharges.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if it's due to the discharge of the intestines, then it is more varied, and when pressed with two fingers it retracts, then reappears, and perhaps it becomes clogged, greatly enlarging at the entrance of the bath and because of hard work.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	If it is due to moisture, it is a light thing, and it appears clearly when you press it with your hand, it does not constrict.
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	and if it is due to blood, it appears with these signs: large and hard abscesses, arranged according to a certain quantity.
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	And if it is due to windiness, it is soft to the touch, and the treatment is that you must observe whether its appearance is caused by arterial blood, venous blood, or windiness.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	You should leave the treatment to others.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	For there is doubt and fear in it, as I told you in the chapter on abscesses, for both artery and vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	And if the appearance is due to the intestine or hernia, you must instruct the patient to hold their breath and lie flat and still, then draw blood all around the affected area.
puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;	Then have them rest often between your hands, go around the marked place with all of your fingers, then extend half an inch above the entire big thumb.
puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	Then bind it around with a strong thread or firm rope of stout silk, ensuring the knot is secure.
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	Work on half of the abscess as it extends onto the ligament, insert your index finger there, and feel for the intestine.
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	If you find it caught by the ligament, free it, and push the intestine out of the abdomen;
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	And if you find an orifice, grasp it with the hook, and cut away any excess;
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	And if the artery or vein is in your way, go carefully around it, then return to your task and take two needles with fine thread, insert them twice, and put these two needles into what you have pierced in a cross pattern.
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	Then extract the abscess four fingers above these needles, and if you can see it, remove the needles, and let this area rot by itself as the dead flesh flakes off.
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	Where you cut it when it is subtle and rotten, then treat according to what is needed, and remove the abscess as we have said.
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	And remove the blood or moisture that you find, then treat the area accordingly, and seal/heal the wound.
dou chancre	The cancerous sore.
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;	We have spoken about the similarities of cancer in the previous section, and how it should be treated with medicine, and when one must avoid iron-based treatments.
et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;	And now we speak of cancer that has spread to the bone marrow and requires great caution in its treatment. The ancients say that when cancers are located where they can be scraped away like those found on mammary glands, thighs or similar areas, one must remove it entirely at its earliest stage.
et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;	and when it is large and old, you must not approach it, for I have never been able to heal anyone with such a condition;
ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	no one has ever healed it before me.

puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;	then make him bleed if he has obvious congestion, then prepare the patient in a good place to perform the operation;
puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;	then cut your oncology or cancerous growth, and shave his head from all sides, and remove it entirely without leaving anything behind;
et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	allow the blood to flow freely and drain it well with your hand or something solid, and if the bleeding flows contrary to the incision of the artery or vein, then cauterize until the bleeding stops;
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat with another treatment until it is healed.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:	We have already spoken about the different types of dropsy and how the accumulation of water is formed, as well as the signs for each type, and the treatment that can be done with medicine or with iron.
si est eclites soulement;	If it is only written down;
et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:	and one should not use iron in these two types of cases:
c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	that is to say, tympanites and hyposarcus, for these are mortal conditions;
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	Therefore, when you treat this type of dropsy called "eclites" with medicine, and the cure is not effective, consider if the patient is weak or has other ailments besides dropsy, such as constipation and digestive issues.
si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	If you use iron, do not touch there as there is doubt.

lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	Make the patient lie straight on your hands, and support them while pressing their belly by pushing water to the lowest part of the abdomen, then take the sharp-edged spathe like this:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And let there be two parts cut.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	It should be pointed but not so sharp that it can reach the intestine when inserted and cause injury.
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	Then check if the dropsy is directed towards the intestines:
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	So you must cut above the bump on the third right bone under the arm.
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	And if the dropsy is due to liver disease, let your incision be on the left side of the third right bump.
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	And if it is due to the spleen, let your incision be on the right side, and do not allow the patient to lie over the incision so that excess fluids do not flow to that weak spot.
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	Then pierce through the skin with your tool, push it in, and lift your hand to scoop out all the fatty tissue between the skin and fascia as if you were skinning something down to the size of a fingernail or so.
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	Then pierce the fascia until you reach the water spot, then pull it out, and insert this tool which is shaped like so.
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	And it is similar to a fine silver chain, and is made of light brass or copper, and has in its lower part a small aperture;
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	and on one side it is fitted with three holes;
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	and two on the other side, and one more;
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	and the tip is cut like a feather, and it is in the shape of the incision which scribes use to cut feathers:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	at the top is an axle, so that when the instruments come to the water, it immediately rises above the instrument;
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	empty it then by half or one-third part, for if you empty more than is appropriate at that time, perhaps the patient will die due to the release of their spirit from the body, or they may fall unconscious, or they will be close to death;
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	but empty according to its quantity of virtue, and according to what the conditions of the virtue of the patient signify, and his pulses;
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	then draw the instrument and retain the water, and it is retained now for the heart which blocks the orifice that I spoke of, so you pierce according to this method;
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	then begin the instrument again the next day if you see that he is suffering so, and draw a small quantity of water;
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	do this each day, and be careful not to draw out too much water but only a little.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	And if you are doubtful of the patient, and leave too much water, it will cool the heart or sand, and by excessive sweating or bathing in sun, and he will become dehydrated.

de l’estopement de la verge	From stopping of the penis.
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Sometimes children are born without an opening in the penis, or with a small one, or it is not in its place.

et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	And perhaps it is not necessary because the urine that flows out will keep the tube open.

Some men are born with their urinary opening at the top of the penis and thus cannot urinate without lifting it upwards.

des pustules de la verge	penis sores
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	This inflammation of the penis occurs many times, and it appears as an ugly redness.
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	And there are both malignant and benign ones.

de la circoncision	Of circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	circumcision is not like the separation of continuity as with other wounds;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	nevertheless, when we do this work of our own will, and especially to children, it is necessary that we perform the best work, and the most gentle for their well-being.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say the ancient ones did not circumcise their children because it was not in their law, and we have only acquired this practice through experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	for I have seen the majority of masters and surgeons performing circumcisions around one day old, with forceps, and all at once.

Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	Now if it were pierced again, the pain would be doubled, and during its removal, which is not done properly due to the depth of the member's point;

And during the removal of the nail, it might happen that the iron escapes, and the wound will spread, and often they heal in such a way that they do not need treatment; I have seen this myself.

Of the cleaning which is done by force on all that is tied in thread I have found the goodness of experiment; because the force cuts as well from above to below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	For when you press your hand down, cut evenly along the line of all that you hold tight;

Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The form of the forceps for cleaning is as follows:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	the two edges should be turned up and sharp, and the blades should also be as wide as the handles equally.

donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	Therefore, you must extend it with your nail, otherwise the flesh will form an abscess.

cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Treat it accordingly, as we have said, until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	where there is retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	Retention of urine is caused by obstruction of stones, or frozen blood, or a tumor, or similar things as we have said in the classification.
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	And if the urine is not released and you see that retention occurs due to a stone at the bottom or neck of the bladder, then the patient must be bent over their knees.

des maladies de la vessie	diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When scalds or blood enter the bladder, and putrefaction is gathered there, and you see it needs to be drained of water and medicine, do so with all the instrument which is called a "catheter", and its shape is thus:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It is closed, and it has three openings:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	Two on one side, and one on the other, as you see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	and the inner hairs by which the medicated plug is such that it blocks the urethra without addition, so that moisture can be drained, and pushed out when needed;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	and when you want to empty your medications into the bladder, put the head of the catheter into the moisture, and drain by pulling on it.
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	you will then be able to draw out the moisture with the catheter, and afterwards push it back firmly again;
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	If moisture enters here, it will go to the bladder immediately, so that the patient will feel it.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	And this is the subtle form of the enema used to cleanse the bladder;
si est ci:	If it is here:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	And it is made of silver or tin, with the head being higher up;
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	And it descends to the left side where the ribs end;
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	Then take a sheep's bladder and put the moisture you wish to use for the enema inside it, then tie it between the two breasts with a good thick thread, and heat the pouch over a fire;
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	then insert the head of the clyster into the urethra, then press your hand onto the bladder gently, until the patient feels that this moisture has reached the bladder.
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	and if you don't have a bladder, take a piece of parchment paper, make a circle out of it, and punch a round hole in the center.
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	then insert a strong thread through the hole, gather the circle together like you would with a funnel, and place within it whatever oil, moisture or water you desire, then tie this to the instrument.
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	and do like you did with the bladder, pressing gently by hand until the moisture reaches the bladder.
de la piere	of stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have spoken of the types of stones, their extraction, and accompanying remedies.
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	And we have explained the distinction between kidney stones and all other types of urinary calculi, along with their specific surgical procedures.
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	and in bladder and urethral stones;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	and we will describe them openly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that bladder stones occur more frequently in children, and this is signified by the urine escaping from the bladder akin to water due to its subtle nature;
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	and there is visible sand in the patient's urine, causing them to feel a burning sensation upon urination, which may occur multiple times before eventually ceasing;
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	And many of them have foundations sunk deep;
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	And the healing is light for children up until four years of age, and it is very difficult in old men, and it is moderate among young men, to those who are between youth and old age;
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	And the treatment is lighter for those who have large stones than for those with small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is necessary first to cleanse the patient with an enema, in order to remove all the bile that is in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For sometimes it becomes difficult to reach the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take the patient by their feet, lift them up and move them downwards, so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, sometimes coming out on its own.
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	Then have the patient sit between your prepared hands, with their hands placed behind their thighs, so that the bladder is completely lowered downwards.
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	Then search for it and touch it inside.
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	If you feel the stone in the space, then hurry now to cut into it.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if it does not fall upon touching all at once, then moisten your index finger with oil from the left hand if the patient is an infant, or your middle finger if they are a grown young person;
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	And push it into their fundament, search for the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, then cut at the neck of the bladder.
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	Then press down with your finger, and push the stone out from where you want to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	Instruct the assistant to press on the bladder with their hand and tell them to stretch out the testicles upwards with their right hand, while removing the skin that is beneath the testicles in the area where you will be cutting, using their left hand.
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	Then I inserted the spatula cutting, from which this is its shape:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And splitting what is between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but on the left side of the groin;
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	and be straight over the stone, and press your two fingers towards the anus or the foundation, and make the incision so that it is wide on the outside and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, but not too large;
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	by chance if the pressure on your two fingers at the anus is such that it would be without effort;
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	and you should know that there are stones with angles and edges;
si est griés a issir;	It must be drawn out gently;
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	and if it is shallow, resembling a hazelnut, round, with only a slight opening.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	On one where there are angles and margins, make the incision larger;
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	and if it does not come out, you must extract with tongs that are like a file at the end, to pull out the stone so that it doesn't escape.
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	or push aside the subtle instrument curved at the end.
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	and if you cannot manage it like this, then enlarge the wound opening, and if blood oozes out, cauterize with vitriol.
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	and if there is more than one stone, first push the largest one towards the neck of the bladder, then cut above it, then pull with force, and the smaller ones after that if there are several.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, one must take care of it, and make a larger wound.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For two things happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	where either he dies, or urine comes back through the wound that the flesh cannot seal;
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	but nevertheless try to pull it out, either by drawing or breaking with tongs, until you extract it in pieces;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	and when you have completed your work, fill the wound with incense, aloe, and dragon's blood, bind it tight, and place atop a cloth moistened with oil and wine, or with oil and rose water in cold water, to soothe the hot abscess;
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	Then resolve the patient onto their neck, and do not loosen the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you loosen the bindings, thoroughly wash the wound with oil and water, then treat it with ointment of daffodil and unguent of basilicon, until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if an abscess arises in the wound and bladder blockages with blood, and urine is retained which escapes together with the urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	So push your finger into the wound, and extract that blood, for if it remains, it will run into the bladder, and cause an infection;
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then cleanse the wound with water, oil, and silk, and treat him in all ways that you know until it is healed;
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And you must ensure that whenever you treat him, the two thighs are tied together, and gather your medical supplies accordingly.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if the stone is small, and it is lodged at the urethra's entrance, stuck there such that urine cannot pass through;
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	if the treatment I describe here fails, then you are justified in cutting it out multiple times.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have already proved this thus.
Pren I foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a III angles fichiees en I tison:	Take an iron rod, shaped according to this form, with three angled prongs at one end like a pitchfork:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	then take the thread and tie it around the penis below the stone so that it cannot retreat back into the bladder;
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	then gently insert the boring iron into the penis until it reaches the stone;
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	and turn the boring iron with your hand within the stone little by little until you are able to pierce through it from one side.
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	urine will come quickly; then press your hand over the remainder of the stone that is still inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	If it is immediately broken [the dislocation] and extracted with urine, then the patient will recover.
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	And if you cannot do this for any reason that prevents it, then tie one string below the stone and another above it, then make an incision towards the stone between the two strings, extract it with force, untie the string, and clean out the clotted blood from the wound.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Treat them until they heal.
de la piere des femmes	Of the stones of women
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	Sometimes stones occur in women, and if it happens once, then the treatment is severe, and it is prevented for three reasons.
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	One reason is that perhaps the woman is a virgin.
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	and the second is that you cannot find a woman who knows well how to uncover herself before mirrors, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	and the third way is that, by chance, you cannot find a woman who knows well this art of hands;
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	and the fourth way is that the stone of the woman is more perfect than the stone of a man, which requires a deeper cut, and there is great fear in it. If necessity arises for this, you must take an expert midwife, and if you barely find one, and if not, seek out no chaste subtle mirror;
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	and the present one is a wise midwife in women's lives or a woman who knows part of the art and instruct her to do what you command for the examination of the stone;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and carefully check if the woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	then you must insert your finger into her anus and search for the stone;
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and if you find it, pull the stone out from under your finger, and instruct her to insert her finger into her vagina, then grasp and press your left hand firmly over her bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	If she finds it, have her pull the stone out gently from the opening of the bladder down to just above the thigh root.
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	Strike the stone in the root of the thigh towards the middle of the vagina, where it moved to, and feel for the stone in that area.
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	and do not move his tooth above or below the stone, let the incision at first be small.
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	then pour the vinegar into the incision, if you feel the stone growing so that the wound increases until the stone can come out freely, and know that there are many kinds of stones.
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	that is to say, small and large, rough and soft, long and round, and those with furrows.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	If you know the symptoms, you can understand the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if the blood overtakes you, apply ground green vitriol to the place, and hold it for an hour until the bleeding stops.
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	then return to your task until the stone is out, and have the instruments I told you about for extracting stones from men, so that they may assist in your work.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	And if the blood defeats you and it is from an artery that has been cut, put powder on the spot along with tent and bandage cloth fibers, do not start again, leave the stone alone and do not pull it out because perhaps the patient would die.
puis cure la plaie.	Then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has subsided and the area can be accessed, return to your work until the stone is completely removed.
de hernie carnouse	Of fleshy hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	A watery mixture is nothing other than a collection of moisture or white liquid, which comes from under the heart of pigs and can be found inside eggs.
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	And it is called "syfac," and sometimes it appears properly in the egg's membrane so that one might think it was another egg.
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	And it is the pig's skin, which lies between the white liquid we mentioned earlier.
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	And this does not happen if you have no pus.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this rice water is due to weakness that comes to calves, and this matter is spread.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	And sometimes it comes from blows to the joints, and this moisture has many colours:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	where it is discoloured towards yellow, or it is without red, or black, or watery white, and this happens often;
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	and these are the signs to recognise this assembly, for if it is white and soft as we have said, then the abscess will be round, like an egg, with pus long in shape but not opening the joint, because there is moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in the very tissue, then it is an abscess which has retained part of the egg, and for this reason one thinks it is another kind of egg;
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	And if moisture is between the skin of the calves and the white sinew, one can feel it well.
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	Therefore, when you wish to know the colour of the moisture, test it with any object that fits as described above.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to that which follows after the introducer, judge what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	And when we treat it with iron, the patient must be bled according to their strength and the fullness of their body.
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	Then place them on their back, on something slightly elevated, and put beneath them a lot of cloth.
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	Then sit on their left side, and instruct the helper to sit on the right, and stretch out the leg towards one of two sides of the calf's heart.
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	then take the spatule knife, and cut the skin of the calves among them from the length up to the wrist, and let your incision be completely straight while separating the skin of the calves until you see white flesh, and carefully peel it according to your ability.
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	then pierce the white flesh with a water-filled tube through the wide opening, and extract all the water, then put your thumbs in place, and stretch the white flesh upwards.
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	and do not touch the heart of the calves, but only the white flesh;
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	cut all of it or in pieces especially the side of him carefully, for if you do not peel it well enough, water will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	And if the egg has been knocked from your work, put it back into place once you have completed the surgery of the sinew.
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then join the two lips of the wound in the heart of the swine with one suture, then treat it like any other wound until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	And if you find the egg corrupted by another illness, you must tie the suspending vessels to prevent blood loss.
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	Then cut the swine open along with its suspending structures and extract the egg, treating it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	And if the fluid is gathered in two parts together, know that these are two roots.
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	If you cauterize the other part just as you did the first one equally, then wipe off the blood, and place on the wound moist linen soaked in rose oil.
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	Place some other linen soaked in wine and oil above it, then put the two pieces of cloth on top, add doubled rags, and tie it all with bandage that is made like this.
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	Then take two cloths, and stuff them with wool like this example so they are sewn together at the waist of the pants, one piece goes under the buttocks up to the back, while the other goes on top towards the armpits.
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	And with the other two at the head on both sides, let it all be tied together in the buckle of the pants.
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	et sometimes this cauterization method is used instead of iron surgery, and you must take a subtle cautery knife, cut the skin on the testicles, heat it as we have said so that the white substance containing water is uncovered.
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	then take the cautery according to this form, and pierce that white substance with small pricks, flay it with this hot subtle cautery.
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	And cut it in every way you can, until everything is eradicated.
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	and ensure the fire does not touch the egg.
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	and know that this work is safer.
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	and be careful of blood loss, and learn from the works of surgery.
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	And if anything opposes you, whether an abscess hardens or blood flows elsewhere or any other matter, treat what opposes you as described above.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	And if the patient is afraid and does not want to undergo this procedure due to its horror, then induce perforation as I have told you, for when you are certain through the signs we mentioned that water-carrying branches are present, make the patient sit on a raised seat;
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	Then pierce the abscess from below with a spatulate object as wide as possible, and place the perforation along the length of the body.
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	And let the openings be wide so that all the water may flow out freely.
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	Afterward, place cotton on the spot and bind it, leaving room for the remaining water to flow, then treat until the wound is healed.
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;	And if the white cloth does not allow the water to drain into the mouth of the wound, then you must insert a feather or an instrument used to draw out water from edematous patients, which has this shape mentioned earlier.
et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	Widen the pouch of the wound, and know that the water will return, and it is re-assembled after six months or so, and when it is re-assembled as before, thus the patient will live through their days.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess on the buttocks
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that in the incision of this branch there is fear in many dispositions, which is why it seems better to me to leave it alone.
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	And I will tell you about the work and its similarities to an abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	I say therefore that many abscesses arise on the body, especially on the head.
et c’est par mout de cas.	And it is due to frequent occurrences.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	That is to say, by excessive acidity and bile which has spread to the head or through injury.
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	And the colour of the abscess is according to the colour of the body;
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	It does not cause any pain, yet it is an aggressive abscess.
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	And sometimes there are fearful, hard abscesses of dark colour which arise from the rupture of an artery or the swelling of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is due to an arterial rupture, it is recognised by the hot disposition of the abscess when you press it with your fingers.
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	And you must not touch it at all.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	Those who are subject to swollen veins are recognized by their reaction when the fingers touch them, and one can easily perform the operation on this resemblance as well as other parts.
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	And you cut the heart of the vein, then stretch out the egg above, and tear away the white substance, and remove all parts of the egg's suspension.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the egg is already hardened with these parts nested together, then you must pull out the egg and cut it.
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	And if it is hollow at the surface or inside the vessels, you must remove all of that membrane and cut it roundly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the birth of the flesh is at the back, you must cut it all away and remove the egg, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is completed, cover the wound with wet wool soaked in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other cures until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess on the buttocks
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	This is an abscess wrapped in a bandage resembling a turban, with the softening of the tendons, and the patient cries out terribly when it bursts.
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	And the cure for this disease is just as fearsome as the one before, yet we will tell you its treatment according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	You must have the patient sit on an elevated chair, then place the tendon suspension below your two hands, at all vessels that are near the artery, and hold them firmly while stretching it greatly.
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	Then cut through with a broad sharp spatula across the vessels until they are uncovered, and then peel back on either side as we have said before when extracting arteries from the temple.
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	Then I insert a needle where there is double thread, and tie it to the first place where the vein came out, and then tie it again to the other end.
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	Then cut them exactly in two, according to the length of the body, and remove the corrupted moisture.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	Then treat the wound like the others where we tie a bow, so that no vessel leaks and nourishes one of the clots.
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	Because from this there is no harm, and if all the vessels leak, then you must treat the clots in all the vessels.
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	So that the flesh does not lose its nourishment due to the incision of the vessels, dry out, and cannot be helped.
de la routure dou syfac	For rupture of the spleen
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The events of this chapter occur through the incision that leads to the abdomen or the extension on the stomach in the region of the intestines, which is why the intestines descend from that rupture towards one of the openings.
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	And this rupture is either from the incision or its extension, and these two types of ruptures occur due to many reasons:
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	or from blows, or jumping, or heavy lifting, or similar activities;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	And the signs that indicate an extension of the incision are a gradual appearance of symptoms over a long period and it does not occur suddenly;
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	And the abscess is equal in size up to the surface due to the incision pressing on the intestine.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs are when it's from the section of the spleen; there is sudden pain at first and different abscesses appear under the skin close by due to the intestine coming out of the body through the rupture in the spleen.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the intestines descend with the gut, and are held there, causing great pain to be endured by the patient, especially when they are pressured.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these iron treatments with fear, which is why it must be avoided.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the method of operation is that you instruct the patient to pull their intestine back into place with their hand inside the wound, if they are able to do so.
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	Then be mindful of his neck. Place your hands under his collarbone. Lift his thighs.
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	Then extend the heart upwards, and cut all the skin from the lower back to the length of the body.
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	Then push the lips of the anus inside with hooks according to how much you need to open the wound, and make sure that the esophagus can exit.
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	Then remove the fat that is under the skin of the lower back until all the white fatty tissue is exposed on all sides.
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	Then insert your index finger into the one that follows the coccyx, which is between the first sacral bone below the egg skin, and between the second sacral bone, and separate what is behind the egg, and between the second sacral bone.
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	And then move your right hand inside the hearts of the coccyxes, and stretch the first sacral bone upwards towards your left hand, and lift the egg toward all the sacral bones on the side.
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	Instruct the assistant to stretch the egg upwards, and untie what is below behind the binding.
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	And feel with your fingers for any coiled intestine or hard sacral bone, and if you find anything, push it towards the stomach below.
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	Then take a needle with one thick thread made of ten strands, and insert it into the posterior part of the sciatic nerve, which is behind the skin covering the buttocks;
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	After the waist, then cut away the flesh that appears to be made up of strands, until there are four threads remaining;
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	Then tie them together one over the other in a cross pattern, and bind the sciatic nerve, which we said is beneath the skin of the buttocks, with a strong two-part ligature;
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	Then wrap the flesh around the threads and bind it in a two-part fashion so that none of the vessels that nourish them can enter from outside, preventing any abscesses forming;
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	and place again the bandage according to the first long bandage with two fingers of that one, and after these two bands leave a gap below the heart of the calves as wide as a finger;
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	and after, do all of the other [round] movements according to the shape that the egg has;
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	then press in the area below the skin of the calves until blood flows into the bowels, as we have said before;
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	then bring moistened wool in oil, and put it on the wound; then apply the bandage as we have mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white flesh is cauterized as we have said, after the incision, due to fear of bleeding.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this often happens, and leave the bandage until it sticks by itself;
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	and if it delays to fall, let it be soaked in warm water, and apply what we have said earlier, until it falls off.
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	then treat the wound with another remedy, until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	Of fleshy hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch, I have never seen anyone who dared to do the operation with an iron tool.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is done like a spiral vine that wraps around a stick, in such a way that you tie vessels together, gently twisting them after cutting.
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	then cut it in half, and treat the abscess with what works, until the vessels fall away.
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	Sometimes rupture occurs in the groin, as we have said, and the testicles become visible.
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	And none of the intestines descend to the calves, but if they do, it is little, and repair every hour.
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	But nevertheless, if it stays too long in this position, the wound or ulcer grows so that the intestines descend.
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	And this happens due to the extension of the ulcer that is in the groin, as we have said, because it extends and softens, then swells and opens.
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	And the treatment is by cauterization, as we have said before.
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	And sometimes it is treated with iron in this way.
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	The patient often lies on their back between your hands, then scrape the area around the rupture swollen for about three fingers wide according to its size.
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	and then extract the synovial sac that is beneath the skin that covers it, then take some fat and place it on the spot where the sac was exposed.
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	press it perfectly against the abdomen, then cut the two visible spots of the synovial sac above the top of the fat, and cut one after another.
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	then extract the top of the fat, and do not cut any part of the synovial sac nor spread out its contents or anything else, as I have already instructed you in the treatment of intestinal prolapse.
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	then treat it by following the procedure for treating wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the sons, clean them and treat the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The sinew is restricted, and it has no appearance in the rupture, but cauterization is suitable here, and more proximate to healing.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	softening of the skin of the calves
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	The skin of the testicles often becomes soft in some men because the contents inside are softened, and this is evident to see.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	and it is necessary, when one wants to cure him, that the patient lies down on his back, and the surgeon cuts the skin that has softened above the natural skin.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	then sew the two lips together in one seam, and if you see any excess of the softened skin first cut it away to three seams or four firmly.
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	then cut between the seams, and treat it like other wounds until they are healed and the threads fall out.
dou chastrement	The castration.
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Know that cauterization is forbidden in our law, and for this reason I would rather not speak of it in this book.
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and it is only necessary for two methods.
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	One is that a doctor must know how to answer when asked, and he knows the treatment.
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	And the other reason is that we often need to castrate certain animals to assist us, such as goats, sheep, cattle, and others.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say, therefore, that castrations are performed in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	By either attraction or incision.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In the method we use by attraction, we make the animal sit in warm water until its testicles are softened and drooping;
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	Then grasp them with your hand until they are removed and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	For the castration of the testicles:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	It is necessary that you hold the animal and press its skin above the testicles with your left hand, then bind the belt, and cut each testicle with one stroke when you have properly scrotumed them.
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	leaving no place for the common surgeon nor the subtle surgeon who is over the vessels,
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	and this manner of castration is better than that which is done by attraction because with the latter some matter from the testicles might remain and thus the animal still desires lust.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	then treat the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	Des hermaphrodites: Of hermaphrodites, where one finds both male and female generative organs mixed together in an individual; this is caused by heat or cold in the womb during pregnancy.
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	A hermaphrodite is of two kinds among men,
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	The one is such that between the two testicles appears like a woman's genitalia in its natural form, where there may be hair, and sometimes it discharges urine.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other manner is found in women, appearing on the wrist like a rod and two knobs.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment of men and women is such that you remove all joined flesh, and treat it like any other wound.
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	In the second manner, for men whose urine spurts through the skin of the testicles, there is no treatment.
de la tentigene	For the sting.
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	Tetigoine is a joined flesh on the natural part, so long as it is too ugly to look at.
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	And some women have it also large like a hand, and that is the treatment.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	You must hold the excess flesh around the wound with your hand or pincers, and gently cut it.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	And do not go too deep, lest blood flow out, then treat with another treatment until it is healed.
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	And at another place where it arises in the mouth of the wound, and it fills, and perhaps bursts out, and is like a cow's udder in appearance, and so the ancients called it "udder disease".
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	You must cut it, as we have said with cauterization, and treat until it is healed.
de erratique	of wandering stones
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	Erratic it is when the woman's nature is not pierced or the opening is small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	And it is natural by birth, or accidental due to illness which has come about;
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	where it is attached by a clamp, or by a fine wire or spike, and it is firmly fixed in the marrow, be it on the side, below, or wherever.
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and prevent conception, childbirth, and perhaps even the flow of menstrual blood;
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	and knowledge of this is obtained through observation of the urine.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the obstructions are close by, take them out with your fingers or a rod.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is fixed with a fine wire, and it is close to the two cubits, then hurry up, and cut it thus:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	place your two index fingers together, and have the woman lie on her back with her legs spread;
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	then extend the two lips widely, so that the fine wire is exposed, and cover it with your fingers;
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	Then take wool, dampen it in oil, and place it on the spot, and have the woman lie with her husband every day, so that it does not heal.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the suture is hard and thick, you should cut it with a spatule similar to a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the obstruction is made of unworked wood, suspend it from an oak branch and split it;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	And have ready the hemostatic medicines, as needed, such as dragon's blood, incense, along with egg whites;
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	Then bring a broad hollow cane so that the wound cannot heal;
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	And thus it shall be for a long time, and bring him a dry linen tent;
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat other treatments until he is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when there is a newborn child in the womb, it must be delivered in this manner, unless there are encrusted abscesses.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For an encrusted abscess in the womb, one should not apply cauterization.
des emorroides	Hemorrhoids.
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins without a usual cortex, and when hemorrhoids are old they become thick.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	And we have already mentioned in the division their similarities with others, and the signs, now I will say which ones receive treatment.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and hardness, when they are deep in the anus and cannot be felt, should not be treated with cauterization.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those who are at the mouth of the swamp, where one can feel it, are those whom one can cure.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	You should thus place the woman in a cold house, then stretch out the hemorrhoid with forceps, and cut it at its root, then powder over it with medicines that restrain blood flow, such as dragon's blood and incense, and similar things.
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	Then press her feet against the wall for an hour, then place them in cold water.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	And if blood flows from it, have her sit in a decoction of sumac, pomegranate rind, gallnuts and similar things; then take barley flour, mix it with honey and egg white to make an ointment which you place on her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if there is no bleeding, that's good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If not, have him apply cups to his back and breasts without piercing them.
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	Then take linen, soak it in plantain juice or hawthorn juice with old wine, and apply to the affected area.
