Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess subsides, treat the area with ointment until it is healed.
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	And the one called "albathir" is red, resembling rough skin, it should be cut like the telul, as I mentioned.
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	Abscesses of the breast.
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many types of abscesses occur in the breast, such as cancer, stony abscesses, herpes, tumors, fistulas, hemorrhoids, hot abscesses, and various other diseases that I have mentioned in my classification.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	Therefore, I must discuss in this treatise the hot abscess that appears on the vulva, which is not one of the abscesses that are meant to burst.
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	And if you wish to know the work of iron [i.e., surgery], then look whether the abscess is acute at the beginning of its appearance, and full of heat and fever, and if it becomes red when you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Then do not hasten to pierce [it], but let it die until the pain is eased.
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	And then make the patient sit on a seat, and have two small seats for him to lean on, supporting his back and bringing together the parts outside of the leg.
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	And let his thighs be spread apart, and place his arms underneath his knees, and bind them well with a good bandage.
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	Then suction from his right side, and introduce the instrument with which you work the mouth of the marrow, from which afterwards the matter comes.
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	and it is necessary that when you go to introduce this instrument, that you insert the point first in order to know the depth of the wound, so that what enters inside with the instrument does not go further than it should and does not harm the patient.
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	and if the instrument is larger, one should cover the depth of the wound with cloth so that the instrument does not harm him.
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	and it is necessary that he put the handle of the instrument on top and hold the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when the abscess opens up, and it is softened by hand, one should cut it at its head with a spatula.
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	And when the bowels are empty, you should place moistened dressings in rose oil or dry green oil into the wound.
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	place the dry dressing outside of the wound over the cavity, and put over the cavity and the hand clean moist wool that has been boiled with mallows.
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat it after two days of dressing, until it is healed.
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	and sometimes you should rinse the cavity and wound with an enema of water and honey, then with water or boiled roots of lily and long aristoloche.
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	then return to the dressing.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	If the wound is swollen in the scab, you must avoid cauterizing with iron but treat it as we have mentioned previously.
de l’enfantement	Of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	Mestier est premier a la baile qu'elle conoisse la figure de l'enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l'ar: 
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	then hasten the child to go out (of the womb).
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	then know that these births are according to the natural position, and the baby comes out headfirst, with the second twin following.
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	and when you see these signs, it is necessary to gently press on her belly so that the baby comes out soon.
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	for when it descends headfirst, so does the twin with him, and the mother's excesses are cleansed through proper childbirth.
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	and this one who comes out differently is not born naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For sometimes it comes out on its feet, or the body or shoulder first, and hands, or on its belly, often, and occasionally turned onto its neck, and in other bad positions.
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	If it is necessary for the nurse to be wise and skilled in these matters, and beware of errors and deception, I will show you all the ways in which she must assist him.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the child comes out feet-first naturally, and the woman gives birth painfully, and her strength is weak, have the midwife sit on a stool, where other women hold her.
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	And mix her nourishment with cooked olive oil or fenugreek, then put the nurse between her two hands using the small spatula which is shaped like this: [shape description]
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	And break the amniotic sac, and scoop out its nail so that all of the moisture that is within flows out.
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	And press the woman's belly so that the child descends, and if it does not descend, then you must give the woman an enema made of ground fenugreek with sesame oil.
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	Then make her sneeze with juice of rue, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour.
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	Now press the child's belly.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if both hands pop out, you must gently push them back in turn.
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	And if they cannot go in, place the woman on a chair, lifting her feet upwards.
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	Then get up the chair from the ground, holding onto the woman so she does not fall when standing up.
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	And if the hands cannot go in and the child is dead, cut her hands with a knife as mentioned before, extract the child, and push it back evenly.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	Of the child's birth upon its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child begins to walk, you must push them upwards.
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	And then turn it over gently, until it is even.
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	Then take one foot and stretch it gently, again and again.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	When they jump up to the hips, instruct them to grab hold, and make them sneeze vigorously.
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	If it jumps, so be it, if God wills it.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it does not go beyond as we have said, turn it over and over until it is according to the natural shape.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it is lightly done.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it does not come about as we have done, say one must take muskroot from the pharmacy, and sesame oil, and molten gum, and grind everything in a mortar.
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and apply this ointment to her female nature, then have her sit in warm water up to below the ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when she is moistened below, make her a collar of myrrh, and place it underneath, leaving it for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then have her sit on the chair, make her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose, gently press on her belly, for the baby is jumping now.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	From the birth of the child upon its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the baby comes in this manner, put balm on its hands back and forth;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	then be mindful of her neck, let her feet hang down, and have her lie on the bed;
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and she bends her hands back and forth, then he presses her hands onto the stomach, and removes the cushions underneath, until she is properly aligned below.
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the child does not jump, take her feet and move them vigorously, then massage the stomach upwards, finally put in your hands.
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and shake the child back and forth;
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and instruct the woman to hold herself so that the child comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	From the birth of the child with one hand hanging out
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	I must devise a way to bring back the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if one cannot retrieve it, make the woman get up and walk.
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	if she cannot walk, have her lie down on the bed, and lift her legs vigorously;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	Then bring forth the musk concoction I have described.
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	And if she does not give birth, make her sit on the chair, then carefully help to bring back her hand.
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	Also guide the child according to its natural position, make her sneeze, and instruct her to grasp [the child] until the baby is out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	From the exit of the child upon its neck, and have its hands spread out, and its face turned towards the back of its mother.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	It is necessary for the midwife to hold her hand, then turn it back and forth, and lift [the baby] gently.
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	And when it is equalized, place upon [the baby] the natural musk concoction with oil, as we have said, then instruct her to move a little bit at a time.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	and when you have done this, make her sit on a seat, and instruct her to hold still.
et la fai esternuer.	and make her sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in the same manner for all secondary dislocations
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes out forcefully in this manner every time, cut the phlegm with your nail until all moisture is drained.
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the child spits on their face and neck, wipe it away from the root so that nothing is left behind, and clean the child.
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then push the child inside until you have positioned it correctly, and tell the woman to hold still once.
adonques si istra legierement.	now gently pull out the legs.
de l’issue des gemelz	Of a dislocated ankle joint.
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII; 
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	And this is not a strange thing, and often happens.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Two things are strange indeed, yet they exist.
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know them, though they multiply, divided by the surgeon's knife, bound to sorrow.
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	And sometimes they arise naturally as we have stated.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	If they arise severely, treat as we have said, with a skilled surgeon acting swiftly and gently.
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	And act so that it moves towards salvation.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Sometimes they are formed in the month of I or II or III or IV or V or VI or VII, and even up to XV, all shaped as children by the wondrous flow of blood, and it is essential that the surgeon knows all this, for such things may befall him.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	si do as is required.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat a woman for a dead child in her womb, as I have mentioned before, and it does not come out naturally, and you are forced to perform manual labor;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	you should know if the woman is of sound virtue and has no accidents or fears of death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	the woman should be supine on her back, with her head tilted downwards, and her legs lifted;
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the minister should hold her in two parts, or tie her to the bed so she cannot move during the extraction of the child;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	then rub the woman's mouth with moist oils mixed with a poultice of althea and fenugreek seeds, then anoint her hands with these oils and poultices;
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	Then place them in the mild bath, then position it where they put the weights so that they are suitable for this, and be careful if the child is fitted with one so that he does not fall on his head.
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	If you insert the weights in their eyes or neck or mouth or palate or under the beard or armpit or near the ribs, and if he falls onto his feet, then pierce him with it or hold it to his lower ribs.
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	And it is necessary that he hold the weight in his right hand and place the basket between two fingers of his left hand, and put all this into his hand gently, then insert the weight into any one of these places we have said until its contents come out.
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	And this is the form of oncine (swelling):
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	Then insert it against another oncine (swelling), or the third if you require more, so that the extractions are equal;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	And then stretch them evenly from one side to the other, so they can be removed, and let the oncines (swellings) interlock to keep them in place, like this is the form:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	If any part remains, anoint the wound with some of your fingers' oil, and press those into that part, and pull on the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	And if nothing remains there, place this oncine (swelling) higher up, and do so until it comes out entirely.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes before the other, and he cannot move it due to stiffness, you must wrap it in a cloth until it is entirely covered.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	Then cover the knuckles of the sole or heel, and do likewise for the other hand and both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the child's head is large and it becomes stuck during delivery, or if there is an acute assembly of membranes around its head, you must press the pointed spatula between your fingers, split open the membranes, and extract the fluid.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	Or you may use an instrument called 'almidach', the construction of which is described in the following chapter along with other instruments.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	And do the same if the child has an abnormally large head naturally.
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	then extract the bones with tongs, and if the head pops out and is held by forceps, let it be split open so that the moisture which is inside comes out.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it cannot come out, cut it into pieces as much as you can.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if it is swollen in the belly or under the ribs, you must pierce it so that the moisture flows out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the child is on his feet, the attraction is light, and the guidance to the mother's breast is easy.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is trapped in the belly or the head, you must extract it with fabric wrapped around the hand.
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and split open the belly or the head so that the moisture inside flows out.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if the other limb is removed, and the head remains, then insert your hand into the shoulder socket perfectly, and draw it down to the mouth of the socket;
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	then insert two or three fingers, and withdraw them gently;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the mouth of the socket is narrowed due to abscess which has occurred there, it should not be operated on, but moist and oily things must be applied;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	he applies poultices, along with warm softening and moistening agents dissolved in water.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is lying on its side, and you are able to put it upright, then apply what we have said about living children;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	If one has no power over it, then break it into pieces, leaving nothing of the sinew behind.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, if it brings on the hot abscesses we spoke of that come from the marsh;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	And if there is an outflow of blood, it should be dressed with cold water compresses restraining the flow, and other treatments should be administered.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whose belly a child had died; then another formed on top of it, and this one also died.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess formed in the buttock; it swelled until it opened and began to produce a great deal of pus.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to treat [the wound], and I thought about it for a long time, but could not heal/close the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a plaster of strong attraction, and an [the first] bone came out, and after some days another one did too.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was greatly astonished as there is no bone in the belly.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	So I thought it must be bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I cauterized the wound, and extracted pieces of bone from it, such that the woman was in a better state.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	And for a long time the woman dressed it thus, and only now does there seem to be a little lump in its place;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	And I have not written this chapter except to aid those who, when they find a strange case, might know how to help it.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	To return the marrow to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Ci après vient le forme du pressoir, à quoi on a les livrés.
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	Et à deux tours aux deux têtes des deux liens.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	However, the horns should be more subtle than those of the restrainer, and they should be made of ebony or boxwood.
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	And the mouth of the post should be two fingers wide, and the edge of the wood one finger thick, and its length a palm and half.
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	And in the middle of the two bindings there should be two fittings made from this same wood, firmly attached to each other, half a palm long or slightly longer.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	And these two fittings should be inserted into the mouth of the post to open when one turns the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter in appearance, should be made of ebony or boxwood, resembling the shape of a pair of tongs;
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and it should have two jaws, as you see, one palm in length, and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you see to open the womb with all the instruments, have the woman sit on the bed, her feet hanging and legs spread, then insert the two jaws of the instrument together into the womb, and hold the head of the instrument below between her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then operate your hand with the instrument, just as you would with tongs evenly, according to the extent that you see fit to open the mouth of the womb, so that she may do what she wishes.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	Cist estrument sunt tuit sormontez, 
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	And when the physician has prepared them, it is all the more urgent to operate on them, and it is of higher importance for men according to their condition.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not despair if you do not have the instrument ready, for its necessity is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the midwife is hindered during childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold her breath and then make her sneeze with conviction; bind your hands over her mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she faints from this, it is good.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, take a pot and pierce it where the cover is, and place herbs that can open the mouth of the sufferer gently inside, such as valerian, wormwood, anise, chamomile, cassia-lignea and centaury.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	All these herbs, or some of them, should be boiled in the pot with water over a fire.
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	Then put a cane or tube from the pot, and place the other end in the mouth of the patient, and hold it so that the vapors enter into the patient's mouth.
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	Then make them sneeze, as we have said before.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the assistant runs out of medicine.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if it remains after this treatment and does not leave, instruct the nurse to wet her left hand with oil of sesame or muskroot infusion, then place it on the affected area, and call for the midwife.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	Once she has found it, have her grasp it gently but firmly, ensuring the patient does not twist during the extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	But she should move it slightly to the right and left, and then pull gently.
si venra et se desaerdra.	Will come and will dislodge itself.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the wound is narrow, we have mentioned the treatment of coughing and herbal fumigations;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it does not work with all that we have said, be careful not to go astray when extracting (the humors).
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary that he who is at the mouth of the wound should tie himself to the thigh of the woman and then cleanse her with ointment made from four ingredients.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	it will heal and reset (itself), and come back strongly.
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	but nevertheless, when it heals, if foul-smelling wind comes to the stomach and head, it will afflict the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	So suitable fumigations are required for this:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	None of the ancients have tried fumigation with watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the instrument with which one fumigates a woman to retain her flowers and menstruation is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it should be similar to that of a dog, with the head placed above the fire in such a way as to allow for careful observation.
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	And the fumigation should be over the coals, letting the fabric smolder until it is completely consumed, then start another one.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the fundament.
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born without the anus being pierced, instead having it blocked by some delicate membrane.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	So at the bath, she should pierce this membrane with her fingernail, and not use a sharp spatula, taking care that it does not touch the surrounding area.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then place on it wet linen soaked in wine and oil, then treat with ointment until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will heal, insert a piece of lead wire into the hole, leave it for several days, and remove it when the child wants to go outdoors.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes this blockage occurs suddenly in wounds or abscesses;
si covient coper celui soudement:	Thus it is necessary to cut into that blockage:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	Then treat as cured, just as we have said about the case of the tongue.
de la fistule dou fondement	On the subject of anal fistulas.
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come from under the anus are suppurations, and swellings that come from around the anus outside, or in the space between the two parts, whether there is one fistula or multiple.
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	And when this suppuration is old, it should be worked on, and still moist with white or subtle bowels, and sometimes these fistulas are penetrating.
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And it is known to those who have experienced this through evacuation or flatulence when the patient evacuates, and perhaps a worm jumps out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And if there are fistulas that perforate up to the bladder, and up to half of the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and reach up to the hip joint, and up to the knee bone.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one recognizes a fistula that perforates the anus, but not through it:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and it is that you insert your index finger into the anus, and carefully push a thin needle of iron or steel into the fistula if there is no curvature.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it is twisted, insert a slender probe or horsehair until you feel the probe or hair with your finger.
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	if you cannot feel it, nor does air or wind escape from any opening as we have mentioned:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	know that it has not pierced;
si te haste dou curer.	hurry to treat it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula has perforated up to the bladder or up to the urine duct, it allows urine to escape, and cannot be healed by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If the probe has pierced down to the hip joint, then it is positioned correctly.
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is no twisting and the pain is around that area, then it indicates a bowed condition, and neither medication nor immediate dressing will help.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	And for these fistulas, there is no cure but to work on them, and the foolish pride of surgeons who involve themselves with it.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In that which is not perforated and is not ancient, there is hope for healing with iron, as I have experienced, and the patient lies between your hands on their back;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	And lift their legs up to the thighs, and have their thighs bent towards their belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then insert an iron probe, or brass if there is curvature, until you know where the probe enters.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels it around the anus, you must insert your index finger, and then feel that the probe has pierced [the fistula];
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	And if you feel a gap between your finger and the bone or flesh, then know that it is pierced.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If you do not exert pressure there, one cannot heal it.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	One says that they can be healed well sometimes, but this rarely happens.
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	And the assistance provided is to heat the subtle cautery according to the width of the fistula, as previously stated.
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	Then push it fully heated into the fistula until it reaches its base.
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	Do this twice or three times until you know that these faulty flesh bits are burnt, which resemble a bird's feather.
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then treat wet wounds with butter until all moisture disappears; afterwards treating them with an ointment that coats and heals the skin.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If he is thus healed, it is good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this wound cannot be healed in any other way;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the wound is inside and does not reach down to the bone that lies at its base, but rather there is between your finger and the wound a thick covering of flesh or sinew, and you see the fistula in what remains of this covering over the core;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	cut away from the beginning of the fistula and push back before the wound, then you may cauterize after so that it reaches to the head of the wound.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and the wound will be released and fall out.
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	Then beware of these flawed flesh wounds which appear like a bird's feather, and leave nothing behind.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the blood defeats you, flowing between your thumb and the incision, then cauterize with fire or medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cautery brings together two good things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	that is to say, the burning of these joined flesh wounds, and the stemming of blood flow and drying of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then treat the wet wounds with butter or crushed matter until the skin turns pale and the burnt flesh falls in the pallor.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat the wound of suppurating ingrown toenails with hardening dry medications.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if the fistula comes up to the anus, and is far from the body, put your finger in the anus and feel it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the wound, and between two is the membrane or the skin or flesh where it is about to break, then have no fear that can be seen as a sign of hope and trust through one of these three ways:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	where you cauterize it as we have said, or cut it down to the bottom, or if you can treat it with tents and heal it as initially intended.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deep, so as to avoid cutting the membrane that holds the foundation, and it results in involuntary evacuation of feces.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then heal it, as we have said.
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	perhaps it will be cleansed, or you can remove this covering and clean it after being cut near the foundation with a tent or another pointed instrument.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then remove this faulty flesh which is in the wound as much as you can.
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	Study to restore the wound, and stop the fistula from forming outside of the anus.
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	If it were less serious for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And sometimes their fistulas form in this way:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and it is when you insert a tent into the fistula, and it is situated by the anus near the skin above, take a perforated tent according to this form:
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	...and insert the curved wire into it in such a way that the probe follows this path.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is penetrating the edge of the anus inside, then remove the thread from that perforation, like you would insert your finger into the anus;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	And draw the head of the thread, and join the two ends together, holding them tight to each other, and leave it for one or two days.
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	And restrain it at times so the son cuts off its limbs which are between them, and they fall.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	Then treat the wound until it is healed and healthy.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not rupture, make it burst in every way you can, unless it is too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not suitable to operate on if too deep, then treat it as we have said until it heals.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the sharp-spined spatula that is used to make a fistula is very thin on one side and piercingly sharp.
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	And on the other side it is not sharp, so as to avoid cutting what should not be cut; as you can see here.
des emorroydes	Of hemorrhoids.
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Hemorrhoids occur in two ways:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	When they are inside the anus, like grains of resin, and there may be small or large ones, with some bleeding from them, and there may be one or many, these protrude outside the anus and at its head.
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	but those which are outside have little moisture, and even now or a little citron water or a little blood, and they have the body's colour;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and the treatment for those who have them inside the fundament is that you instruct the patient to strain themselves to go into chambers, until the fundament leaves them outside, and the worms appear.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	if you rush, and grasp it with the pincers or hold it with your nail, then cut it at its roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the pincers cannot hold them due to their moisture, take them with a cloth, or cotton, or a piece of chamois.
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and extract them with your fingers, then cut them, and apply some hot powders on them in place of cauterization.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	Where you cauterize them as it is said in the chapter on cautery, then treat other treatments until they are healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	And if the foundation cannot come out, administer to the patient a biting and harsh enema to wash what is in the fundament, so that it can be expelled clearly.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	When patients complain of pain, and if the filament is far from the foundation, then the treatment is easy.
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	You take them with your nail or pliers and cut off the filament, then treat it as we have said until it is healed without requiring an incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	It is necessary that you administer the suture in this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	Take a twisted thread, and push it into a needle, then draw the thread through and pierce the needle from the other side, turn the two ends of the thread under the needle, and let it be wide.
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	Tighten the thread firmly, then tie a knot in it, remove the needle, and do this for all others, leaving one to drain any excess blood.
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place on the base a damp cloth soaked in rose oil or wax, and put it on the base, instructing the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Leave it there until they subside, and once they do, treat them with ointment and other remedies until the area is healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	dryness of feces or fundament
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times there is constipation of feces in the intestine, and due to the constraint of nature, and when the illness is old and medicine is ineffective.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	You must cut away at the point of a spatule or with your nail the bark above it, so that it does not become damp.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	then treat it until it is firm as it should be;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it cannot heal, then start the scraping again more vigorously than before, until it bleeds a lot and is raw;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it until it is healed.
dou fremit	where there is trembling
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	A formix is a small faulty appearance between the body, and goes deep into the skin;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	and sometimes it strikes cold, and one feels it like a shivering death, and it spreads throughout the body, especially in the hands more than other parts.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is such that you take a quill from a goose feather, or a strong vulture feather, and place this quill on the trembling, so that the purple circles touch the trembling all around.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand around the entire quill so that you grasp it all around the trembling, and place it perfectly, and eradicate the trembling from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you wish, make this with a cane of brass or iron according to this form, and let it be hollow underneath and flat on top.
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	Do not pierce [the skin], for you must hold it with your fingers, and apply pressure.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you see fit, cauterize the trembling, as it is explained in the previous chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the enema form.
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Sometimes one uses silver, or melted lead alloy for the cautery.
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	And sometimes one makes these small and large instruments according to their intended use.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those that are used in the treatment of children and for those who are weak and ailing are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The shape of the enema instrument is broad at one end, where the belly is tied in this way:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	And if there is a separation where the belly is tied, as you see, and the intestine is pierced inside;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	And it has two openings on one side, and only one on the other.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	And let the belly or container for medicines be made from an animal bladder or parchment, pierced all around with small openings, and have one inch between each opening. Then insert into these openings a strong thread of twisted gut formed in the shape of an X or woven around it, and assemble the belly as you would a goat.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	And when the medicine is inside, tie it to an instrument with a strong thread in front, then administer as a clyster.
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and this is the form of the circle
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	and let the medicament not be too hot nor too cold, and grease the head of the clyster with oil or egg white, or something similar, then insert it gently;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	then the ministers squeeze it with both hands together until it is completely empty, then remove the clyster, and have the patient lift their legs to the wall, and if the medicament wants to exit, hold it as long as possible;
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if he sleeps for an entire night after, it is even greater help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you catheterize for a bellyache, and the medicament wants to exit quickly, so redo it until he is cleansed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	And if the haemorrhoids are on the anus or there is an abscess, let the clyster be as gentle as for a child.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	And this is the subtle form of the enema, on which the skin is held taut:
des plaies	wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have already spoken about the treatment of wounds in the classification [or division];
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	and now we will tell you the treatments with your hands and medicines, according to their completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to how they are inflicted, and where the wounds are located, as well as what has caused them.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things by which wounds are made are by stone-throwing, and the cuts of a sword or knife, or of a lance or stick or arrow, or similar things;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or they are made according to the location of the body, such as a wound that falls on the neck, or the head, or the foot, or the belly, or the liver, and similar parts;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	And I will tell you the treatment for each wound, starting with simple head wounds, since they will be remembered in their own chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	I say that when a simple wound occurs on the head, and the bone is not broken, take note if it's due to hitting a stone or similar objects, and the skin is still torn, and the wound is large; you slightly suspect of an abscess forming hot.
si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	Make it bleed just a little from the superficial temporal artery especially if there is very little blood coming out of the wound, and let the bleeding be on the opposite side of where the impact occurred.
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	And purge the patient of fullness from wine and fatty meats.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he does not wish to bleed, his flesh should be reduced, and let him drink no wine nor eat any meat.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	and place upon the wound, if warm abscesses come forth, cotton moistened in rose oil only or in styptic wine;
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	and if there is no warm abscess, place upon the wound, if it is fresh and full of blood, and not moved by the air, a powder which I will describe shortly.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if the air has moved it, apply some ointments until it is healed.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large like that of a sword cut or similar, and the lips cannot be brought together with sutures, then they should be joined by stitching, as I will explain for wounds in the abdomen, specifically about stitching.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope;	If the wound is exposed to the bone, gaping open, and only held together by a little skin, then cut it off.
puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir, et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	Then treat the wound with medicine, restore hard flesh in place of leather, and instruct the patient to eat coarse meats like boiled beef, wheat, cooked pork, chicken, and similar foods.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find skin with corruption that has not reached the bone, carefully cut away all the corrupted tissue, and discard it; then treat it.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is an artery in the wound or vein that does not stop bleeding and cannot be stanched with medicine, remove the artery; if you find it severed, tie it up with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if this does not help, then cauterize it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere:	And if these wounds are small and simple, the treatment is light:
et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	and ensure you add this powder which binds, as soon as the flesh has healed.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est:	and the type of powder is as follows:
pren encens une partie;	take one part incense;
sanc de dragon II parties;	dragon's blood, two parts;
chalz vive III parties, et le poudre subtilment, et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	galangal root, three parts, and finely ground powder, apply to the wound, holding it firmly until it dries well and joins with all its blood;
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle;	then bind it tightly, and leave it bound without loosening, if there is no swelling;
car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	for the medicine is not removed until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And sometimes one uses only quicklime powder when they do not have incense or dragon's blood, but the cold has moved away from the wound.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the burn has moved away from the wound, especially during summer, then do not put this powder on it.
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but apply some digestive ointments, or poultices made of barley flour with water and honey, until it becomes soft.
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if the bone fracture accompanies the wound, and it is minor, extract it with delicate pincers;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and I will tell you about skull fractures later.
de la plaie dou col	On the neck wound:
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If the wound is on the neck and it is straightforward, there is no significant distinction between this and a head wound; however, if the carotid artery or other arteries in the neck are severed.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is the black part, there are no other means than to leave it untreated, and do not apply any constrictive measures, for it harms the bone and causes it to retreat.
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	And do not place anything cold on the wound, for the nature of nerves is cold, and their continuity extends to the brain, which is the highest organ.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce, et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	but let the medicine be warm, just like heat washed in lukewarm water, and mixed with rose oil, and wax also washed in lukewarm water, and other minerals according to this method, and moist salves.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, cut it open and bind with bandages; then treat it until it heals.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and hairy, and filled with worms, pierce them below that level;
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	and if the artery is severed, and bleeding ensues, uncover it, scrape it, and cauterize it if necessary.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va, si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	and if the windpipe of the throat is severed, or the heart, and the conduit remains intact, by which breathing continues, cut into the heart above the trachea in the neck, but do not touch the throat itself, only restore it to its natural shape.
et puis l’estraint avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then hold it firmly in place, and leave it for a few days, then treat it with draining ointments until it is healed.
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	And if the wound has penetrated to the bone, then probe it.
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse, et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	If there are fragments of bone in the wound, pull them out forcefully if you can, and for those that cannot be removed, leave it to become putrid, and let the discharge be eased and alleviated.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	And if the wound is fresh, sprinkle on it the powder I mentioned.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound and it has formed a fistula, treat it as I have described in its respective chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	Of the wound caused by a spear or knife.
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne:	If it is a blow from a lance or knife, and the wound is deep, observe whether there is any windiness coming from the wound when the patient walks.
saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	Know then that the wound is mortal;
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont, et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	And if it is not deep, and fresh with all its blood, do not apply the powder in the first hour, nor bind it to stop the blood from flowing out, and returning to the heart, which would kill the patient;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie II fois le jor;	But put on an attractive ointment, and bind it twice a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor, et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie III jors, ou IIII, ou plusors;	And if you have no ointment, put old cotton into the wound to draw out the moisture, and make the patient sleep on the wound for three days, or four, or more;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’estraingnemens d’alainne;	Then there will be no spasm, nor bad heart tremors or strange breathings;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	And when you see favorable signs, know that the wound is healed.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Treat it then with bandages and other dressings until it is fully healed;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule;	And if it fails to heal, and there is continued discharge, then know that it has developed a fistula;
si la cure si com on doit.	Treat it as one should.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or knife incision, whether on the chest, arm, or back, treat what is visible first.
s’elle est grans, de cousture;	If it is large, suture it.
et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	And if it is small, use powder. If the wound penetrates deep into the bone and has splintered pieces, clean the wound, and realign the sharp ends of broken bones if they are disjointed.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	and if they are not removed, let the wound rot, it will ease the extraction.
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	and for wounds on other body parts, the treatment is as we have said before.
dou derrompement dou ventre	Rupture of the abdomen.
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The ruptures of the belly are large, medium, and small;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	From the large wound, sometimes the intestines or the nerves of the intestines protrude, which requires the insertion of other objects.
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans, por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	And the suturing is more difficult, and sometimes the small wound is worse than the large one, because it requires more precise placement of the intestines, which must be done carefully.
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes, et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres II.	Because the intestines swell when they feel cold, making them harder to place precisely, and for this reason, the medium-sized wound is better, as it allows for easier repositioning of the intestine to its correct location than other sizes.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc IIII manieres:	And know that the rupture of the belly is according to four manners:
les II costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre, et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et II autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	The two common sutures occur in the suture of the belly, and the suture of other wounds of the body, and there are two other specific sutures that are common to other wounds.
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	However, they are more specific when it comes to the suture of the belly, and I shall describe each one and provide clarification.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer, et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des II manieres:	I say that when the wound is small, and a part of the intestine lies outside, and it is easy to replace, it can be done through one of two ways:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit, ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	Or because of the small size of the wound, as we have said, or due to the intestine being swollen from the cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, heat it this way:
moillie une esponge ou I mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement, ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique, et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	Moisten a sponge or soft cloth in lukewarm water only, which you have boiled in sharp vinegar and cypress, and apply it to the intestine until the swelling is gone;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	And sometimes make this restraining wine, and it has been proven to help with swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites, car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	And when you see the swelling subside, moisten the intestine with water or other liquids in which mallow and elderflowers have been boiled, for through this, entry is eased to little things;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	And if nothing can enter, make a small hole in the wound with the instrument used to cut hemorrhoids;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille, que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	and the first treatment is to cauterize the area around the wound, one must not cut it unless there is great need for doing so;
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	and these are the instruments to split or open it:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	if you cut inside at an angle and outwards, and see this form:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer, si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre, se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	And when the wound is enlarged, and the intestines have burst out, so replace them dry according to their natural form in their proper place if you can, for it is worth trying.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre, si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	When the wound is wide and located below the abdomen, you should make the patient lie on their back and raise their legs higher than their head.
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre, si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz, et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des II parties si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	and if it is located below the belly, place the head and chest higher than the lower parts; also, if the abdominal rupture is in one of the two halves, position them so that the wounded part is higher than the other.
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	And thus you must manage what I say for large wounds and small ones.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet, puis aies entre tes mains I ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main, et assemble les levres;	For small wounds use what is available to you, then with your hands administer merciful medicine that holds the entire wound together, and join its lips.
et c’est la maniere commune de costures, et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie, puis laisse des le chief de la plaie I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait I boin fil fort;	And this is the common method of sutures, and it is that you take a needle or several, according to the quantity of the wound's width, then leave two inches from the head of the wound, and there insert a needle with good strong thread.
et perce les II chiés dou cuir avec les II chiés dou siphac, qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie, et assemble les II chief dou siphac les IIII ensamble;	And pierce the two sides of the skin with the two sides of the siphac, which is beneath the skin inside, so that you make it pierced from that part, and join the two heads of the siphac together in fours.
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de II pars, puis assemble les II chiés de la plaie avenanment, et puis laisse I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	Then strain a double thread around the needle in two parts, then bring together the two sides of the wound accordingly, and leave one finger's width, and insert another needle.
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille, et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles, tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	Then tie the thread like you did with the first needle, and do not stop until all needles are tied according to your needs, until the entire wound is constrained.
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses, car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	And use medium-sized needles, between fine and thick ones, because the fine needles cut through all the flesh, and the too thick ones cannot enter well.
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	For this reason, they should be medium-sized.
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir, k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	And one should not insert the needles too far beyond the flesh and skin, lest they cut and open the wound before it is sutured.
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir, et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir, et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and then cover the joints with gauze made from needles, so that they do not wound the patient when asleep, and put a little tent or bandage over the joints of the needles to hold them in place, and leave it until the wound is healed.
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies, car il i soffist une aguille ou II.	this method of sewing with needles is more suitable for small wounds, because it requires just one or two needles.
Li seconde costure si est commune, et est que tu assemble les II chiés dou cuir et les II chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait I fort fil moien;	The second kind of suturing is common, and it involves bringing together the two sides of the skin and the two sides of the subcutaneous tissue with one needle or a strong middle-sized thread.
