puis torne sus la jambe et sus la cuixe le bendeil, puis met sus la briseure esteles, et met une estele sus l’os de la jambe;	Then turn the bandages back over the leg and thigh, put some splints over the fracture, and place a splint over the bone of the leg.
puis emple le leu vuit entre la jambe et la cuixe de drapelz souef por mettre igal l’estrignement, puis comence a liier forment III tors ou IIII sus la briseure;	Then fill the empty space between the leg and thigh with soft cloth to evenly distribute the pressure, then start tying in a triple or quadruple knot over the fracture.
et quant plus vas en sus de la briseure, et moins l’estraint;	and when you go further above the fracture, hold it less firmly.
puis enten as II chiés dou fil que tu as bouteit entre la jambe et la cuixe, et en lie III esteles que sont desus, puis revai au desoz au chief dou fil, tant que tu veignes delez le piet;	then tie two threads to the ends of the bone that you have inserted between the leg and thigh, and bind three splints above them. Then return below the end of the thread until you reach near the foot.
et l’estraint, si qu’il ne se mueve de son leu, puis le laisse ensi, puis k’il n’i vient ne aposteme ne enfleure n’autre semblant.	hold it firmly so that it does not move from its place, then leave it like this, ensuring no abscess nor swelling or other similar thing develops.
Et s’il i avient, si le deslie, et adresce ceu que i vient, si com nos avons dit maintes fois;	and if it does occur, then untie it and address what has arisen, as we have said many times.
et se il i a pieces de l’os que poigne, si le covient ewer, s’om puet;	and if there is any fragment of the bone held within, it must be removed, as far as possible.
et s’on ne puet, si covient fendre le leu, et traire fuer;	and if one cannot, it is necessary to split the place and draw out fire.
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant k’il soit sanez.	and treat the wound as we have said, until it is healed.
Et aucune fois est brisie li cuixe ensi c’on i met esteles, si com en l’ajutoire et ou bras;	And sometimes the thigh is broken in such a way that one must insert nails into it, as with the shoulder and arm;
toutevoie, en la restauration ensi faite ne cloche mie li malaides.	however, the patient does not suffer any harm from this restoration.
Et saiches que li cuixe est restoree en L jors, ou poc moins ou poc plus, selonc les diversitez des complexions.	And know that the thigh is restored in an average of 50 days, perhaps a little less or more depending on the diversity of temperaments.
de la ruelle dou genoil	From the groove of the knee.
Saiches que en la ruelle dou genoil avient poc brisure, mais elle ploie maintes fois.	Know that at the knee area there are few breaks, but it bends many times.
Et s’elle brise, si n’est mais c’une fendure, ou I pertus, et avient a tout plaie, et sens plaie, et ce sent om bien.	And if it breaks, it is only a crack, or a hole, and this happens to every wound, and unhealed wounds, and one feels it well.
Et li restauration si est c’on mette igal ceu qui est rons a ses dois, tant qu’il soit assemblez mues c’on puet;	And this restoration is done by placing what is rounded in its place equally with both hands until it can be assembled.
puis met l’emplaustre, et i met une estele reonde, se tu en as mestier, et l’estraint si com il covient, puis rewarde toutes les dispositions que nos avons dit ens autres briseures, si com aposteme chaut et autre semblant;	Then apply a plaster and insert a round nail if you need one, securing it as required. Then continue with all the procedures we have described for other fractures such as hot abscesses and similar conditions;
si met a chescun accident ceu k’il li covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If you apply to each case what is appropriate for it, until they are healed.
de la brisure de la jambe	On the break of the leg
Saiches que en la jambe ait II os, de coi li uns est apelez par droit non «mustelz», et li autres est apelez «foscile»;	Know that in the leg there are two bones, of which one is rightly called 'shin' and the other is called 'calf';
et avient tout auteil briseure com il vient au bras, et por ceu est li restauracion si com celle dou bras igalment, et li ovraiges est tout i. Et se li dui os sont brisiet ensamble, si torne li jambe de toutes pars.	And they have similar fractures like those that occur in the arm, and for this, the restoration is equal to that of the arm, and the treatment methods are all the same. If both bones are broken together, it turns the leg from all sides.
Et se li os subtilz est brisiez, si torne devant.	And if the fine bone is broken, it twists forward.
Et se li gros os est brisiez, si sent on grant dolor, et le voit on bien;	And if the larger bone is broken, one feels great pain, and it is clearly visible.
et torne desoz.	And it turns downwards.
Adonques amenistre extension, et le met igal, et lie les esteles igalement;	So extend it gently, place it straight, and bind the splints evenly.
mais toutevoie, il covient se li brisure est laide, et il i a plusors pieces, que li extension soit menor et plus legiere;	But nonetheless, if the fracture is severe and there are multiple pieces, the extension should be less intense and more gentle.
et l’alige selonc ta vertu.	And ease it according to your skill.
Et quant tu as tout acomplit ton ovraige, si pren II faixes de fust chevees que porpreignent la jambe d’une part et d’autre, et soient dou lonc de la jambe des le genoil jusque desoz;	And when you have completed your work, take two wooden splints that cover the leg from one side to another, and they should be as long as the leg from knee to below.
puis envoloupe en II leus I bendeil desus et desoz, et le lie em mileu ausi, et a ceste lieure ne pora li jambe decliner a destre ne a senestre, et ensi est bien;	Then wrap two layers of bandage around them and tie it in the middle as well, so that the leg cannot bend to the right or left, and thus it is secure.
et aucun i aministrent I bers dou lonc de la jambe, et s’est de fust, et i met on la jambe por warder de movement, et proprement fait on ceu en la brisure ou il a plaie;	And they apply one splint along the length of the leg, which is made of wood, and it holds the leg in place to prevent any movement, and properly done, it supports the fracture or wound.
et remue chescun jor la jambe, por veoir s’il i a aposteme chaut n’autre accident;	and move each leg daily, to check for abscesses or other complications.
si le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	heal it until it is fully cured.
de la brisure des os dou piet	Of broken bones of the foot.
A la cheville ne vient point de brisure, mais as os dou piet vient aucune fois brisure et as dois poc, et n’i avient fuer que quassure em plusor dispositions.	At the ankle, there is no fracture, but in the bones of the foot, there may be a break or crack, and it can be crushed in various ways.
Et s’il avient as os dou piet brisure, et tu vois ces os sormonter l’un l’autre, si mette si malaides som piet sus la terre, ausi com s’il voloit aler, et puis met maintenant ton piet sus lou sien, lai ou li os sont levez, puis le presse tant k’il reveignent en lor leus;	And if there is a broken bone in the foot, and you see these bones overlapping each other, place the patient's foot on the ground as if they were trying to walk, and then put your foot on theirs, where the bones are raised, pressing until they return to their places.
puis met l’emplaustre et estoupes sus, et met desoz lou ventre dou piet une petite tauble a II chiés plains, puis l’estraint au piet avenanment, puis que tu as envoloupez drapelz entor, et autres choses dont tu as mestier.	Then apply a plaster and bandage it on top, and place under the belly of the foot a small board with two curved ends, then tighten it to the foot appropriately, after you have wrapped cloth around it, and other things that are necessary.
Et quant III jors ou IIII seront passez, si deslie lou liien, car tu troveras les os igalz, soient brisiez, soient desaluez.	And when three or four days have passed, untie the binding, for you will find the bones equalized, whether broken or dislocated.
Et s’il i a aucuns des dois brisiez, si les restoure, si com nos avons dit as dois de la main;	And if there are any broken fingers, restore them as we have said for the fingers of the hand;
puis met au doi brisiet une estele selonc la longesce dou doi, et soit un poc plus large, puis met desoz le piet celle tauble que j’ai dit, et l’estrain avenanment;	Then place a splint on the broken finger in line with its length, and let it be slightly wider, then put under the foot that table I mentioned, and strain it appropriately;
et s’il en i a II ou III, ou plus, brisiez, si met sus chescun doi une estele selonc sa quantiteit, envoloupee en I drapeil de lin, et estraint la tauble desoz lou piet;	And if there are two or three or more broken fingers, place a splint on each finger according to its size, wrapped in a piece of linen, and strain the table under their foot.
et soit estans sus lou chief de la tauble defuer lou ventre dou piet, si qu’il le teigne bien.	And let it be stretched over the top of the table away from the foot's belly so that it holds it well.
Et covient que tu n’oblier mie les autres choses que j’ai dit as autres briseures, des que nos avons dit;	And you must not forget the other things I have said about other fractures, just as we have said before.
et secor chescun accident si com il covient.	And treat each accident as it ought to be treated.
de la brisure de l’os dou poignil	Of the fracture of the bone in the wrist.
Quant li os de la nature la femme est brisiez, si la fai seoir enlargie, puis l’encline a la partie dou dos, et soit tenue par derrier;	When the woman's hip bone is broken, make her sit with her legs spread apart, then lean her towards her back part and hold her from behind;
puis emplisse li baile la nature de la malaide de couton, et en i mette ausi gros com I sto;	Then fill the wound of the patient with cotton until it is filled up;
puis deboute la femme, et lieve lou dos poc et poc, et adonques saut li coton, tant qu’il vient a l’entree de la nature, et revient li os avec lou sto;	Then make the woman stand up, and lift her back bit by bit until the cotton comes out, reaching the entrance of her body, and the bone returns to its place along with the stool.
et quant elle vuet pissier, si oste lou coton, et quant elle a pissiet, se li remette, et ensi faice VII jors ou entor:	And when she wants to urinate, remove the cotton, and once she is done, put it back in, doing this for seven days or so.
si sera restoree li brisure, et se tu vues, pren une vessie de berbis, et lie au pertus une cainne, et boute toute la vessie en la nature;	If the fracture is restored, and if you see it, take a goat's bladder, tie a reed to its opening, and insert the whole bladder into the body.
puis soffle en la cainne forment, tant que li vessie soit enflee dedens:	Then blow strongly through the reed so that the bladder is fully inflated inside.
la nature si revenra li brisure;	The body will thereby restore the fracture.
puis soit emplie de coton, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit sanez.	It should then be filled with cotton and left in place for several days until it is healed.
Et quant li os dou poignil de l’ome est brisiez, ou de la femme, si le restoure ensi com nos avons dit en l’os de la hainche;	And when the wrist bone of a man or woman is fractured, restore it as we have said for the hip bone;
et ne sont mie occultees ces briseures prochienes a celui qui i met son estude et son us, et entent mon livre.	These fractures are not hidden from one who applies study and practice to them, and reads my book attentively.
Car li brisure li signifie em plusors dispositions la droite voie de la restauration:	For the fracture indicates to many the right way of restoration:
enten le donques.	understand it therefore.
En la verge, quant elle est brisie, pren une gorge d’oie et i boute la verge;	In the rod, when it is broken, take a goose's throat and insert it into the rod;
puis envoloupe drapelz entor, et le laisse III jors ou enqui entor, et il sera sanez hastanment.	Then wrap it with fine cloths around, and leave it for three days therearound, and it will be swiftly healed.
de brisure avec plaie	When fracture is associated with wound:
Il covient a celui qui a brisure avec plaie, meismement s’elle est grans, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire ou semblant, qu’il soit sainiez maintenant, si que les sainies que nos avons dit le tesmoignent.	It is necessary for one who has a fracture with wound, especially if it's large, such as the bone of the thigh or shoulder, to be immediately treated so that the wounds we have described may testify (to its efficacy).
Et se li plaie saine, si la restainche de vitriole, se tu n’as autre chose, puis rencomence a restorer la briseure en cele meisme houre, ou celui jor, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	And if the wound heals, treat it with vitriol to stop bleeding, unless you have other means, then restart restoring the fracture that very hour or day, provided no hot abscesses arise.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si laisse la restauration jusc’a nuevime jor, tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et n’i touchier ne au tier jor ne au quart, car tu i feroies venir malvais accident.	And if hot abscesses do arise, leave the restoration until the ninth day, until the abscess is pacified, and do not touch it on the third or fourth day, for you will bring about an evil event.
Et se li os brisiez est aparans sus lou keur descovert, si covient que tu lou mettes a point legierement a tes mains, a extension petite.	And if the broken bone is visible on an exposed heart, you must set it gently with your hands at a small extent.
Et se li extensions ne t’est apareillie por mettre igal a tes mains, si le ramoine a cest estrument qui est de fer, qui a VII dois ou VIII de lonc, et li largesce est selonc la quantiteit de la plaie;	And if the extension is not equipped to align with your hands, use this iron instrument which has seven or eight tines and is as long as the width of the wound;
et por ceu est mestier au mire qu’il empreigne III ou IIII, selonc ceu qu’il en ait mestier en chescune cure de briseure;	and for this the surgeon must grip three or four, according to what is needed in each treatment of a fracture;
et soit rons et un poc gros, k’il ne ploie mie a la compression sus lou membre a ton ovraige, et soit agus devant, et gros des le mileu en avant, ensi:	and be round and slightly thicker so that it does not bend under the pressure on the limb during your work, and be sharp at the front, and thick in the middle towards the front, like this
Et est apelez «palainche», por coi il covient que li chiés corbes soit mis sus lou chief de l’os apparent;	And it is called a "palanche," so the curved blades must be placed over the head of the protruding bone;
et le boute a une fois, tant k’il reviegne, et soit igalz l’un encontre l’autre.	and push it in once until it returns and is even with the other one.
Et se li brisure est subtilz, et li estrumens ne puet bien prendre l’os, si covient que tu copes lou chief de l’os, tant que li estrumens en ait possance.	And if the fracture is subtle, and the instrument cannot grasp the bone well, then you must cut off the head of the bone until the instrument has a hold of it.
Et se tu ne pues ramener l’os, si com nos avons dit, si lou cope d’un estrument covenable a ceu, ou incisoire ou soieure, a ton pooir;	And if you cannot reposition the bone as we have said, then use an appropriate tool for this, either a chisel or a saw, according to your ability.
puis reis ceu qui est demorez en l’os d’aspreteit et de menues escorces.	then remove what remains in the bone of roughness and small splinters.
Et quant li os est ramenez, et li malaides sent grant dolor aprés, saiches qu’il n’est mie en son leu natureil.	And when the bone is reset, and the patient feels great pain afterward, know that it is not in its natural place.
Si fai tant qu’il soit en son leu, puis moille I drapeil en vin stiptique noir, et proprement se c’est en esteit;	Si do your best to ensure it is back in its place, then soak a cloth in black styptic wine, and apply it properly if that was the issue.
et ne mettre mie sus la plaie cerote ne autre chose ou il ait oile, qu’il n’i faice venir porriture et corruption;	and do not apply any ointment or other oily substance to the wound, as it will cause it to become infected and corrupt.
puis aministre esteles quant tu as restoreit l’os, et laisse la plaie descoverte, et cope la coverture tout entor, selonc la quantiteit de la plaie, et te done bien en garde que li plaie ne soit estrainte avec la brisure;	Then apply stars when you have restored the bone, and leave the wound uncovered. Cover it all around with a bandage according to the size of the wound, and be very careful that the wound is not constricted by the broken area.
et maintes fois ont ce fait li fol mire, et ont fait venir sus le malaide ou mort ou corrodent aucune fois;	and often these foolish surgeons have done this, causing death or corrosion in some cases.
et soit li estrignemens plus molz et plus souef des autres brisures.	And the constriction should be looser and softer than other breaks.
Et se li plaie est male ou grans, et tu doutes que mavais accidens n’i veigne, si com nos avons dit, et tu trueves dolor au leu, si n’i covient mie mettre sus esteles;	And if the wound is bad or large, and you fear an adverse event may occur as we have stated, and you find pain at the site, it should not be treated with stellar [astrology] remedies.
mais envoloupe entor, en leu d’esteles, drapelz durs, et les lie.	but wrap around it, instead of using stars [astrology], hard rags, and bind them.
Et quant tu vois aprés I jor ou II enjanrer bowe a la plaie, si oste ceu que tu as mis sus a tout vin, et i met oignement sanant plaies, si com oignement tetrafarmaçon et semblans.	And when you see after one or two days that the wound is swelling again, remove what you have put on it previously and apply a healing ointment, such as tetrapharmacon ointment and similar ones.
Et covient que tu deslies lou membre II fois le jor, lou matin et au vespre, tant qu’il soit soudez et sanez.	And you should loosen the limb twice daily, in the morning and at dusk, until it is fused and healed.
Et covient que li membres soit aparilliez en teil maniere que li bowe corre aval legierement.	And the limb should be bandaged in such a way that the swelling flows downwards gently.
Et se maint jor trespassent, et il ne puet souder mais rent adés bowe, saiches k’il i a petites pieces d’os, por coi il covient que tu quieres la plaie avec tente, et oste toutes ces pieces desevrees que font venir celle dolor.	And if after many days it does not heal but swells again, know that there are small bone fragments present, which is why you must examine the wound with a probe and remove all these troublesome pieces causing this pain.
Et se fistule vient au leu, ou autre maniere de corruption, si covient que tu le cures, selonc ceu qu’il dist en son chapistre ci devant.	And if a fistula forms at that spot or some other kind of infection develops, you must treat it according to what he said in his previous chapter.
Et quant li os est brisiez, et apert sus lou membre, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire, et autres semblans des grans membres, si ne le traire mie, car maintes fois en vient li mors, mais le laisse tant qu’il porrisse;	And when the bone is broken and exposed on a limb, as with the bones of the thigh or shoulder, and other similar large limbs, do not draw it [the wound] out, for many times death follows, but leave it until it rots.
par aventure cherra par lui aprés XX jors ou XXX, puis cure la plaie, se tu pues;	Perhaps after twenty or thirty days it will fall out by itself, then treat the wound if you are able to.
et se tu ne pues, si la laisse.	And if you cannot, then leave it.
des brus qui vienent sor la sodure	The scabs that form over the suture.
Nous vienent maintes fois aprés la santeit de la briseure, meismement quant c’est pres de la jointure, et laide chose est a veoir li figure dou membre;	We often encounter the healing of fractures, especially when they are near the joints, and it is an unpleasant sight to see the appearance of the affected limb.
et par aventure ne puet faire li membres ses ovraiges naturelz.	And sometimes the limb may not be able to perform its natural functions.
Pren warde donques se li nous est fres:	Take care then if it is fresh for us.
si li aministre medicines stiptiques, si com aloes, encens, et mirre, et sarcocolle, acaice, et semblans autres, ensi que tu preignes aucune de ces choses, ou toutes ensamble, et les confit avec vin stiptique ou avec abun d’uef ou avec aisil;	If you administer styptic medicines such as aloe, incense, and myrrh, as well as sarcocolle, alum, and similar substances, in whichever of these things you choose or use them all together, and mix it with a styptic wine or egg white or isinglass.
et les met sus le nout en estoupes, et l’estraint bien, et ne la desliier en mains jors;	and place them on a cloth with pads, and hold it tight, and do not release for two days.
et puis la desloie, et rencomence une autre, tant que li nodations soit ostee;	then remove the first bandage, and start another one, until the inflammation is gone.
ou tu estrain sus une piece de plonc bien faite;	or you bind it onto a well-made wooden board;
car li proprietez dou plonc si est qu’il oste toutes les enfleures desus les membres;	because the property of wood is that it removes all swelling from the limbs;
et se li nodation est ja convertie en durteit ausi com piere, et il est besoing de l’oster, si la cope desus, et fent la superfluiteit apparent;	and if the inflammation has already hardened like stone, and it needs to be removed, scrape away the top layer, and expose the excess.
ou tu la reis a aucun raseur, tant qu’ele soit ostee, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee.	or you reduce it with a scraper until it is removed, then treat it until it is healed.
dou membre qui est foibles aprés la garison	Of the limb which is weak after recovery
Quant li brisure de l’os est restoree, et demoure aprés li membres foibles et subtilz, si avient por mout de causes:	When the bone fracture is healed, and afterward the limb remains weak and delicate, this happens for many reasons:
de coi l’une est por ceu qu’il fut liiez trop estroit, et ne fut mie liiez si com il covenoit;	because one reason is that it was bound too tightly, and was not bandaged as it should have been;
ou por ceu qu’il i ot trop de liiens, et ne pooit venir li norrissemens au membre;	or because there were too many bindings, preventing the nourishment from reaching the limb;
ou por multitude d’arosement;	or due to excessive bloodletting;
ou por trop grans movements, ne mie en son houre;	or because of too much movement, not at the right time;
ou por ceu qu’il a poc de sanc en son cors, si est foibles.	or due to having little blood in their body, they become weak.
Et li cure si est que tu faices mengier le malaide, et faire le cors tendre, tant que li sans soit multipliiez en lui;	And the treatment is for you to have the patient eat, and make their body tender, so that the blood is multiplied within them;
et li aministre bain, et li done joie et liesce;	and administer it well, and give him joy and permission;
puis met poix sus le membre, si que li poix atraie a li grant norrissement, et l’arose sovent d’aigue tede, tant que li norrissement corre au membre;	then apply pitch onto the limb, so that the pitch draws out the great nourishment, and irrigate it often with warm water, until the nourishment reaches the limb;
et reviegne a sa figure natureil.	and returns to its natural shape.
dou membre tort aprés la santeit	Of a twisted limb after the sanctity.
Quant li membres est tors aprés la restauration, et li os brisiez apert, et li forme dou membre est laide, toutevoie ne pert mie son ovraige natureil:	When the limb is twisted after restoration, and the bone is evidently broken, and the shape of the limb is ugly, nevertheless it does not lose its natural function:
si ne croire mie les folz qui dient c’on doit brisier lou membre tout de noveil, et maint fol mire ont ce fait en nostre terre;	do not believe the fools who say that one must break the limb anew, and many a foolish doctor has done this in our land;
et cist ovraiges est blamez, et en vient grans malz, et par aventure li mors;	and these procedures are blamed for causing great harm, often resulting in death;
toutevoie, se li nodations et li torture sont fres, si covient k’il soient arosez d’aigue chaude, ou herbes mollifians soient cuites, si com foilles de vismalve, et racines, et mellilote, et semblans choses;	However, if the nodules and torticollis are fresh, they should be treated with hot water or softened herbs that have been cooked, such as leaves of marshmallow, roots, and honeysuckle, and similar things.
et li fai I emplaustre mollificatif, si com dyaquilon bien fait, et tu pren le muscillaige de vismalve, et la confit avec graisse de geline ou oile de sisament, et fai emplaustre sus;	Make a softening plaster, such as well-made daisy plaster, and take the juice of marshmallow, mix it with goose fat or sesame oil, and apply this plaster on top.
ou tu pren figues graisses, et les broie avec fien de colon, et semblans medicines que amenuisent le soudement.	Alternatively, take fatty figs, grind them with colander husk, and similar medicines that reduce swelling.
Et aucune fois est ostee li nodacion por froter continuelment et longement a mains moistes.	And sometimes the swelling is removed by rubbing continually and for a long time with moist hands.
Et soit amenistrez movement au membre chescune houre.	Let there be gentle movements to the limb every hour.
Et se li tortuositez est enveillie et endurcie, ausi com piere, et besoins est de l’oster au fer, si la covient coper jusc’a l’os, a l’incisoire subtil legierement;	If the torticollis is old and hardened like stone, requiring removal with an iron tool, it should be cut down to the bone using a delicate and light knife.
et mettre cusenson et estude en la cure.	and apply a compress and devote attention to their care.
Ci encomence li livres des dislocations	Here begins the book of dislocations.
Dislocations est issue d’aucune jointe de son leu, por coi il ne se puet muevre, et est li membres mal figurez, et sent li malaides grant dolor et grant lesion.	Dislocation occurs when a joint moves out of its place, which prevents it from moving, and the limb is misaligned, causing the patient great pain and injury.
Quant dislocation vient a aucun, si le covient maintenant ramener sens targier.	When dislocation occurs in someone, you must reset it immediately without delay.
Car s’on tarde, si enfle li leus, et par aventure si le remet on a poines au leu;	For if one delays, the joint will swell, and perhaps it may be reset painfully into its place;
por ceu ne covient mie c’on le mueve a l’oure k’il est enflez:	due to which one should not move it at the hour when it is swollen:
maintes fois fait venir spame et autres dolors;	often causing infection and other pains;
toutevoie, quant ce avenra, si fai sainier lou malaide, puis le laisse, tant que li apostemes chas soit apaisiez;	nevertheless, when this happens, have the patient bleed, then leave them be until the abscess subsides;
puis arose le membre d’aigue chaude et d’oile, puis le ramoinne legierement, et cure chescun membre si com li cure venra en son leu.	then bathe the limb in warm water and oil, then gently reset it, and treat each limb as it returns to its place.
Et j’ai ordenez les chapistres des dislocations des lou chief jusc’a piez.	And I have ordered the chapters on dislocations from head to foot.
des mandibules	Of jaws.
Poc avient que les mandibules soient desaluees andous, et li dislocations d’ambedous est selonc II manieres:	Often it happens that jaws are dislocated on both sides, and dislocation of both occurs in two ways:
ou elles sont un poc ostees de lor leus, et mollifies un poc;	where they are slightly moved from their places, and softened somewhat;
ou elles sont desaluees entierement, et pendent vers lou pis, et cort li salive de la bouche qu’il ne la puet tenir, ne ne puet clore sa bouche, et envoloupe sa langue avec la parole.	or they are completely dislocated, and hang downwards, and the saliva falls from the mouth so that he cannot hold it, nor can he close his mouth, and his speech is slurred.
Quant li dislocations est petite, si revient par li em plusors disposicions.	When a dislocation is minor, one can recover through many treatments.
Et s’elle est entiere et acomplie, si covient que tu la ramoinne hastanment, et ne targier mie;	And if it is complete and perfect, then you must reset it promptly, and not delay;
et en tel maniere que li ministres teigne le chief dou malaide, et boute li mires som pochet de l’une de ses mains en la racine de la dislocation de la mandibule dedens la bouche, se li dislocations est de II pars;	and in such a manner that the assistant holds the patient's head, and pushes their finger from one of their hands into the root of the jaw dislocation inside the mouth, if the dislocation is on two sides;
et li autre doi des mains soient defuer, por mettre igal;	And the other fingers of the hands shall be bent outwards, to make them equal.
et comande au malaide qu’il les amollisse, ses mandibules, et les mueve de toutes pars.	And instruct the patient to soften their jaws and move them in all directions.
Et li mires la mete igal, tant qu’elle reveigne en son leu.	The assistant should apply equal pressure until it returns to its place.
Et se li ramener est griés, meismement se ce sont les II mandibules ensamble, si les arose d’aigue chaude et d’oile, tant que les ramoinnes legierement;	And if it is badly dislocated, especially if both jaws are involved, bathe them with hot water and oil until they can be gently reset.
ne ne targier mie dou ramener, si com nos avons dit.	Do not delay in resetting it, as we have said.
Et quant elles sont ramenees igalment, et li bouche dou malaide clot bien sens mollifiier, si met sus drapelz moilliez en cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire, puis le lie legierement de molz liiens;	And when they are reset evenly, and the patient's mouth is well closed with softened gums, apply moist lint dressings in a soft ointment made of rose oil and wax, then lightly bind it with soft cords.
et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ses chiés soit estans entre II cussins, si qu’il ne lou mueve ne a destre ne a senestre, ne ne s’efforce mie de maixier, mais preigne legiere viande, tant que les dolors soient ostees, et soient noees les mandibules;	And let the patient sleep on their back, with their shoulder extended between two pillows so that they cannot move it to the right or left, and do not try to bend it. They should eat lightly until the pain is gone, and keep their jaws clenched shut.
et puis menjuce ce qu’il vuet legierement, et ne se travaille mie d’ovrir la bouche au mengier et au boivre, tant que li mandibule soit bien noee et sanee.	Then let them eat whatever they want lightly, and do not strain themselves by opening their mouth too wide when eating or drinking, until the jaw is well healed and healthy.
Et se les II mandibules ne pueent estre remises a point a une houre, et ne sont mie converties a lor leus, si en vient fievres et sode acostumees, et par aventure solution de ventre, et par aventure vomist cole pure.	And if the two jaws cannot be brought back to their proper place within an hour, and they do not return to their correct position, fevers and persistent soreness will occur, and possibly violent purging, and perhaps vomiting of clear fluid.
Et quant tu verras ceu, adonc saiches que c’est perdicions;	And when you see this, know that it is ruinous;
et maintes fois muert cil cui il avient, en VIIII jors.	and many times the person dies within nine days.
de la forcelle	Of the fork.
Li forcele ne puet desaluer dou costeit dedens la continuation de li et dou pis, et est desaluee aucune fois au defuer, et bien le sent on.	The fork cannot be dislocated from the inside, along its length or at the base; and is sometimes dislocated outwards, which can easily be felt.
Et li restauration si est que li malaides gise sovin sor son dos, et estende ses bras;	And the recovery process is as follows: let the patient lie frequently on their back with their arms outstretched;
et puis presse le leu forment a ta palme, et elle revenra;	and then press the place hard with your palm, and it will return
puis met sus l’emplaustre et lou bendeil, et l’estraint;	then apply the plaster and bind it tightly;
et li chiez qui est devers lou coute ne puet desaluer;	and if the shoulder is facing towards the knife, it cannot be reset;
se poc non, et se il desalue aucune fois, si le ramoinne a son leu, si com nos avons dit;	if not, and if it dislocates at any time, reset it to its place as we have said;
puis met sus l’emplaustre et le bendeil, et l’estraint, et coumande au malaide qu’il se repose tant qu’il soit sanez;	then put on the plaster and bind it, securing it tightly, and instruct the patient to rest until they are healed;
et ensi meisme est ramenez li chiés de l’espale, quant il est desevrez de son leu.	in the same way, reset the shoulder blades when they have dislocated from their place.
de la dislocation de l’espaule	Of shoulder dislocation
Saiches que li espaule n’est desaluee fuer que selonc III manieres:	Saiches que li espaule n'est desaluee fuer que selonc III manieres: 
de coi l’une est qu’ele desalue a la partie de l’assele au desoz;	Of which one is that it dislocates to the part of the socket below
et li seconde est a la partie dou pis;	and the second [dislocation] is at the part of the shoulder blade;
et par aventure desalue a la partie desus, et ceu avient poc;	and by chance dislocates above, and this occurs rarely;
et ne desalue mie derrier por l’espaule, et ne desalue mie dedens por les ners;	and it does not dislocate behind the shoulder, nor inside towards the nerves;
et plusors fois desalue desoz vers l’assele, meismement a ces qui ont poc de char, car a ces saut ele fuer hastanment;	and often dislocates below towards the socket, especially in those with little flesh, for it easily falls through to the bone.
a ces qui ont assez char, saut ele a poines, et rentre a poines.	in those who have sufficient flesh, it falls [dislocates] slowly and returns slowly.
Et par aventure avient a aucuns homes percussion ou casseure, et enfle li espaule d’un aposteme chaut, et cuide qu’elle est desaluee par ceu.	And occasionally it happens to some men that there is a blow or fracture, and the shoulder swells from a hot abscess, and they think it has dislocated because of this.
Il covient donques que tu l’esprueves, tant que tu en soies certains;	Therefore, you must test it until you are certain.
et adonques encomence la cure.	And then begin the treatment.
Et est conue li dislocations quant il est aval vers l’assele, et met difference entre l’espaule malade et la saine, et tu troveras entre lor diversiteit manifeste;	And it is understood that dislocation occurs when the arm falls towards the shoulder blade, and there is a notable difference between the affected shoulder and the healthy one; you will find an evident disparity between them.
et troveras au chief de l’espaule une fosse, et desoz l’assele au tochier le chief de l’espaule, ausi com se ce soit uns oes;	and you will find a hollow at the shoulder head, and beneath the shoulder blade up to the neck is like an egg.
et ne puet li malaides ramener sa main a son neis, ne movoir de nulz movemens;	and the patient cannot bring their hand to their nose nor move in any way.
et ausi, s’elle est desaluee en haut, si n’est mie occultee, car tu le trueves manifestement au tochier;	and if it is dislocated upwards, it is not hidden, for you will find it evident at the neck.
et ceste maniere de dislocation n’est mie fors a ramener, quant elle est novele, ou se li enfes est malaides.	and this manner of dislocation is not difficult to reset when it is new or the patient is young.
Et li maniere est que li ministres lieve la main dou malaide en haut, puis met tes peuchas desoz l’assele, et lieve la jointure a force en haut au leu;	And the procedure is that the minister lifts the patient's hand upward, then places your palms underneath the armpit, and forcibly lifts the dislocated joint upwards to its place;
et li ministres lieve la main, et l’estende en haut, pues le mette desoz;	and the minister lifts the hand, extends it upward, then places it underneath;
si venra hastanment.	thus will come numbness.
Et s’elle ne vient si com nos avons dit em mains jors aprés, si covient ke li malaides soit baigniez en aigue chaude;	And if it does not come about as we have said with hands exposed afterward, then the patient must be bathed in warm water;
et li amenistre arosement mollifiant et assouajant, si com decoction de altee et de fenugrec et de mellilote en aigue, et soit amenistree;	and the minister applies soothing and softening ointments, such as a decoction of althea, fenugreek, and melilot in water, to be applied accordingly;
puis soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos, et mette on desoz l’assele un sto de lainne igal, ne trop mol ne trop dur, puis mette li mires son talon sus le sto, et lieve le chief de l’espaule vertuousement, et traie la main dou malaide;	then the patient is turned onto their back, and a block of even wool, neither too soft nor too hard, is placed underneath their armpit, then place the heel of their foot on the block, lift the head of the virtuous shoulder, and pull the patient's hand;
et uns autres ministres teigne lou chief dou malaide, si qu’il ne se mueve aval;	and another minister holds the patient's head, so it does not move downwards.
celle espaule revient tout maintenant, et se tu vues si le ramoinne selonc ceste maniere:	this shoulder returns immediately, and if you see that it resets following this method:
et est que tu faices estre present I home qui soit plus grans que li malaides;	and have a man who is larger than the patient be present;
et soit drois devers lou costeit, et boute s’espaule desoz l’assele dou malaide, et lieve l’assele en haut, si que li malaides pende en l’ar;	and he should stand straight facing the patient's side, and push their shoulder from under the armpit of the patient, lifting the armpit upwards so that the patient hangs in the air.
et uns autres ministres traie la main dou malaide aval devers lou ventre.	another minister pulls the patient's hand downwards towards their belly.
Et se li malaides est trop legiers, si pent avec lui aucune chose pesant, et li dislocation revient maintenant.	And if the patient is too light, you may use something heavy with them, and the dislocation will return now.
Et le ramoinne on ausi en autre maniere:	And it is also reset in another way:
et est c’on fiche I lonc tison en terre, dont li chiés soit ausi reons com I pistal, et ne soit ne trop gros ne trop graile;	And one fixes a long stake into the ground, so that the head is as round as a pistol, and it should not be too thick nor too thin.
puis soit mis desoz lou malaide, mais k’il ait drapelz souef sus, et li malaides soit estans dou lonc dou fust;	Then one should be placed underneath the patient, but let them have soft blankets on top, and the patient must be extended along the length of the stake.
puis soit estendue sa main aval d’autre part forment, et li jointure revenra en son leu hastanment;	Then one must stretch their arm downwards on the other side in such a manner that the joint will return to its place gradually.
et s’elle ne vuet revenir por toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si fai ceste cure:	And if it does not wish to go back into place due to all the things we have said, then do this treatment:
pren I tison de II bras de grant et IIII dois de large, qui ait le chief reont por mues entrer em parfont desoz l’assele, selonc ceste forme:	Take a stake two arms lengths long and four fingers wide which has a rounded head so that you can insert it perfectly beneath the shoulder blade according to this shape:
puis lie sus le chief dou fust drapelz souez, que li fust ne blece lou malaide, puis le met desoz l’assele dou malaide;	Then place over his head a soft linen cloth so that it does not hurt the patient, then put it underneath the armpit of the patient;
et estende som bras sus le fust dou lonc, et lie l’ajutoire sus le fust, et lou bras au chief de la main, puis met le bras sus I eschillon d’une eschiele dou large, et soit estendue li mains aval, et soit laissiez li cors pendans d’autre part:	and extend his arm onto the long side of the log, and tie the shoulder joint to the log, and the arm to the head of the patient, then place the arm on a plank from an upright ladder, and let the hands be extended downwards, and leave the body hanging from the other side:
li jointure reva ens maintenant.	the dislocation has returned again now.
Et quant elle est ens, en quel maniere que ce soit, si covient que tu mettes desoz l’assele une spere de laine igal, puis met l’emplaustre aparilliet de poudre dou molin, avec encens et aubun d’uef, sus toute l’espaule et entor, puis l’estrain desoz l’assele avenanment, et torne le liien sus l’emplaustre, et embraice la main a son col, et soit li mains demorans ensi.	And when it is thus, in whatever way, you must put under the bedstead a woollen pad of equal size, then apply the plaster prepared with flour of mill, together with incense and egg white, over the whole shoulder and around it; then strain the binding under the bedstead suitably, and turn the bandage back upon the plaster, and embrace the hand to his neck, and let the hands remain thus.
Et covient qu’il menjuce poc, tant que li membres soit confortez, car il sanera plus tost;	And ensure that he moves little, so that the limb may be comfortable, for it will heal sooner;
et puis menjuce plus aprés V jors ou VII, et le mueve;	and then let him move more after five or seven days, and set the limb again;
et s’il est fermeis et il n’est mollifiez, si est sanez.	And if it is closed and not softened, then it is healed.
Et se li jointure est fuer de leu por moistor que i est venue, ou por autre cause, si covient que tu i aministres cauteres a III pertus, si com il est mis devant ou chapistre des cauteres.	And if the joint is dislocated due to moisture that has entered it or for another reason, you must apply cauterization to three openings, as described earlier in the chapter on cautery.
Et se tu fais tout ceu, et il deslie aprés VII jors, et li jointure ne se tient, et ne puet lever som bras amont, adonc saiches que li nerf au chief de l’espaule sont copeit ou estendut ou amollis;	And if you do all that, and it dislocates again after seven days, and the joint does not hold, and he cannot lift his arm upwards, then know that the nerve at the head of the shoulder is either cut, stretched, or weakened.
et saiches que li jointure n’iert jamais fichie en son leu.	and understand that the joint will never be properly fixed in place.
Li dislocation qui est devers lou pis, et les mameles, ou derrier, si est faite par impulsion, et estendement de mains, et i aministre on autre lieure;	The dislocation towards the armpit, breasts, or back is caused by a thrust and stretching of the hands, and another remedy should be administered there.
et cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it until it is healed.
Et se aprés la sanation vient grietez au membre, et tardemens em movement, si use li malaides bain maintes fois, tant que celle grietez soit alegie, et reviegne a sa premiere nature.	And if after the healing process the member becomes cracked and moves slowly, the patient should bathe frequently until this cracking is alleviated, and it returns to its original state.
de la dislocation dou coute	On the dislocation of the neck
Saiches que li jointure dou coute est desaluee a poinnes, et a poinnes revient;	Know that the joint of the neck is dislocated to a small degree, and it returns in the same way;
et s’est desaluee de toutes pars, et meismement devant et derrier, et li dislocations n’est mie reponue, car on la voit bien et sent bien;	And if it is dislocated from all sides, especially in front and behind, and the dislocation has not been reduced, for it can be seen clearly and felt well;
et desalue selonc chescune figure.	And reset according to each particular case.
Et quant tu joins le coute malaide avec lou sain, si le pues veoir apertement.	And when you join the sick person's wound with the healthy one, you can see it clearly.
Car li jointure est chevee, et ne puet ploier lou bras, ne touchier son espaule a tout.	For the joint is separated, and cannot bend the arm or reach their shoulder at all.
Et covient que tu le ramoinnes ainsois que apostemes chaus i viegne, car se apostemes chaus i venoit, si seroit grief li ramener;	And you must reset it even if there is an abscess present, for if the abscess occurs, it would make reduction difficult;
et par aventure ne puet estre ramenez dou tout en tout, meismement quant ele est au derrier;	and perhaps it cannot be fully reduced from end to end, especially when it is at the back;
si vaut pis que les autres dislocations, et est de plus grant dolor, et par aventure i vient li mors.	it is worse than other dislocations, and causes even more pain, and perhaps death may result.
Et li restauration si est, quant elle est telz c’on la puet ramener, que tu li estendes sa main a tes II mains;	And the restoration is as follows when it can be reduced: extend your hand to their two hands;
et ses bras soit espandus, et les mains dou mire selonc le coute entor, desor et desoz, et boute la jointure a ses peuchas ensamble, ou a la racine de sa palme, tant qu’ele reviegne a son leu.	And let his arms be spread out, with the hands of the patient placed mirror-like according to the cut around, above and below, then push the joint towards the armpit or the palm root until it returns to its place.
Et se li dislocations est au devant, si revient quant il double sa main a sa main, et fier de la racine de la palme lou coute qui est desaluez.	And if the dislocation is at the front, it returns when he bends his hand towards his hand, and press firmly on the root of the damaged palm's wrist.
Et s’il ne vuet revenir au leu, si aministre fort extension;	And if it does not want to return to its place, apply strong extension.
et est que dui ministre estendent le bras, et le teignent dui ministre, si qu’il ne se mueve a l’estension;	and make two ministers extend the arm, and let two ministers bend it, so that it does not move during extension;
puis torne le bras de chescune part, puis que tu as envoloupeit un drapeil double lonc et large;	then turn the arm from each side, then wrap it with a double-folded long and wide cloth;
et quant li mires a jointe la jointure a sa main, si l’oigne d’aucun oile por amolir la jointure, puis boute la jointure forment, tant qu’ele reviegne;	and when the mirror has joined the joint to the hand, anoint it with some oil to soften the joint, then push the joint firmly until it returns;
et quant elle est au leu, si met sus emplaustre sec avec aubun d’uef, et l’estrain forment, et pent le bras au col dou malaide, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le deslie.	When it is in place, apply dry poultice with egg white on top, press firmly, and bind the arm to the patient's neck; leave it for a few days, then remove it.
Et se li jointure est ferme en son leu, si deslie lou liien, et le laisse;	And if the joint is firmly in place, unbind the bandages and leave it alone.
et se tu vois que li jointure n’estrigne bien, si rencomence l’emplaustre et lou lien, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit fermement mis;	If you see that the joint is not well-bound, restart with the poultice and bandages, leaving it for a few days until it is firmly in place.
puis le deslie.	Then remove the bindings.
Et se il sent grieteit aprés le ramenement de la jointe, et elle se muet, si le baigne et frote bellement, et presse tant qu’il soit assouagiez;	And if the patient feels a tearing sensation after the joint is reset and it moves again, bathe them and massage gently, pressing until they feel relief.
ou tu met sus la jointure une naige de mouton grasse, puis la laisse I jor et une nuit, puis l’oste, et lou fai entrer ou bain;	Where you put on the joint a sheep's fat pad, then leave it there for a day and a night, then remove it, and have him enter the bath;
et quant il sue, se li frote la jointure tempreement, puis remet la naige sus, et puis entre ou bain;	And when he sweats, rub the joint gently, then put back the fat pad, and have him enter the bath again;
et ensi fai II fois ou III, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And do this twice or three times until he is healed;
et se tu vues, si met sus fien de vaiche moiste chaufeit avec burre, et l’estrain sus;	And if you see pus, put on moist warm cow dung mixed with butter, and keep it on top;
si revenra a sa disposition.	It will return to its normal position.
li dislocation de la main	The dislocation of the hand
Li jointure de la main desalue, et li revenue est legiere, plus que les autres jointures.	The wrist dislocated, and its recovery is light, lighter than the other joints.
Toutevoie, il la covient ramener au leu hastanment, en l’oure meisme qu’ele est desaluee, ainsois que li leus soit enflez, ou qu’il i viegne aposteme chaut.	Nevertheless, it must be reset immediately to its place of origin, in the same hour that it is dislocated, unless the area becomes swollen or an abscess forms there.
Et li ramenemens si est que tu mettes la main malaide sus une tauble, et estende li ministres la main, et li mires la mette igal, ensi que il mette sa paume sus l’aparance de la jointure, et la boute tant qu’elle reviegne.	And the resetting is done by placing the patient's hand on a table, having your assistants stretch out the limb, and ensuring it is aligned correctly, so that you place their palm over the appearance of the joint, pushing until it returns.
Toutevoie, il covient que vos regardez s’il est bien a leu;	Nevertheless, one must check that it is indeed in place;
adonc mette li malaides lou dos de sa main sus une tauble a l’estension et au ramenement.	Then have the patient put the back of their hand on a table, both during extension and resetting.
Et se li dislocations est au dos de la main, si mette li malaides son dos de sa main sus la tauble, et li mires mette sa main sus cele apparance de la jointure.	And if the dislocation is on the back of the hand, have the patient put the back of their hand on the table, and place your hand over that joint's area.
S’elle revient maintenant, c’est bien.	If it stays in place now, that's good.
Se ce non, si l’estrain d’emplaustres apaisans apostemes chaus, et lou laisse ensi sens rencomencier.	If this is not done, strain the emollient plasters to soothe hot abscesses, and leave them be without restarting.
Et s’il ne le puet soffrir, et tu ne la pues mettre au leu aprés aucuns jors, si demore li jointure torte;	And if he cannot endure it, and you are unable to put it back in place after a few days, the joint remains twisted;
et ne nuist niant au malaide fuer que tant que li mains est amoillie, et ne puet estraindre aucune chose a tout:	and it does not harm the patient for as long as the hand is softened, and cannot grip anything at all:
adonc saiches que li nerf sont copez, ou li artere;	then know that the nerve or artery has been severed;
si n’i a autre engien fuer que d’estraindre par cautere delez le cas, et par aventure n’i vaut autre chose.	if there is no other way to grasp it except by cauterizing around the case, and perhaps nothing else will help.
Et quant li mains est au leu, si met sus l’emplaustre que nos avons dit, puis l’estrain et le laisse V jors, puis le deslie et laisse ensi.	And when the hand is in place, apply the plaster we mentioned, then strain it and leave for five days, then release and leave as such.
Et s’il ne la puet bien movoir, et il i a aucune grieteit, si la moille d’aigue chaude, et le frote tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if it cannot move well, and there is any injury, then bathe it in warm water, and rub until it is healed.
de la dislocation des dois de la main	Of the dislocation of the fingers of the hand
Aucune fois sont desaluez li doi de la main a chescune part, aucune fois au dos de la palme ou au ventre;	Sometimes the fingers of the hand dislocate in every direction, sometimes on the back of the palm or the belly;
adonques estent le doi, et boute la dislocation a tes pouchés tant qu’il reviegne, puis sostien lou chief dou doi, et le pent vers la partie ou il est desjoins;	Thus stretch the finger, and push the dislocation with your thumbs until it returns, then support the head of the finger, and bend it towards the part where it is dislocated.
et le laisse II jors, et puis le met igal celui jor;	Leave it for two days, and then make it equal on that day;
et de nut le lie, si com nos avons dit, et lou deslie de jor, et lou fai movoir, et le relie la nut;	Bind it at night as we have said, unbind it during the day, make it move, and bind it again at night;
et fai ce sovent, tant qu’il soit estroit, et tout ausi fai, se il est desaluez au ventre de la main, et fai si com tu as fait ci devant, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Do this often until it is narrow, and do the same if it is dislocated at the palm of the hand, and act as you have done before, until it is healed;
et tout ausi fai, quant il est desaluez d’autre part.	And do likewise when it is dislocated in any other place.
dou desaluement de l’eschinee dou dos	Of dislocation of the spine from the back
Quant l’eschinee dou dos ou dou col est desaluee, ou il en i a plusors desaluees, si n’i a point de cure, car li mors haste le malaide.	When the spine from the back or neck is dislocated, or there are multiple dislocations, there is no treatment, as death comes swiftly to the patient.
Et li signes si est que li egestions saut fuer sens volunteit, ne ne la puet tenir, et maintes fois sont mollifiez aucun membre, ou les II cuixes ou li dui bras ou I.	And its signs are that the evacuations come out without wanting it, nor can she hold them in, and many times certain members are softened, or the two thighs or both arms or one.
Et maintes fois se muet li eschinee a IIII pars;	And many times the spine is dislocated into four parts.
celle qui se muet au derrier si est apelee «gilbositez»:	that which is displaced to the rear is called "crookedness".
li cure si est que tu rewarde se li gilbositez est venue d’enfance:	the treatment is that you must wait if it came from childhood.
si n’i ait point de cure ne de sanation dou tot.	there is no cure or healing for it at all.
Et celle que vient de cheoir ou de percussions ou de semblans choses, dirent li ancien manieres de cures par grans paroles, ou il n’a mie en toutes grant profit;	And that which comes from falling or blows or similar things, the ancient ways of treatment say there is little benefit in all of it.
mais je l’ai abregiet selonc mon entention, et ai formez estrumens en diverses manieres.	But I have shortened it according to my intention, and I have designed instruments in various ways.
Je dis que en la gilbositeit que vient au pis devant, nen a engien ne santeit;	I say that in the case of curvature which occurs at the foot in front, no one knows its cause nor its treatment;
et ausi cele que vient droitement en II costez, et ne puet on curer fuers que celi proprement qui vient au dos, si com je dis;	And also that which occurs directly on two sides, and it cannot be treated except for that which properly comes to the back, as I say;
et est que li malaides soit estendus sus sa faice en I leu igal, et ait de l’estrain desoz lui, qu’il ne se blece;	And it is that the patient should be extended on their face in an equal place, and have a strain beneath them, so they do not get hurt;
puis fiche I tison au chief en terre forment, et I autre as piez, et lie un liien pardesoz les asseles dou malaide, et I autre as hainches, et as genous, et as chevilles;	Then fix one iron rod firmly in the ground at the head and another at the feet, and tie a cord beneath the joints of the patient, and another to the hips, knees, and ankles;
et dui ministre saichent les liiens, li uns au chief et li autres as piez, parmi les II tisons;	And have two assistants hold the bindings, one on the head and the other on the feet, between the two firebrands.
et soient bien fermez, li tison si com nos avons dit, et li mires mette ses paumes sus l’espinee forment, tant qu’ele reviegne.	And ensure they are well secured, the firebrands as we have stated, and let the physician place their palms on the spine firmly, until it returns to its proper position.
Et s’elle ne revient par ceste cure, si pren une tauble de III bras de lonc, et chevé desoz la paroit, et li malaides soit en costé, et boute le chief de la tauble desoz la paroit, puis met le mileu de la tauble sus l’espinee;	If it does not return with this treatment, take a board three arms-length long, and place it under the patient's side, let the patient lie on their side with their head resting on the board, then put the middle of the board on the spine.
et mette li mires ses piez sus l’autre chief de la tauble, et presse bien, tant qu’il reviegne au leu;	And let the physician place their feet on the other end of the board, pressing firmly until it returns to its proper position.
et se tu vues, si le fai au tornet qui torne a la main.	and if you see this, make him turn his hand over.
Et est que tu fiches II tisons au chief dou malaide d’un bras de grant, et devers les piez II autres, et ait entre chescun tison, desoure et desoz, une paume d’espaice de lonc;	and put two red-hot irons on the patient's head for a long arm, and towards their feet another two, with each iron being separated by about one palm's length.
et ait en chescun tison I pertus, ou li tornet corre, et soient li tison fermement en terre, si qu’il ne se muevent;	and have one hole in each iron where the pivot goes, and let these irons be firmly planted so they don't move.
et entre chescuns II tisons ait I tison tornant, sor coi li liien tornent, et ait en II tornans II petis tisons d’une paume de lonc, por torner le tornet;	and between each pair of irons put one turning iron, upon which the pivots turn, and have two small irons about a palm's length to turn the pivot.
et puis lie lou lien qui est parmi les asseles au tornet devers le chief, et l’autre liien devers les piez a l’autre tornet, et chescuns des ministres torne son tornet a tout le liien, et li maistres mette l’espinee igal si com nos avons dit.	then bind the pivot which is among the handles to the pivot towards the head, and another binding from the feet to the other pivot, each of the assistants turns their own pivot with all their strength, while the master keeps the spine even as we have said.
Et quant elle est igalz, si met sus emplaustre desiccatif avec abun d’uef, et puis les estoupes, et puis l’estele d’une tablete de III dois de lonc, que porpreigne lou leu de la gilbositeit et la partie de l’espondile sainne, puis le lie d’un liien, si com nos avons dit, et use li malaides de norrissement subtil, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when it is even, apply a drying poultice with an abundance of egg, then some swabs, and finally the stem of a tablet three fingers long to treat the area of curvature and the healthy part of the spine. Then bind it with a bandage as we have said, using subtle nourishment for the patient until healing occurs;
et s’aucune chose vient en la fin de la santez, si covient aministrer medicines amollissans et asouajans, avec l’estele que nos avons dit ci devant;	and if any issue arises at the end of treatment, administer softening and soothing medications along with the stem we mentioned earlier;
et aucune fois i aministre on une piece de plonc, et aucune fois vient li apparance en la derriere spondile dou dos, et cuide on que ce soit dislocations;	and sometimes it is administered in one piece of lead, and at other times the appearance arises in the lower spine of the back, which people believe to be a case of dislocation;
et c’est li os qui apert, por coi on n’i doit mie avoir presumption:	and this is the bone which appears, for this reason one must not presume:
par aventure feroit venir la mort.	may cause death to come upon you.
des dislocations de la hainche	Hip dislocations.
Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures;	Know that only the joints of the hip and shoulder are subject to dislocations, not any other joints;
et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc IIII parties:	and the hip joint is dislocated according to four parts:
dedens et defuer ,et devant et derrier;	inside and outside, and in front and behind;
et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	and especially inside, or rather dislocated forward and backward.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	The knowledge of its internal dislocation is as follows: when one joins the affected leg with the healthy one, it is longer, and the sick knee appears more prominent than the healthy one, and the patient cannot bend their sick knee to the fire.
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	And it is the place next to the swollen abscess that is hot, because the hip joint has come loose there.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	And the sign of him for whom it happens in reverse is that this affliction stands contrary to what came before.
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement;	And for the signs of the one who is about to experience this in front, it is that he stretches his leg well according to its course.
toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	However, he does not bend the knee without pain, and if one wants him to walk, he cannot forward, and retains his urine, and the ankle swells, and when he goes, he steps on his heel.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	And the signs of him who has it behind are such that he cannot bend his knee or double up, and one leg is more twisted than the other, the groin is softened, and the shoulder head is in place under the ribs.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;	The remedy for this type of dislocation is that you reset it if the dislocation is old and remains according to its position, there is no treatment.
et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	And one must not have any presumption about it.
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des IIII manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre;	And for the one with fresh dislocation, which has four types of dislocation, hasten to return the joint, stretch it inward and outward, and move it right and left;
par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	By chance, it may return to its place, and no other treatment is needed.
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	And if it does not return with this method, you must prepare one strong assistant and stretch the leg vigorously by hand, or bind it with a ligature above the knee.
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	Another assistant should extend their hand above in such a way that they press their hands under the patient's armpits, then bind them tightly with a ligature around the thigh.
et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	Another should hold the head of the ligature.
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	and they extend upstream and downstream all at once, such that the patient is lifted from the ground all at once, and remains hanging.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as IIII semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This method of extension is common for the four similar cases, and if the dislocation has been corrected, as we have said, it is good.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	If not, it's necessary to apply treatment in a similar manner.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	When the dislocation is on the inside, you must place the patient on their healthy side, then put the bandage at the root of the thigh and the part below the groin, stretching the bandage upward towards the groin and towards the hip;
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	Then have another attendant take his arms and embrace the thick part of the injured thigh, stretching it outwards forcefully.
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	It will return to its place immediately.
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	And this type of dislocation is lighter than the others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	And if you cannot secure it in this way as we have said, then you must bind the two feet of the patient together with a strong soft bond above the heels and below the knees, keeping the injured leg extended twice more than the other.
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	Then be hung above from a post, and be raised above the ground two arms in length;
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	Then command one attendant to embrace the head of the thigh, and let another attendant be suspended with the patient, who firmly embraces the thigh, for the joint returns now forcefully.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when the dislocation is outward, let the patient lie as we have said for one with curvature, and bind the soft bond above the injured leg properly, and also above the foot;
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	Then place two red-hot irons, one on the head and another at the feet, then insert a red-hot iron between the thighs of the patient in this position.
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	Cover it with wet bandages so as not to scorch the patient, then stretch each assistant toward him, and have the assistants mirror the position of his hand at its dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it returns, it's good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If not, place [the patient] on a board, i.e. a plank, and press them as we have described for 'gilbosse', and let the patient lie on their sound side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when the dislocation is forward, it is necessary to extend the afflicted leg until it reaches its full length, according to what I have said.
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	And have the assistants place their weight on the afflicted limb, then push with one hand and stretch downwards towards the knee with the other. 
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And if the dislocation is outward, one should not stretch the patient downwards nor lift them off of the ground. Instead, they must be positioned as if their hip were dislocated outwards, just as we have described placing a person with two dislocated hips on their back. 
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	And place it on his face, with the bandage extended as we have said before, and one must apply pressure to the joint against the board.
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	And it will be effective when the patient extends their legs, and they are even in length.
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	Then adjust the thighs, apply the plaster, and use a bandage to hold it tight so that the hip does not move.
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	And let him rest for three or four days, then untie the bandage, and apply more plaster on top.
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	And if you see that they are even in length, bind it as before, and leave him like this for another three days.
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	Then untie it, and have him walk gently until the limb is strengthened.
de la dislocation dou genoil	Of the dislocation of the knee
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The knees are dislocated according to three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	That is to say, inwardly and outwardly, and behind;
et ne desalue point devant.	It does not dislocate forward.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the sign of this is that you instruct the patient to bend their leg towards their thigh, and if it does not reach their thigh, know that they are dislocated.
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	And the restoration of all these is that you make the patient sit upright, and stretch their leg if they can, and place your back on their face, and put their foot upon your feet.
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	Then take their kneecap in your palms, and pull it between your fingers, then bend the two sides of the knee sharply.
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	and another minister extends his foot, so that the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that he flexes his leg lightly at his thigh;
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	put the plaster on top, and make him stretch his leg towards his thigh, and bind them together tightly for three or four days, then untie it;
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	and the patient should not exert himself to walk until the limb is strengthened.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not aligned, apply strong traction, as we have mentioned in the treatment of hip injuries, until it is healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	Of the dislocation of the heel...
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels may be partially or fully dislocated, internally or externally...
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And the sign of this is that the ankle is swollen, and more so on the side where it is dislocated:
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	the reset is gentle, and it should be gently extended with the hands when he is only slightly moved.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it is dislocated completely, you must make the patient sit upright, and have one assistant hold them by the leg above the ankle;
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	Then draw the foot towards you with your right hand, then to the left twice, then stretch it upwards, and push the foot gently upward;
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	Do this twice, as we have said, pushing and drawing the foot each time;
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	If it stays in place, that is good;
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	But if not, start the process again, for it will return;
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	And if it cannot be done that way, then have the patient lay on their back on the ground, and firmly fix a forked stick into the earth between their thighs, then wrap the cloth around them to avoid injury;
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	Then have the ministers hold the thigh, and another minister extend the foot with their hands or use rope to tie it above the ankle;
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	Then each minister should extend equally, and the stick is placed between the patient's thighs to hold them in place as they are extended.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	Next, have the lead surgeon grasp the dislocation evenly with their hands, and another minister hold the healthy leg underneath; the dislocation will then return under pressure.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it is in place, apply the plaster and swabs on top, bind it tightly, and tie the foot to the leg; ensure the ligaments above the ankle are not too tight.
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	Leave it for two or three days, and if the bond softens, then strain it.
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	Then untie it on the third or fourth day, and prevent the patient from moving for four days.
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And if they move before this period is over, it is not certain that it will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If an abscess forms here, you must treat it as we have said elsewhere until it is healed.
des dois	Twice.
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the thumb is dislocated, it should be gently stretched without work, and this is a minor thing.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	If the dislocation is in any of the back or foot joints, you should make the patient sit on a flat surface or a straight chair, and place your foot on what appears to be the affected jointure, then press hard with your foot until it returns.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	And when it is even, and nothing appears to be wrong, place underneath the sole of the foot a board with two edges, then strain it hard, and leave it for three days, then untie it.
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let him rest until he is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	Of wounds and dislocations together.
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When a wound occurs along with dislocation, and one wishes to restore it, often the patient dies.
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	Be not presumptuous in the treatment if you are not wise in this art and have not practiced it for a long time, and if you lack compassion, mercy, and patience.
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	Employ at the outset soothing remedies for abscesses first, and leave the patient in God's hands if you see no hope of recovery.
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	And when you see some hope for the patient's recovery, then reset this limb now even if hot abscesses form there.
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	When the limb is replaced, administer soothing things for hot abscess, and treat the wound as required with drying ointments.
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	And if the dislocation involves a fracture with small broken bones, remove them, and do as we have said for simple injuries.
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	Beware of entering a state of fear as I have mentioned, for this is worthy according to your Creator and for the well-being of your arm and body.
